### 9.14 Energy Availability тАФ Complete End-to-End Reference

> **Scope:** This section documents every part of the EA and carb-floor override feature as it relates to the **Daily Intake Estimates** card on the dashboard. All EA logic is **Fight Camp only** тАФ it does not exist for standard fat-loss, maintenance, or weight-gain goals. Non-fight-camp users never see the EA row, EA modal, or carb modal.

#### 9.14.0 Server vs Client responsibility map

| Responsibility | Location | What it does |
|---|---|---|
| EA formula | ЁЯЦея╕П **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Computes `ffmKg`, `eaValue`, `isLowEA`, `eaRecommendedCalories` |
| Carb floor formula | ЁЯЦея╕П **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Computes `carbsPerKg`, `isLowCarb`, `carbRecommendedG` |
| Soft carb performance warning | ЁЯЦея╕П **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Sets `isBelowPerformanceCarb` + `performanceCarbWarning` string |
| Override decision storage | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `useFightCampOverride` hook | Reads/writes `localStorage`, exposes `overrideCalories` / `overrideCarbs` |
| Auto-opening modals | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `useFightCampOverride` hook | Reacts to `isLowEA` / `isLowCarb` flags from server |
| Final target merging | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `computeAdjustedTargets()` in `dashboard.tsx` | Applies `overrideCalories` / `overrideCarbs` on top of server values |
| EA row display | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Renders inline EA row inside Daily Intake Estimates card |
| EA modal UI | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Full-screen Dialog, sourced from `fcOverride.eaModalOpen` |
| Carb modal UI | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Full-screen Dialog, sourced from `fcOverride.carbModalOpen` |
| Performance toast | ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` `useEffect` | Fires once per date when `isBelowPerformanceCarb` + `shouldShowPerfToast` |

---

#### 9.14.1 ЁЯЦея╕П SERVER тАФ EA and carb-floor calculation

**Route:** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` тАФ fight camp branch only

**Step 1 тАФ Fat-free mass**
```
bodyFatPct = user.bodyFatPct ?? 0.15   тЖР defaults 15% if not set
ffmKg      = currentWeight ├Ч (1 тИТ bodyFatPct)
```

**Step 2 тАФ Energy Availability value**
```
eaValue = (plannedCalories тИТ exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
         тЖС plannedCalories = tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAddedBack тИТ plannedDeficitKcal
         тЖС exerciseKcalAdjusted = sum of all session estimatedKcal (0 on rest day)
```
`eaValue` is the number of kcal available per kg of fat-free mass after exercise is accounted for.

**Step 3 тАФ Hard EA flag**
```
isLowEA = eaValue < 30          тЖР IOC RED-S threshold
eaRecommendedCalories = Math.round(exerciseKcalAdjusted + 30 ├Ч ffmKg)
                        тЖР minimum calories that exactly hits EA = 30
```

**Step 4 тАФ Hard carb floor flag**
```
carbsPerKg  = targetCarbs / currentWeight
isLowCarb   = exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0 && !isRestDay && carbsPerKg < 3
              тЖР only fires on actual training days with calories burned
carbRecommendedG = Math.round(3 ├Ч currentWeight)   тЖР IOC/ISSN minimum
```

**Step 5 тАФ Soft performance warning** (only if `!isLowCarb`)
```
if dayType === "hard"      && carbsPerKg < 4 тЖТ isBelowPerformanceCarb = true
if dayType === "very_hard" && carbsPerKg < 5 тЖТ isBelowPerformanceCarb = true
// moderate / light: hard floor at 3 g/kg already covers them; no separate soft threshold
```
`performanceCarbWarning` string is set with the appropriate message per day type.

**Step 6 тАФ Response fields** (subset relevant to EA/carb feature)
```json
{
  "ffmKg":                 72.3,
  "eaValue":               28.4,
  "isLowEA":               true,
  "isLowCarb":             false,
  "carbsPerKg":            2.6,
  "eaRecommendedCalories": 2344,
  "carbRecommendedG":      219,
  "isBelowPerformanceCarb": false,
  "performanceCarbWarning": null,
  "planId":                7,
  "planFightDate":         "2026-09-15",
  "planTargetWeight":      70.0
}
```
The last three fields (`planId`, `planFightDate`, `planTargetWeight`) are included so the client can build the `planFingerprint` that detects plan changes and re-triggers consent modals.

---

#### 9.14.2 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ `useFightCampOverride` hook тАФ decision layer

**File:** `client/src/hooks/useFightCampOverride.ts`

This hook is the sole manager of override state. It never calls any API.

##### localStorage key

```
fightCamp:{userId}:{date}:{planId}:{fightDate}:{targetWeight}
```
If the user modifies the fight camp plan (different date, different target weight, new plan), the fingerprint changes тЖТ new key тЖТ stored decisions are not found тЖТ modals auto-trigger again for the new plan.

##### Stored value shape
```typescript
{
  ea?: "accepted" | "declined",
  carb?: "accepted" | "declined",
  perfToastShown?: boolean
}
```

##### Decision restoration on load

When `storageKey`, `date`, or `effectiveTargets` changes (including initial page load):
```typescript
// If ea === "accepted" and server still reports eaRecommendedCalories:
setOverrideCalories(effectiveTargets.eaRecommendedCalories);

// If ea === "declined" (or no decision):
setOverrideCalories(null);   // server value used as-is

// Same pattern for carb:
setOverrideCarbs(carbRecommendedG)   // if accepted
setOverrideCarbs(null)               // if declined / no decision
```

##### Auto-open sequence

Triggered by a `useEffect` watching `isFightCamp`, `isLowEA`, `isLowCarb`, `storageKey`:

```
1. If isLowEA && !stored.ea  тЖТ open EA modal immediately
2. Else if isLowCarb && !stored.carb тЖТ open carb modal immediately
```
Only one modal is ever open at a time. The carb modal chains via a 350 ms `setTimeout` after either `acceptEA()` or `declineEA()`.

##### Action outcomes

| User action | Function | `overrideCalories` | `overrideCarbs` | Stored | Carb chain? |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Accept EA | `acceptEA()` | `= eaRecommendedCalories` | unchanged | `ea: "accepted"` | Yes, if `isLowCarb && !stored.carb` |
| Decline EA | `declineEA()` | unchanged (`null`) | unchanged | `ea: "declined"` | Yes, if `isLowCarb && !stored.carb` |
| Backdrop / Esc (EA) | `closeEAModal()` | unchanged | unchanged | **nothing written** | No |
| Accept Carb | `acceptCarb()` | bumped up if needed┬╣ | `= carbRecommendedG` | `carb: "accepted"` | тАФ |
| Decline Carb | `declineCarb()` | unchanged | unchanged (`null`) | `carb: "declined"` | тАФ |
| Backdrop / Esc (Carb) | `closeCarbModal()` | unchanged | unchanged | **nothing written** | тАФ |

┬╣ `acceptCarb()` bump logic: `carbBasedCals = protein├Ч4 + fat├Ч9 + carbs├Ч4`. If `carbBasedCals > (overrideCalories ?? serverCalories)` тЖТ `setOverrideCalories(carbBasedCals)`. This prevents an impossible macro split where carbs alone exceed the calorie target.

**Key rule:** Backdrop/Escape never records a decision. The modal re-appears every time the page loads until the user explicitly taps Accept or Keep Plan.

---

#### 9.14.3 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ `computeAdjustedTargets()` тАФ merging overrides

In `dashboard.tsx`, `computeAdjustedTargets()` is called each render (no memo) and produces `adjustedTargets`, which drives every number displayed in the Daily Intake Estimates card.

```typescript
// Fight camp branch only:
const finalCals = fcOverride.overrideCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCalories;

let finalCarbs:
  if (fcOverride.overrideCarbs != null)         тЖТ fcOverride.overrideCarbs
  else if (fcOverride.overrideCalories != null) тЖТ Math.round(
                                                    Math.max(0,
                                                      overrideCalories
                                                      тИТ serverProtein├Ч4
                                                      тИТ serverFat├Ч9
                                                    ) / 4
                                                  )   // extra cals go to carbs
  else                                          тЖТ effectiveTargets.targetCarbs

// Re-computed effective EA from final values (for display):
effectiveEA = (finalCals тИТ exerciseKcal) / ffmKg

// Re-computed flags (after any override):
isLowEA  = effectiveEA < 30
isLowCarb = (finalCarbs / bodyWeightKg) < 3 && exerciseKcal > 0

// Preserved server originals тАФ remain true even after override brings EA to 30:
originallyLowEA   = effectiveTargets.isLowEA   // drives "adjusted тЬУ" indicator
originallyLowCarb = effectiveTargets.isLowCarb
```

> тЪая╕П The client **re-computes** `isLowEA` and `isLowCarb` after applying overrides. This means: once the user accepts the EA fix and `overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories`, `isLowEA` becomes `false` (EA is now exactly 30), but `originallyLowEA` stays `true` so the "adjusted тЬУ" state can still be shown.

---

#### 9.14.4 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ EA row inside the Daily Intake Estimates card

This inline row appears **only in fight camp mode** and only when `adjustedTargets.eaValue != null`.

##### Normal / OK state (isLowEA = false)
```
div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-xs
               bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"
```

##### Warning state (isLowEA = true AND eaDecision тЙа "accepted")
```
div className="тАж bg-orange-500/10 border border-orange-500/30 text-orange-400"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openEAModal}
          className="text-[10px] underline underline-offset-2 opacity-80 hover:opacity-100"
          data-testid="button-ea-review">
    {eaDecision === "declined" ? "Review" : "Review тЖТ"}
  </button>
```
Label changes from "Review тЖТ" to plain "Review" after the user has explicitly declined (so they know it was already considered).

##### Accepted state (originallyLowEA = true AND eaDecision = "accepted")
```
div className="тАж bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"   тЖР now тЙе 30 after override
  "┬╖ adjusted тЬУ"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openEAModal}
          data-testid="button-ea-review-accepted">
    Review
  </button>
```

##### Low carb inline warning (isLowCarb = true AND carbDecision тЙа "accepted")
```
div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-xs
               bg-yellow-500/10 border border-yellow-500/30 text-yellow-400"
  data-testid="text-low-carb-warning"

  "Carbs below 3 g/kg"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openCarbModal}
          data-testid="button-carb-review">
    {carbDecision === "declined" ? "Review" : "Review тЖТ"}
  </button>
```

##### Low carb accepted state (originallyLowCarb = true AND carbDecision = "accepted")
```
div className="тАж bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-carb-adjusted"

  "Carbs adjusted to 3 g/kg"
  "┬╖ adjusted тЬУ"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openCarbModal}
          data-testid="button-carb-review-accepted">
    Review
  </button>
```

#### 9.14.7 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ Soft performance toast

This is a non-blocking advisory тАФ no modal, no user action required.

**Trigger conditions (all must be true):**
1. `effectiveTargets.mode === "fight_camp"`
2. `effectiveTargets.isBelowPerformanceCarb === true`
3. `effectiveTargets.performanceCarbWarning` is a non-empty string
4. `fcOverride.shouldShowPerfToast === true` (i.e. `perfToastShown` not yet in storage for this key)

**Timing:** 1500 ms `setTimeout` after the `useEffect` fires (delayed to avoid clashing with page load).

```typescript
toast({
  title: "Performance note",
  description: effectiveTargets.performanceCarbWarning,
});
fcOverride.markPerfToastShown();
// writes { perfToastShown: true } to localStorage тАФ toast never repeats for this plan/date
```

**Server-side warning strings by day type:**

| Day type | Carbs threshold | `performanceCarbWarning` |
|---|---|---|
| `hard` | < 4 g/kg | "Carbohydrate intake may be low for this training load. Increasing toward ~5 g/kg may support performance." |
| `very_hard` | < 5 g/kg | "Carbohydrate intake may be low for a very high training load. Increasing toward ~5тАУ7 g/kg may support performance." |
| `moderate` / `light` | covered by hard carb modal | *(not set тАФ hard modal fires at < 3 g/kg)* |

---

#### 9.14.8 Complete decision flow diagram

```
Page loads / date changes
       тФВ
       тЦ╝
GET /api/me/targets/effective  тЖР ЁЯЦея╕П SERVER
  computes: eaValue, isLowEA, isLowCarb,
            eaRecommendedCalories, carbRecommendedG,
            isBelowPerformanceCarb, performanceCarbWarning
       тФВ
       тЦ╝
useFightCampOverride() reads localStorage     тЖР ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT
  тФЬтФА ea === "accepted"   тЖТ restore overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories
  тФЬтФА ea === "declined"   тЖТ overrideCalories = null (server value used)
  тФФтФА ea === undefined    тЖТ check isLowEAтАж
       тФВ
       тФЬтФА isLowEA && !stored.ea
       тФВ    тФФтФА OPEN EA MODAL
       тФВ         тФЬтФА [Adjust] acceptEA()
       тФВ         тФВ    overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФР
       тФВ         тФВ    stored: { ea: "accepted" }                         тФВ
       тФВ         тФВ    тЖТ chain carb modal if needed (350 ms)              тФВ
       тФВ         тФЬтФА [Keep plan] declineEA()                              тФВ
       тФВ         тФВ    overrideCalories = null                             тФВ
       тФВ         тФВ    stored: { ea: "declined" }                         тФВ
       тФВ         тФВ    тЖТ chain carb modal if needed (350 ms)              тФВ
       тФВ         тФФтФА [Backdrop/Esc] closeEAModal()                        тФВ
       тФВ              nothing stored тАФ modal re-appears next load         тФВ
       тФВ                                                                  тФВ
       тФФтФА isLowCarb && !stored.carb                                      тФВ
            тФФтФА OPEN CARB MODAL (or chained from EA modal)               тФВ
                 тФЬтФА [Adjust] acceptCarb()                                тФВ
                 тФВ    overrideCarbs = carbRecommendedG                   тФВ
                 тФВ    if carbCals > currentCals: overrideCalories тЖС тЖРтФАтФАтФАтФШ
                 тФВ    stored: { carb: "accepted" }
                 тФЬтФА [Keep plan] declineCarb()
                 тФВ    overrideCarbs = null
                 тФВ    stored: { carb: "declined" }
                 тФФтФА [Backdrop/Esc] closeCarbModal()
                      nothing stored тАФ modal re-appears next load

computeAdjustedTargets()   тЖР ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT
  finalCals  = overrideCalories ?? serverCalories
  finalCarbs = overrideCarbs ?? (overrideCalories тЖТ recalculate) ?? serverCarbs
  effectiveEA re-computed from finalCals

Daily Intake Estimates card renders:   тЖР ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT
  тФМтФА EA row: normal / warning / accepted
  тФЬтФА Carb row: warning / accepted (if applicable)
  тФФтФА Macro grid: finalCals / serverProtein / finalCarbs / serverFat

Performance toast (separate path):   тЖР ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT
  isBelowPerformanceCarb && shouldShowPerfToast
    тЖТ toast after 1500 ms тЖТ perfToastShown persisted
```

---

#### 9.14.9 All data-testids for the EA feature

| Element | data-testid |
|---|---|
| EA row in card (all states) | `text-ea-value` |
| "Review тЖТ" button (low EA, not yet accepted) | `button-ea-review` |
| "Review" button (EA already accepted) | `button-ea-review-accepted` |
| Low carb inline warning row | `text-low-carb-warning` |
| "Review тЖТ" button (low carb, not yet accepted) | `button-carb-review` |
| Low carb accepted row | `text-carb-adjusted` |
| "Review" button (carb already accepted) | `button-carb-review-accepted` |
| EA modal | `dialog-ea-warning` |
| EA modal "Adjust target" button | `button-ea-accept` |
| EA modal "Keep current plan" button | `button-ea-decline` |
| Carb modal | `dialog-carb-warning` |
| Carb modal "Adjust carbs" button | `button-carb-accept` |
| Carb modal "Keep current plan" button | `button-carb-decline` |

---

#### 9.14.10 Edge cases and important rules

| Rule | Detail |
|---|---|
| EA floor is advisory, not enforced | Server does NOT clamp `targetCalories` to `eaRecommendedCalories`. It passes both values and lets the user decide. |
| Carb floor is advisory only | `isLowCarb` is a flag тАФ the server does not bump `targetCarbs` to 3 g/kg automatically. |
| Rest days exempt from both floors | `isLowEA` can still fire (no training = lower denominator), but `isLowCarb` will not (`exerciseKcalAdjusted === 0` required for carb floor). |
| EA modal takes priority | Auto-open checks EA first, carb second. Carb modal is always chained after EA is resolved (350 ms delay), never opened simultaneously. |
| Plan change clears all decisions | If `planId`, `planFightDate`, or `planTargetWeight` change, the storage key changes and no prior decisions are found тЖТ all modals re-trigger. |
| Backdrop never persists | Dismissing either modal via backdrop or Escape writes nothing to storage. Only explicit button clicks (`acceptEA`, `declineEA`, `acceptCarb`, `declineCarb`) are persisted. |
| `originallyLow*` is from server | After accepting the EA override, the client's re-computed `isLowEA` becomes `false`. The `originallyLowEA` field keeps the server's original `true` so the "adjusted тЬУ" badge can still appear. |
| Body fat default | If `user.bodyFatPct` is null, the server assumes 15% BF for FFM calculation. Users can update body fat % in their profile to improve accuracy. |

---

### 9.15 Training тЖТ Target Reconciliation

> **Why this section exists:** Adding, editing, or deleting a training session changes how many calories the user burned. Both the calorie target shown in the Daily Intake Estimates card **and** the EA/carb floor checks must update immediately to reflect that change. This section documents the full end-to-end chain тАФ from the training mutation to the updated card numbers and (if needed) the re-opened consent modals.

---

#### 9.15.0 The two add-back models

There are two completely different paths depending on whether Fight Camp mode is active. Mobile replicators must implement both separately.

| | Fight Camp mode | Standard goals (fat loss / maintenance / weight gain) |
|---|---|---|
| **Who adds training calories** | ЁЯЦея╕П **Server** bakes them into `targetCalories` | ЁЯТ╗ **Client** adds `trainingSummary.totalKcal ├Ч creditPct` on top of server base |
| **Client rule** | Use `effectiveTargets.targetCalories` as-is. Do NOT add training again. | Compute `adjustedCalories = baseCalories + round(totalKcal ├Ч creditPct)` |
| **Credit percentages** | `trainingCalorieCreditPct: 0` (always returned by server as `0` as a guard) | fat_loss: 50%, maintenance: 75%, weight_gain: 100% |
| **EA / carb checks** | Server computes `isLowEA`, `isLowCarb` and client shows modals | No EA / carb checks тАФ these fields are `false` / `undefined` for non-fight-camp |
| **Macro adjustment** | Protein + fat fixed; carbs absorb remaining calories (server computes) | Protein + fat from profile; extra carbs absorb training credit (client computes) |

---

#### 9.15.1 ЁЯЦея╕П SERVER тАФ how training is read at request time

`GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD` is **not a cached snapshot** тАФ it queries the database live every time it is called.

In the fight camp branch:
```
todaySessions  = storage.getWorkoutSessions(userId, date, date)
todayActivities = flatten(storage.getSessionActivities(session.id) for each session)

exerciseKcalRaw      = sum(session.estimatedKcal for all todaySessions)
                       = 0 when isRestDay
exerciseKcalAdjusted = exerciseKcalRaw          // RPE already baked into estimatedKcal at write time
exerciseKcalAddedBack = round(exerciseKcalAdjusted ├Ч 0.8)   // 80% policy

plannedCalories = round(tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAddedBack тИТ plannedDeficitKcal)
targetCalories  = plannedCalories    // EA floor check is advisory only тАФ no clamping

eaValue  = (plannedCalories тИТ exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
isLowEA  = eaValue < 30
isLowCarb = exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0 && !isRestDay && carbsPerKg < 3
```

**Consequence:** If the user goes from 0 sessions to 1 session, `exerciseKcalAdjusted` jumps from 0 to the session's `estimatedKcal`. The next call to `GET /api/me/targets/effective` will return a higher `targetCalories` and potentially new `isLowEA` / `isLowCarb` flags.

---

#### 9.15.2 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ `estimatedKcal` is baked in at write time

The server bakes RPE into `estimatedKcal` when a session or activity is **created or updated** тАФ not when targets are fetched. The effective-targets route simply sums the stored `estimatedKcal` values.

```
POST /api/workouts/sessions          тЖТ creates session, estimatedKcal starts at 0
POST /api/workouts/sessions/:id/exercises тЖТ creates exercise, triggers recalculateSessionCalories()
PATCH /api/workouts/exercises/:id    тЖТ if rpe/duration changes тЖТ re-runs RPE ├Ч rawKcal
PATCH /api/workouts/sessions/:id     тЖТ if rpe/duration changes on session level тЖТ recalculates

POST /api/me/training/manual-burn    тЖТ creates a session with estimatedKcal = caloriesBurned directly
```

`recalculateSessionCalories()` (server-side helper):
- Sums `estimatedKcal` across all exercises in the session
- Applies RPE factor: `rpeFactor = 0.85 + (sessionRpe тИТ 1) ├Ч 0.05` (RPE 1тЖТ0.85, RPE 10тЖТ1.30)
- Writes result back to `session.estimatedKcal`
- The target-fetch route reads this stored value тАФ no runtime RPE calculation

---

#### 9.15.3 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ cache invalidation chain

Every mutation that changes today's training **removes** the cached effective-targets response so the next access triggers a fresh fetch.

| Mutation | Queries removed / invalidated |
|---|---|
| Create session (`POST /api/workouts/sessions`) | `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` |
| Delete session (`DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id`) | same triple |
| Add exercise to session | `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training-load"]` |
| Update exercise (rpe/sets/duration) | same as add exercise |
| Delete exercise | same as add exercise |
| Add/edit/delete activity (cardio) | same as add exercise |
| Mark rest day | `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| Manual burn (`POST /api/me/training/manual-burn`) | `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| AI log тАФ training intent | `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| Morning check-in тАФ session created | `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |

**`removeQueries` vs `invalidateQueries`:** `removeQueries` drops the cached data entirely so the next subscriber immediately triggers a network fetch (no stale data shown). `invalidateQueries` marks as stale and re-fetches in the background. Both result in the same eventual state. Training mutations use `removeQueries` on `targets/effective` to guarantee the old number is never shown after training changes.

---

#### 9.15.4 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ the automatic re-fetch chain

```
Training mutation fires
  тФВ
  тФФтФА onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"], exact: false)
                removeQueries(["/api/me/training/summary"],  exact: false)
       тФВ
       тЦ╝
TanStack Query sees the cache is empty for the active queryKey
       тФВ
       тЦ╝
Re-fetches GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD   тЖР ЁЯЦея╕П SERVER
  тЖ│ reads updated todaySessions from DB
  тЖ│ returns new targetCalories, eaValue, isLowEA, isLowCarb, etc.
       тФВ
       тЦ╝
React re-renders:
  effectiveTargets updates тЖТ computeAdjustedTargets() re-runs
       тФВ
       тФЬтФА Daily Intake Estimates card shows new numbers
       тФВ
       тФФтФА useFightCampOverride useEffect fires (watches isLowEA, isLowCarb, storageKey)
              тФВ
              тФЬтФА if isLowEA && !stored.ea  тЖТ open EA modal
              тФФтФА else if isLowCarb && !stored.carb тЖТ open carb modal
```

**Key point:** The modal auto-open logic in `useFightCampOverride` runs every time `isLowEA` or `isLowCarb` changes. So if a training session is added that pushes EA below 30, the EA modal **automatically opens** without any extra code тАФ the re-fetch is the only trigger needed.

---

#### 9.15.5 ЁЯТ╗ CLIENT тАФ standard goal add-back (non-fight-camp)

For fat loss / maintenance / weight gain, the server returns a flat base target. The client applies the credit:

```typescript
// GET /api/me/training/summary/:date тЖТ { totalKcal, totalKcalAdjusted }
// totalKcalAdjusted mirrors totalKcal (RPE baked in at write time)
const trainingKcal = trainingSummary?.totalKcalAdjusted ?? trainingSummary?.totalKcal ?? 0;

const creditPct: Record<string, number> = {
  fat_loss:    0.5,   // 50%
  maintenance: 0.75,  // 75%
  weight_gain: 1.0,   // 100%
};

// From server (base, before training):
const baseCalories = effectiveTargets?.targetCalories ?? user.targetCalories;
const baseCarbs    = effectiveTargets?.targetCarbs    ?? user.targetCarbs;

// Client adds back:
let adjustedCalories = baseCalories + Math.round(trainingKcal * creditPct[goal]);

// Fat-loss cap: deficit тЙд 1% BW/week
if (goal === "fat_loss") {
  const maxDailyDeficit = Math.round((0.01 * bodyWeightKg * 7700) / 7);
  const tdee = effectiveTargets?.tdee ?? baseCalories + 500;
  if (tdee - adjustedCalories > maxDailyDeficit) {
    adjustedCalories = tdee - maxDailyDeficit;
  }
}

// Protein + fat stay fixed; extra calories go to carbs:
const adjustedCarbs = baseCarbs + Math.round(Math.max(0, adjustedCalories - baseCalories) / 4);
```

The standard path **never checks EA or carb floors** тАФ `isLowEA` and `isLowCarb` are always `false`, and no EA/carb modals ever appear.

---

#### 9.15.6 ЁЯЦея╕П SERVER тАФ training summary endpoint

Used by the client (both fight camp and standard) to display session cards and provide `totalKcal` for the non-fight-camp add-back.

```
GET /api/me/training/summary/:date
```

Response:
```json
{
  "date": "2026-06-22",
  "totalKcal": 480,
  "totalKcalAdjusted": 480,
  "isRestDay": false,
  "sessions": [
    { "id": 12, "timeOfDay": "morning", "estimatedKcal": 480,
      "exerciseCount": 4, "activityCount": 1 }
  ]
}
```

`totalKcalAdjusted` mirrors `totalKcal` тАФ RPE is already baked into each session's `estimatedKcal` at storage time, so no further adjustment is needed here.

---

#### 9.15.7 End-to-end example: user adds a 500 kcal session in fight camp

```
Initial state (no training logged today):
  effectiveTargets.targetCalories = 1800   (NEAT + 0 exercise тИТ deficit)
  effectiveTargets.eaValue = 24.6          (LOW тАФ only resting NEAT available)
  effectiveTargets.isLowEA = true
  тЖТ EA modal opens on page load

User dismisses modal (backdrop tap) тАФ no decision stored

User navigates to Training page тЖТ creates a morning session
  POST /api/workouts/sessions { date, timeOfDay: "morning" }
  onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"])

TanStack Query re-fetches GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=2026-06-22
  Server reads session: estimatedKcal = 0 (no exercises yet)
  exerciseKcalAdjusted = 0 тЖТ targetCalories still 1800, isLowEA still true

User adds a 60-min run activity (MET 9.5, 75 kg тЖТ ~285 kcal) with RPE 7
  POST /api/workouts/sessions/:id/activities  { durationMinutes:60, metValue:9.5, rpe:7 }
  Server: rawKcal = 9.5├Ч3.5├Ч75/200├Ч60 = 748 тЖТ wait, estimatedKcal = 285 (MET formula)
          rpeFactor = 0.85 + (7тИТ1)├Ч0.05 = 1.15
          estimatedKcal = round(285 ├Ч 1.15) = 328
  recalculateSessionCalories() writes session.estimatedKcal = 328
  onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"])

TanStack Query re-fetches targets:
  exerciseKcalAdjusted = 328
  exerciseKcalAddedBack = round(328 ├Ч 0.8) = 262
  plannedCalories = 1800_base + 262 = 2062  (using tdeeNoExercise, not the old 1800)
  ffmKg = 63.75 (75 kg ├Ч 0.85)
  eaValue = (2062 тИТ 328) / 63.75 = 27.2    (still < 30)
  isLowEA = true тЖТ EA modal re-opens (no stored decision yet)
  isLowCarb = 328 > 0 && carbsPerKg < 3 тЖТ possibly true

User accepts EA modal:
  overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories = round(328 + 30 ├Ч 63.75) = 2241
  stored: { ea: "accepted" }
  тЖТ carb modal chains if isLowCarb

Card now shows:
  Calories: 2241
  EA row: "27.2 тЖТ 30.0 kcal/kg FFM ┬╖ adjusted тЬУ"
```

---

#### 9.15.8 What a mobile app must implement

If you are building a mobile app and currently not reconciling training with targets, here is the minimum required implementation:

**Step 1 тАФ After any training mutation, re-fetch effective targets**
```
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id/exercises
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id/activities
POST /api/me/training/manual-burn
POST/DELETE /api/me/rest-day/:date
  тЖТ onSuccess: invalidate / re-fetch GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD
                                      GET /api/me/training/summary/:date
```

**Step 2 тАФ Use the right calorie source**

| Mode | Calorie target to display |
|---|---|
| Fight camp (`effectiveTargets.mode === "fight_camp"`) | `effectiveTargets.targetCalories` directly (already includes training) |
| Standard goals | `effectiveTargets.targetCalories + round(trainingSummary.totalKcal ├Ч creditPct)` |

**Step 3 тАФ Check EA / carb flags after each re-fetch (fight camp only)**

After re-fetching `effectiveTargets`:
```
if mode === "fight_camp":
  if isLowEA && no stored ea decision for this date/plan:
    тЖТ show EA consent modal

  elif isLowCarb && no stored carb decision for this date/plan:
    тЖТ show carb consent modal

  if isBelowPerformanceCarb && soft toast not yet shown:
    тЖТ show advisory toast after 1500 ms
```

**Step 4 тАФ Apply user overrides on top of server values**
```
displayCalories = overrideCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCalories
displayCarbs    = overrideCarbs    ?? recalculatedFromDisplayCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCarbs
```

**What NOT to do:**
- тЭМ Don't add `trainingSummary.totalKcal` to `targetCalories` in fight camp тАФ it's already included
- тЭМ Don't cache `targetCalories` at app startup and use it for the day тАФ it changes as training is logged
- тЭМ Don't skip the re-fetch after deleting a session тАФ removing training lowers the target and may change EA flags
- тЭМ Don't re-trigger EA modals if the user already accepted/declined for this plan+date (check localStorage / your local decision store first)

---

### 9.16 isLowEA / isLowCarb тАФ Warning Flag Reference

This section documents the exact conditions under which the two nutritional-warning flags are set, the server/client split of responsibility, and the design decisions behind each rule. Both flags appear in the `GET /api/me/targets/effective` response and drive the warning rows inside the **Daily Intake Estimates** card.

---

#### 9.16.0 Where each flag lives

| Flag | Server field | Client field | Who computes final value |
|---|---|---|---|
| `isLowEA` | `effectiveTargets.isLowEA` | Re-read from server response | **Server only** тАФ client always trusts it |
| `isLowCarb` | `effectiveTargets.isLowCarb` | `isLowCarbFinal` (see ┬з9.16.3) | Server for standard mode; client overrides **only** in Fight Camp when `overrideCarbs != null` |

---

#### 9.16.1 isLowEA тАФ Energy Availability warning

**Server code location:** `server/routes.ts` тЖТ `GET /api/me/targets/effective`

**Condition (all must be true):**

```
isLowEA = true   when:
  fightCampActive === true
  AND energyAvailability < 30          // kcal / kg FFM
```

Where:
```
energyAvailability = (calorieTarget - exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
```

`ffmKg` is derived from user body fat if available, otherwise estimated from a lean-population formula.

**Threshold: 30 kcal/kg FFM**  
This is the internationally recognised RED-S / LEA threshold for combat athletes. Below this, the user is at clinical risk of Relative Energy Deficiency in Sport.

**No `hasActualActivities` guard on isLowEA** тАФ even with zero exercise today, a fight-camp calorie target that is structurally low relative to FFM should still warn.

**UI trigger:** Low-EA row in Daily Intake Estimates card тЖТ "Review тЖТ" opens EA warning Dialog (┬з9.10).

---

#### 9.16.2 isLowCarb тАФ Low-carbohydrate warning (server side)

**Server code location:** `server/routes.ts` тЖТ `GET /api/me/targets/effective`

**Condition (all must be true):**

```typescript
const hasActualActivities = todayActivities.length > 0;

isLowCarb = true   when:
  hasActualActivities === true          // at least one logged activity today
  AND exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0          // that training burns real calories
  AND isRestDay === false               // user has not marked the day as rest
  AND carbsPerKg < 3                    // g carbs / kg bodyweight below performance threshold
```

`carbsPerKg = targetCarbs / weightKg`  
`targetCarbs` is the server-computed carbohydrate target for the day (fight-camp or standard).

**Why `hasActualActivities` exists:**  
Without this guard, a rest day or a day where the user has not logged any training yet would generate a false-positive low-carb warning purely because the baseline macro targets happen to set carbs below 3 g/kg. The warning is only meaningful when real training load has been confirmed.

**`isBelowPerformanceCarb`** (separate flag, same file) uses the same `hasActualActivities` guard and a lower threshold (< 2 g/kg) to drive the more urgent "performance carb" state.

**UI trigger:** Low-carb warning row in Daily Intake Estimates card тЖТ "Review тЖТ" opens Carb warning Dialog (┬з9.11).

---

#### 9.16.3 isLowCarb тАФ Client-side resolution (`computeAdjustedTargets`)

**Client code location:** `client/src/pages/dashboard.tsx` тЖТ `computeAdjustedTargets()`

The client must resolve a final `isLowCarbFinal` value for rendering. The rule is:

```typescript
// fcOverride = result of useFightCampOverride()
const isLowCarbFinal =
  fcOverride.overrideCarbs != null
    ? effectiveCarbsPerKg < 3          // FC active + carb override present тЖТ recompute locally
    : (effectiveTargets?.isLowCarb ?? false);  // all other cases тЖТ trust server
```

**When `overrideCarbs != null` (Fight Camp active, carb override applied):**  
The fight-camp hook may adjust carbs beyond what the server already computed. The client recomputes `effectiveCarbsPerKg` from the final adjusted carb target, then applies the same `< 3` threshold. This avoids a stale server value when the carb override shifts the target mid-session.

**All other cases:**  
The client reads `effectiveTargets.isLowCarb` directly from the server. The client does **not** re-evaluate the `hasActualActivities` guard тАФ it trusts the server's result unconditionally.

> тЪая╕П **Do not** replicate the full `isLowCarb` logic on the client for non-FC cases. The server has access to `todayActivities` (the actual logged sessions array) which is not separately available on the client. Re-computing it from macro targets alone would reproduce the false-positive bug that was fixed by the `hasActualActivities` guard.

---

#### 9.16.4 Complete conditions table

| Scenario | `hasActualActivities` | `isRestDay` | `exerciseKcalAdjusted` | `carbsPerKg` | `isLowCarb` (server) |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Rest day (marked) | any | **true** | any | any | **false** |
| No sessions logged yet | **false** | false | any | any | **false** |
| Session logged, carbs тЙе 3 g/kg | true | false | > 0 | тЙе 3 | **false** |
| Session logged, carbs < 3 g/kg | true | false | > 0 | < 3 | **true** |
| Session logged, 0 kcal burn | true | false | **0** | < 3 | **false** |

---

#### 9.16.5 Key design decisions

1. **Server is source of truth for `isLowEA` always.** Energy availability requires `ffmKg`, which involves body-fat estimation logic that lives only on the server.

2. **Server is source of truth for `isLowCarb` in standard mode.** `todayActivities` (the raw session list for the day) is fetched inside the `/targets/effective` handler and is not separately exposed on a client-readable endpoint that would be available at render time.

3. **Client overrides `isLowCarb` only in Fight Camp + carb-override active.** This is the single case where the fight-camp hook adjusts carbs beyond what the server target already shows, and the server's cached flag would be stale.

4. **`hasActualActivities` uses `todayActivities.length > 0`, not a calorie threshold.** A session can be logged with 0 kcal estimated burn (e.g. yoga, mobility). The double-guard (`hasActualActivities && exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0`) ensures both that a session exists AND that it actually contributes load.

5. **`isRestDay` gates both `isLowCarb` and `isBelowPerformanceCarb`.** Rest days are expected to have lower carb targets; warning on them would be noise.

6. **The 3 g/kg threshold is sport-science consensus** for minimum carbohydrate availability during moderate-to-high training volume for combat athletes. 2 g/kg (`isBelowPerformanceCarb`) is the acute-performance-impairment floor.

7. **No debounce on the warning.** If training is deleted, the next `/targets/effective` fetch will drop `isLowCarb` back to `false`. The cache invalidation chain in ┬з9.15.3 ensures this re-fetch happens automatically after session changes.

8. **Modal re-trigger prevention** (EA modal only, ┬з9.10) is managed client-side via `localStorage`. The key is `ea_modal_dismissed_{userId}_{planId}_{date}`. isLowCarb has no equivalent suppression тАФ the carb warning row is always shown when the flag is true.

---

### 9.17 Micronutrient Quality Card & Page (AMQS) тАФ Full Replication Guide

This section is a standalone build spec for the **Athlete Micronutrient Quality Score (AMQS)** system: the dashboard card, the dedicated `/micronutrients` page, and all server-side computation behind them. Read this section top to bottom before implementing тАФ it is written so a replicating agent does not need to re-derive the scoring model.

#### 9.17.0 File map

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `server/lib/micros.ts` | Raw micronutrient aggregation тАФ sums food entries + taken supplements into per-nutrient daily totals |
| `server/lib/amqs.ts` | The scoring engine тАФ nutrient definitions, two-layer targets, weighted scoring, tiers, gaps, trend |
| `client/src/components/AMQSCard.tsx` | The dashboard card AND the detail dialog (same component, used on both the dashboard and the dedicated page) |
| `client/src/pages/micronutrients.tsx` | The dedicated `/micronutrients` page тАФ date navigator + `AMQSCard` + full-width 7-day trend chart |
| `data/ingredients.json` | Ingredient database used both for computing intake (per-100g micronutrient values) and for generating "Try: X" food suggestions |

**Key architectural fact:** there is no separate "micronutrient page logic" тАФ `micronutrients.tsx` is a thin wrapper that adds date navigation around the exact same `AMQSCard` component embedded on the dashboard. Replicate the card once; the page just gives it a date picker and appends a full-size trend chart.

---

#### 9.17.1 Raw aggregation layer (`server/lib/micros.ts`)

This layer answers one question: **"How much of each micronutrient did this user consume today?"** It knows nothing about targets, scoring, or tiers тАФ that's the job of `amqs.ts`.

**17 tracked nutrient keys** (naming convention `{name}_{unit}`):
```
iron_mg, calcium_mg, vitamin_d_ug, magnesium_mg, zinc_mg,
iodine_ug, selenium_ug, folate_ug, vitamin_b12_ug,
vitamin_c_mg, vitamin_a_ug, potassium_mg,
vitamin_b1_mg, vitamin_b2_mg, vitamin_b3_mg, vitamin_b6_mg,
omega3_g
```

**Two independent sources are computed in parallel and merged:**

1. **`getFoodMicrosForDate(storage, userId, date)`** тАФ for each logged food entry:
   - Resolve an `Ingredient` record three ways, in priority order:
     a. **Composite/"core food" decomposition** тАФ a hardcoded `COMPOSITE_FOODS` map (e.g. `"porridge (oats + milk)"` тЖТ 40g Oats (Raw) + 200g Milk (Whole) per 250g reference serving) scales sub-ingredient grams by `entryGrams / referenceServingGrams`, then sums each component's contribution. This exists because combo meals ("beans on toast", "scrambled eggs") don't map to a single ingredient row.
     b. **Mapped Open Food Facts entry** тАФ if `entry.sourceType === "off"` and `entry.microSource === "ingredient"` and `entry.ingredientIndex` is a valid index, use `ingredients[ingredientIndex]` directly (a curated micronutrient-mapped OFF item).
     c. **Name match fallback** тАФ for non-OFF entries (manually logged whole foods), case-insensitive exact match against `ingredients.json` by name.
   - OFF entries that are neither composite nor validly index-mapped contribute **zero** micronutrients (there's no silent guess тАФ if there's no mapping, the food is skipped for AMQS purposes but still counts toward calories/macros elsewhere).
   - Contribution formula: `(valuePer100g * entryGrams) / 100`, summed across all matched entries.

2. **`getSupplementMicrosForDate(storage, userId, date)`** тАФ for each `supplement_intake` row where `taken = true`:
   - Look up the user's `supplements` row тЖТ its `catalogId` тЖТ the `supplement_catalog` row тЖТ its `microsPerUnit` JSONB field.
   - Contribution: `microsPerUnit[key] * doseAmount`, where `doseAmount` is the user's logged dose.
   - **Special-case unit conversion:** Vitamin D only. If the user's `doseUnit` doesn't match the catalog's `defaultUnit`: IUтЖТmcg multiplies by `0.025`; mcgтЖТIU multiplies by `40`.

3. **`mergeMicros(food, supplements)`** sums the two dictionaries key-by-key. `getDailyMicros()` is the single entry point that returns `{ totals, breakdown: { food, supplements } }` тАФ the `breakdown` split is what powers the "top contributor" line on the card (┬з9.17.3).

**To replicate:** you need (a) a per-100g micronutrient table on your ingredient/food data, (b) a `microsPerUnit`-style per-dose table on your supplement catalog, and (c) a composite-food decomposition map for any multi-ingredient "quick add" meals you support. Everything else is arithmetic.

---

#### 9.17.2 The two-layer scoring model (`server/lib/amqs.ts`)

This is the core design concept of AMQS and the most important thing to replicate faithfully.

**Layer 1 тАФ "General Score" / Baseline Adequacy.** Targets are ordinary population reference values (UK RNI / US DRI-style). This answers "is this person meeting basic nutritional adequacy as an average adult?"

**Layer 2 тАФ "Performance Score" / Athlete Optimisation.** Same nutrient set, but targets are raised where sports-nutrition literature supports a higher requirement for training athletes (e.g. Vitamin D 10┬╡g тЖТ 25┬╡g, Calcium 700mg тЖТ 1000mg, Magnesium 300/270mg тЖТ 400/350mg). Some nutrients (Selenium, Iron) are **not** raised in Layer 2 тАФ the source comment explicitly notes "L2 must not be easier," i.e. Layer 2 targets are never lower than Layer 1.

Both layers run through the **identical weighted-adequacy formula** тАФ only the target table differs:

```
for each nutrient i:
  adequacy_i = min(intake_i / target_i, 1.0)     // capped at 100% тАФ overconsuming one nutrient
                                                   // cannot compensate for a deficiency in another
score = round( 100 * ╬г(weight_i * adequacy_i) / ╬г(weight_i) )
```

**Full nutrient table** (17 nutrients, with weight and both target layers):

| Nutrient | Key | Weight | Layer 1 target (M / F) | Layer 2 target (M / F) |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Iron | `iron_mg` | 2.0 (2.5 if female тАФ see below) | 8.7 / 14.8 mg | same (individualized, not raised) |
| Calcium | `calcium_mg` | 2.0 | 700 mg | 1000 mg |
| Vitamin D | `vitamin_d_ug` | 2.0 | 10 ┬╡g | 25 ┬╡g |
| Magnesium | `magnesium_mg` | 1.5 | 300 / 270 mg | 400 / 350 mg |
| Zinc | `zinc_mg` | 1.5 | 9.5 / 7.0 mg | 12 / 9 mg |
| Iodine | `iodine_ug` | 1.0 | 140 ┬╡g | 150 ┬╡g |
| Selenium | `selenium_ug` | 1.0 | 75 / 60 ┬╡g | same (aligned тАФ no stronger athlete target) |
| Folate | `folate_ug` | 1.0 | 200 ┬╡g | 400 ┬╡g |
| Vitamin B12 | `vitamin_b12_ug` | 1.0 (2.0 if vegan тАФ see below) | 1.5 ┬╡g | 2.4 ┬╡g |
| Vitamin C | `vitamin_c_mg` | 1.0 | 40 mg | 120 / 100 mg |
| Vitamin A | `vitamin_a_ug` | 1.0 | 700 / 600 ┬╡g | 900 / 700 ┬╡g |
| Potassium | `potassium_mg` | 1.0 | 3500 mg | 4000 / 3500 mg |
| Vitamin B1 | `vitamin_b1_mg` | 0.75 | 1.2 / 1.1 mg | 1.4 mg |
| Vitamin B2 | `vitamin_b2_mg` | 0.75 | 1.3 / 1.1 mg | 1.5 mg |
| Vitamin B3 | `vitamin_b3_mg` | 0.75 | 16 / 14 mg | 18 mg |
| Vitamin B6 | `vitamin_b6_mg` | 0.75 | 1.3 mg | 1.6 mg |
| Omega-3 | `omega3_g` | 1.0 | 1.6 / 1.1 g | 2.0 g |

**Dynamic weight overrides** (applied identically in both layers, before summing):
- `iron_mg` weight becomes **2.5** (from 2.0) if `user.gender === "female"` тАФ reflects higher clinical iron-deficiency risk.
- `vitamin_b12_ug` weight becomes **2.0** (from 1.0) if diet is vegan тАФ B12 is the single highest-risk nutrient on a vegan diet. (Note: diet is currently hardcoded to `"omnivore"` in `getUserProfile()` тАФ this override exists in the formula but is not yet wired to a user-facing diet-type field.)

**Per-nutrient status labels** (used for coverage display, not scoring):
```
rawPct = (intake / target) * 100
status = rawPct < 50 ? "low" : rawPct > 150 ? "high" : "ok"
pctOfTarget (displayed) = round(min(rawPct, 100))   // capped for the progress bar, but "status" uses the uncapped rawPct
```

**Tier thresholds** (identical scale for both layers):
```
score >= 95 тЖТ Elite
score >= 85 тЖТ Optimal
score >= 70 тЖТ Good
score >= 50 тЖТ Fair
else        тЖТ Basic
```

**Critical-nutrient Elite floor.** Elite is special: even if the weighted score is тЙе95, the tier is capped at **Optimal** if any of these 5 "critical" nutrients sits below **70% of its Layer-1 (baseline) target**:
```
CRITICAL_NUTRIENT_KEYS = [iron_mg, calcium_mg, vitamin_d_ug, magnesium_mg, zinc_mg]
CRITICAL_FLOOR_PCT = 70
```
This check always evaluates against **Layer-1 coverage**, even for the Layer-2 tier calculation тАФ the rationale in the source is that a Layer-2 Elite tier would be meaningless if the person is still deficient by ordinary population standards. Replicate this cross-layer dependency exactly; it's the one place the two layers are not fully independent.

**`allMet` flag:** `true` when every Layer-1 nutrient is at тЙе100% of target (i.e., zero entries in the `underTarget` gap list). This drives the "Baseline adequacy covered" success state on the card (┬з9.17.3) and fires a one-time-per-day toast.

---

#### 9.17.3 "Top gaps" and the 3 food suggestions тАФ exact algorithm

The card always shows **at most 3 rows** in the "Top gaps" section, and in the reference screenshots (a well-logged day) it shows exactly 3: `Omega-3 20% тЖТ Try: Flax Seeds`, `Folate 39% тЖТ Try: Chickpeas (Dry)`, `Vitamin A 48% тЖТ Try: Sweet Potato (Baked)`. This is not a hardcoded list тАФ it is the live output of the algorithm below, recomputed from that day's actual intake. Replicate the **pipeline**, not the example values.

**Step 1 тАФ build the gap list (per layer independently):**
```
1. Filter to nutrients where pctOfTarget < 100 ("under target").
2. Sort ascending by pctOfTarget (worst / lowest-coverage deficiency first).
3. Take the first 3 entries тЖТ this becomes topGaps (Layer 1) / layer2TopGaps (Layer 2).
```
If fewer than 3 nutrients are under target, fewer than 3 rows render (e.g. only 1 gap row if the user is deficient in just one nutrient). If zero nutrients are under target, the gaps section is replaced entirely by the green "Baseline adequacy covered" banner (┬з9.17.7) тАФ the two states are mutually exclusive, never both rendered.

**Step 2 тАФ attach a "Try: X" suggestion to each of those 3 (and in fact to every nutrient key, since the suggestion engine runs unconditionally and cheaply for all 17 keys, not just the 3 that end up on screen):**
```typescript
candidates = ingredients
  .filter(ing => getMicronutrientValue(ing, `${nutrientKey}_per_100g`) > 0)
  .map(ing => {
    potency = value of that nutrient per 100g
    common  = ing.commonScore ?? 0.5     // "how staple/common is this food", 0тАУ1
    score   = potency * 0.6 + potency * common * 0.4
  })
  .sort by score descending

bestFood = candidates.find(c => c.common >= 0.5) || candidates[0]
suggestion = bestFood?.name  // e.g. "Flax Seeds", "Chickpeas (Dry)", "Sweet Potato (Baked)"
```
In plain terms: rank candidate foods primarily by how much of the nutrient they deliver per 100g, but weight in a "commonness" factor so the suggestion is a food people actually eat (e.g. suggesting "Cod (Baked)" over an obscure exotic fish with technically higher iodine). If no food scores `commonScore >= 0.5`, fall back to the single highest-potency candidate regardless of commonness. A gap row with no matching ingredient at all simply omits `suggestion` (the "Try: тАж" line is conditionally rendered тАФ see ┬з9.17.7).

**To reproduce the exact reference-screenshot suggestions**, your ingredient data needs entries such that: Omega-3 тЖТ the single highest `score` candidate is Flax Seeds (a very high-potency, moderately common source); Folate тЖТ Chickpeas (Dry); Vitamin A тЖТ Sweet Potato (Baked). Concretely this means those three ingredients need (a) a high per-100g value for the respective nutrient, and (b) `commonScore >= 0.5` so they clear the commonness filter ahead of higher-potency-but-obscure alternatives.

**`ingredients.json` needs a `commonScore` field (0тАУ1) per entry** for this to work тАФ this is not optional metadata, it's load-bearing for suggestion quality.

**Server response shape per gap (exactly what the client receives per row):**
```typescript
{ microKey: string, label: string, pctOfTarget: number, suggestion?: string }
```

---

#### 9.17.4 Confidence / Data Confidence indicator

Answers: "how much of today's logged data actually has micronutrient info attached, so how much should the user trust this score?" Computed once, shared by both layers.

```
totalItems = foodEntries.length + takenSupplements.length
itemsWithMicros = foodEntriesWithMicros + takenSupplementsWithMicros
overallCoverage = totalItems === 0 ? 0 : itemsWithMicros / totalItems

confidence = totalItems === 0        ? "Low"
           : overallCoverage >= 0.75 ? "High"
           : overallCoverage >= 0.40 ? "Medium"
           :                            "Low"
```

A food entry counts as "with micros" if: it's a known composite food, OR it resolves to an ingredient (by index or name match) that has a nonzero value for **at least one** of the 17 tracked nutrients. A supplement intake counts as "with micros" if its catalog entry has a non-empty `microsPerUnit` object.

**UI mapping** (`getConfidenceValue` in `AMQSCard.tsx`): High тЖТ progress bar value 100, Medium тЖТ 60, Low тЖТ 30. Displayed as a `<Progress>` bar plus a badge, with an info tooltip reading: *"Measures how much of your logged data has micronutrient info. High = 75%+ coverage, Medium = 40тАУ74%, Low = under 40% or no data."*

---

#### 9.17.5 7-day trend computation (`computeAMQSTrend`)

This single server function powers **three different UI surfaces**: the mini sparkline on the dashboard card, the two side-by-side sparklines in the detail dialog, and the full-width dual-line chart on the dedicated page.

```
1. Build 14 consecutive date strings ending at asOfDate (today, by default).
2. Run computeAMQSScore() for each of the 14 days (yes тАФ 14 full daily computations per trend request; there is no caching layer, see note below).
3. Split into prevWeek = days[0..6] (oldest), currentWeek = days[7..13] (most recent, includes asOfDate).
4. avg(list) = round(mean of scores), 0 if list empty.
5. delta = currentWeekAvg - prevWeekAvg.
6. trend classification:
     delta >= +3  тЖТ "improving"
     delta <= -3  тЖТ "slightly_down"
     otherwise    тЖТ "steady"
```

This is computed **twice** in the same response тАФ once for Layer 1 scores, once for Layer 2 scores тАФ returned as sibling `layer1` / `layer2` objects, each with `{ currentWeekAvg, prevWeekAvg, delta, trend, dailyScores }`. `dailyScores` only contains the **current** 7 days (for charting), not all 14.

**Client-side trend line formatting** (identical logic duplicated in both `AMQSCard.tsx` and `micronutrients.tsx` тАФ replicate as one shared helper, don't duplicate):
```typescript
function formatTrendLine(layer) {
  if (!layer) return "";
  if (layer.prevWeekAvg === 0) return "still building";      // no baseline yet
  if (layer.trend === "improving")    return `тЖС +${delta} vs last week`;
  if (layer.trend === "slightly_down") return `тЖУ ${delta} vs last week`;
  return "тЖТ steady vs last week";
}
function trendLineColor(layer) {
  if (!layer || layer.prevWeekAvg === 0) return muted/40;
  if (layer.trend === "improving")     return emerald (text-emerald-500);
  if (layer.trend === "slightly_down") return amber (text-amber-400);
  return muted;
}
```

**Performance note for replicators:** `computeAMQSTrend` performs 14 sequential `computeAMQSScore` calls, each of which itself does 2+ DB queries (food entries, supplement intakes, supplements, catalog) тАФ this is intentionally simple/uncached in the current implementation. If you have significant user volume, consider caching daily AMQS results once a day is "closed" (i.e., not today) rather than recomputing on every trend fetch.

---

#### 9.17.6 API endpoints

| Method | Path | Auth | Returns |
|---|---|---|---|
| `GET` | `/api/me/amqs/score/:date` | Session | Full `AMQSScoreResult` for one day тАФ both layers, coverage, gaps, confidence |
| `GET` | `/api/me/amqs/score-range/:startDate/:endDate` | Session | `{ startDate, endDate, averageScore, tier, dailyScores[] }` тАФ Layer 1 only, used for the "Weekly Avg" fallback state when Layer 2 isn't shown |
| `GET` | `/api/me/amqs/trend/:date` | Session | `AMQSTrendResult` тАФ both layers, 14-day computation, see ┬з9.17.5 |
| `GET` | `/api/me/amqs/micros/:date` | Session | Raw `DailyMicrosResult` (totals + food/supplement breakdown, no scoring) |

**Full `AMQSScoreResult` shape** (returned by `/score/:date`):
```typescript
{
  date: string,
  // Layer 1
  score: number, tier: "Basic"|"Fair"|"Good"|"Optimal"|"Elite",
  confidence: "Low"|"Medium"|"High",
  coverageStats: { totalFoodEntries, foodEntriesWithMicros, totalTakenSupplements, takenSupplementsWithMicros, overallCoverage },
  totals: MicroTotals,               // actual intake per nutrient key
  targets: MicroTotals,              // Layer 1 targets per nutrient key
  coverage: Record<string, { pctOfTarget: number; status: "low"|"ok"|"high" }>,
  topGaps: { microKey, label, pctOfTarget, suggestion? }[],   // max 3
  allMet: boolean,
  breakdown: { food: MicroTotals, supplements: MicroTotals },
  // Layer 2
  layer2Score: number, layer2Tier: string,
  layer2Targets: MicroTotals,
  layer2Coverage: Record<string, {...}>,
  layer2TopGaps: {...}[],
}
```

---

#### 9.17.7 Dashboard card UI (`AMQSCard.tsx`) тАФ exact layout

The card fetches 3 queries in parallel: `score/:date`, `score-range/:weekStart/:date` (weekStart = date тИТ 6 days), and `trend/:date` (enabled only once `score` has resolved).

**Design tokens used throughout (exact values тАФ match these, not approximations):**
- **Brand primary color** (orange): CSS var `--primary: 24 100% 50%` (HSL) тЖТ this is the orange used for the score underline, the "General Score" progress-bar-style trend line, the worst-gap progress bar, and the "+N" micro-goal numbers. Referenced in Tailwind as `text-primary` / `bg-primary` / `border-primary`, and directly as `hsl(var(--primary))` inside inline chart styles (Recharts can't consume Tailwind classes).
- **Layer 2 / "Performance" accent color** (blue): hardcoded literal `#3b82f6` (Tailwind's `blue-500`), NOT a CSS variable тАФ used consistently for every Layer-2-specific surface (Performance score number tint, Layer-2 trend sparkline stroke/fill, Layer-2 gap-row background/border, the blue line in the page's dual-line chart).
- **Success/tier-met color:** `emerald-500` (green) тАФ the "Baseline adequacy covered" banner and positive trend arrows (`тЖС +N vs last week`).
- **Regression color:** `amber-400` for the "General Score" card's own down-trend text, `amber-500` for the "Good" tier badge.
- **Card surface:** `bg-card` (near-black, matches the app's global dark theme), `rounded-xl` (12px corner radius), `p-6` (24px padding on all sides), `space-y-6` (24px gap between the header/scores/confidence/trend/gaps/goals/footer blocks).
- **Card glow:** a custom `amqs-card-glow` class (defined in `index.css`) gives the card a very subtle border to distinguish it as a premium/highlighted feature; when clickable, `amqs-card-interactive` adds a hover/press affordance.
- **Fonts:** headings use `font-display` (Space Grotesk) only inside dialog titles ("AMQS Details", "How AMQS is scored") тАФ the card body itself uses the default `font-sans` (Inter) for all labels/copy. All numeric scores (`69`, `57`, `94`, `92`, etc.) use `font-mono` тАФ this is a deliberate choice so digits don't shift width as they change, keeping the layout stable on every re-render.
- **Type scale on the card** (Tailwind sizes, smallest to largest): eyebrow/caption labels `text-[10px]` uppercase tracking-wide muted (e.g. "ATHLETE SCORE (AMQS)", "Optimisation targets", the italic disclaimer); gap/goal row body copy `text-xs` (12px); section labels ("Top gaps", "Micro-goals", "7-day trend") `text-[11px] font-semibold` muted; the two score numbers are the loudest element on the card at `text-4xl font-extrabold` (General) and `text-xl font-semibold` (Performance/Weekly, deliberately smaller+lighter-weight so General reads as primary) тАФ the card title "Micronutrient Quality" is `text-lg font-semibold`.
- **Muted-foreground opacity ladder:** rather than several distinct gray shades, the design uses ONE muted-foreground color at different opacities to create a visual hierarchy cheaply: `/70` for primary secondary-text (e.g. "General Score" label), `/60`/`/50` for section labels and confidence caption, `/40` for the disclaimer and least-important trend states, `/30` for placeholder icons. Replicate this "one color, many opacities" approach rather than picking arbitrary new grays тАФ it's what makes the muted text feel consistent across the card.

**Empty state** (`isEmptyState = !daily || (!hasFoodToday && !hasSupplementsToday)`):
- Score shows `"тАФ"` with a grey "Provisional" badge (`bg-slate-600 text-slate-300`).
- Confidence badge forced to "Low", progress bar at 0.
- Top-gaps section shows **3 hardcoded example gaps** (Vitamin D 15%, Magnesium 32%, Omega-3 8%) at 30% opacity with `aria-hidden`, captioned "Example тАФ updates after your first log" in italics.
- A "Log first meal" button (`variant="default"`, i.e. solid primary/orange) appears if `onLogFirstMeal` callback was passed (dashboard passes a function that opens the Add Food dialog; the micronutrients page passes one that navigates to `/dashboard?openAddFood=1`).

**Populated state, top to bottom (matches the reference screenshot pixel-for-pixel):**
1. **Header row:** "Micronutrient Quality" (`text-lg font-semibold`, white) directly above "ATHLETE SCORE (AMQS)" (`text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground/60`, small gap `mt-0.5`). A `ChevronRight` icon (`h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground/40`) sits right-aligned when the card is clickable (opens the detail dialog); replaced by a static `ShieldCheck` icon at `/30` opacity in the empty state.
2. **Two-column score row** (`grid grid-cols-2 gap-4`):
   - **Left column тАФ "General Score":** caption `text-xs text-muted-foreground/70`. Below it, the score number `69` at `text-4xl font-extrabold font-mono` with a subtle `amqs-glow` text-shadow effect (`text-shadow: 0 0 10px hsl(var(--primary)/0.15)`), plus a **thin 2px orange underline bar** positioned absolutely beneath the digits (`absolute bottom-0 h-[2px] bg-primary/30`) тАФ this is the horizontal orange line visible directly under the "69" in the screenshot. Immediately right of the number, a tier badge (`Fair` in the reference тАФ `bg-slate-500 text-white`, see tier color map below). Below that: the "what moved it" one-liner in `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/70` (e.g. `"+1901% Potassium Mg ┬╖ Ome..."`, truncated with CSS `truncate` if it overflows one line). Below that: the trend line in `text-[10px] font-medium`, colored green (`text-emerald-500/70`) when improving, e.g. `"тЖС +24 vs last week"`.
   - **Right column тАФ "Performance Score"** (shown whenever Layer 2 data exists, which is always in practice): caption `text-xs text-muted-foreground/50` (note: dimmer than the General caption тАФ Performance is visually secondary). Score number (`57` in the reference) at `text-xl font-semibold text-muted-foreground/60 font-mono` тАФ deliberately smaller and desaturated compared to General's bold white `text-4xl`, reinforcing that this is the "stretch" score, not the primary one. Tier badge next to it uses `variant="outline"` with muted styling (`border-border/30 text-muted-foreground/60`) rather than the solid tier-colored badge General gets. Below: "Optimisation targets" caption at `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/40`. Below that: its own trend line, same green/amber/muted color logic as General's.
   - Fallback (rare тАФ only if Layer 2 genuinely has no data): right column instead shows "Weekly Avg" + the `score-range` endpoint's average + its tier, styled identically to the Performance slot.
3. **Data Confidence row:** label `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/50 font-medium` + a small `Info` icon (`h-2.5 w-2.5 text-muted-foreground/30`) with a hover tooltip, badge (`variant="secondary"`, `text-[10px] bg-secondary/50`) showing `Low`/`Medium`/`High` right-aligned on the same row, then a full-width `<Progress>` bar (`h-1`, i.e. 4px tall) directly beneath тАФ in the reference screenshot this renders as a **solid orange bar filled 100% of the width** because confidence is High (progress value 100). At Medium it would render ~60% filled; Low ~30%.
4. **Mini 7-day trend sparkline:** label "7-day trend" (`text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground/50`) above a `h-12` (48px tall) `<AreaChart>` тАФ single muted line (Layer 1 score only), no legend, no Y-axis, only tiny (`fontSize: 8`, opacity 0.4) date-tick X-axis labels like `06-29`, `06-30`. Only rendered if the weekly range has >1 day of data. Line/fill color is `hsl(var(--muted-foreground))` at low opacity тАФ this sparkline is intentionally understated/monochrome (unlike the page's full chart, which is the colorful orange/blue dual-line version тАФ see ┬з9.17.8).
5. Then, one of three mutually exclusive blocks:
   - **Empty-state example gaps** (see above), or
   - **"Baseline adequacy covered" success banner** (`bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20 rounded-lg p-3`, `ShieldCheck` icon in `text-emerald-500`, copy in `text-xs text-emerald-600 dark:text-emerald-400 font-medium`) if `allMet === true`, or
   - **Top gaps list** (the reference screenshot's "Top gaps" section) тАФ section label `text-[11px] font-semibold text-muted-foreground/50`, then up to 3 rows, each a `bg-secondary/15 rounded p-2` block containing: a flex row with the nutrient label (`font-medium`, e.g. "Omega-3") left and the percentage right-aligned in muted text (formatted `"Target met"` if тЙе100, else `"{n}%"`, e.g. `"20%"`); directly below, a thin **1px-tall** progress bar (`h-1 bg-secondary/40 rounded-full`) where the **first/worst gap's fill is `bg-primary/70` (orange)** and all subsequent gaps are `bg-muted-foreground/30` (gray) тАФ this is why in the screenshot only the Omega-3 bar is orange and Folate/Vitamin A are gray; then, if a suggestion exists, a `"Try: {suggestion}"` caption at `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/60` with the food name itself bolded (`text-foreground/80 font-medium`).
6. **Micro-goals section** (only rendered if at least one of the top-3 gaps has a `suggestion`) тАФ separated from the gaps list by a top border (`border-t border-border/15 pt-3`). Section label "Micro-goals" (`text-[11px] font-semibold text-muted-foreground/50`). Each row: a bold orange point value (`text-primary/80 font-bold`, e.g. `"+6"`) immediately followed by `"if you add {suggestion} ({label})"` in `text-xs`, with the suggestion name bolded (`text-foreground/80 font-medium`) and the rest muted (`text-muted-foreground/70`). In the reference screenshot this renders as three stacked rows once expanded: `+6 if you add Flax Seeds (Omega-3)`, `+4 if you add Chickpeas (Dry) (Folate)`, `+4 if you add Sweet Potato (Baked) (Vitamin A)`. By default only the single best (highest-point) goal is shown; a `"See N micro-goals тЖТ"` link (`text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/50`, hover `text-muted-foreground`) expands the rest via a `framer-motion` height/opacity animation (`initial={{opacity:0,height:0}}`, staggered `delay: i * 0.05`). Point estimate formula:
   ```typescript
   pointEst = clamp(round(((100 - pctOfTarget) / 100) * 7), min=2, max=8)
   ```
   i.e., a bigger deficiency yields a bigger displayed point value, floor 2 / ceiling 8. (Sanity check against the reference: Omega-3 at 20% тЖТ `round(0.8*7)=6` тЬУ; Folate at 39% тЖТ `round(0.61*7)=4` тЬУ; Vitamin A at 48% тЖТ `round(0.52*7)=4` тЬУ тАФ confirms the formula.)
7. **Footer** (`pt-2 border-t border-border/15 space-y-1.5`, always shown): disclaimer in italic `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/40 leading-tight` тАФ *"General nutrition targets тАФ not medical advice. Blood tests, diagnosed deficiencies, or a registered dietitian override these figures."* Directly below, a "How scored" link/button: a small `BookOpen` icon (`h-3 w-3`) plus the text "How scored", both `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/40` with a `hover:text-muted-foreground/70` transition тАФ clicking opens the separate "How AMQS is scored" reference dialog (┬з9.17.7b).

**Tier color map** (`getTierColor` тАФ applies to both the daily-score badge and the weekly/tier badges throughout the card and dialogs):
```
Elite   тЖТ bg-emerald-500 text-white
Optimal тЖТ bg-blue-500 text-white
Good    тЖТ bg-amber-500 text-white
default (Fair, Basic, or the empty-state "Provisional" pseudo-tier) тЖТ bg-slate-500 text-white
```

**"What moved it" line logic:**
```typescript
if (no data today) тЖТ "Log a meal or supplement to see drivers"
else:
  topContributor = nutrient with the highest combined (food + supplement) raw intake value across all 17 keys
  topGap = topGaps[0]
  line = `+{round(contributor.value)}% {contributor.label} ┬╖ {topGap.label} at {formatPct(topGap.pctOfTarget)}`
  // if neither exists: "Log one more meal to improve insight quality"
```
Note this uses the **raw summed intake value**, not a percentage-of-target тАФ it's just "which nutrient did you get the most of today" as a rough narrative hook, not a scientific claim. This is why the reference screenshot shows an odd-looking `"+1901% Potassium Mg"` тАФ that's not a percent-of-target, it's the raw combined-intake number for potassium (mg) that happened to be the highest of the 17 raw totals that day.

---

#### 9.17.7a Detail dialog (opens on card click, only when not in empty state)

A `shadcn` `<Dialog>` (`sm:max-w-[400px] max-h-[85vh] overflow-y-auto`), title "AMQS Details" in `font-display` (Space Grotesk тАФ the one place on this feature that departs from the card's default Inter body font, consistent with the rest of the app using Space Grotesk for headings). Content, top to bottom:

1. **Side-by-side score cards** (`grid grid-cols-2 gap-3`): left card `bg-secondary/20 rounded-lg p-3` shows "GENERAL SCORE" / "Baseline Adequacy" captions + the Layer 1 score (`text-2xl font-bold font-mono`) + tier badge. Right card `bg-secondary/10` (slightly dimmer background than the left, reinforcing Layer 2 as secondary) shows "PERFORMANCE SCORE" / "Athlete Optimisation" + the Layer 2 score (`text-2xl font-bold font-mono text-muted-foreground/70` тАФ note it's tinted muted even though it's the same font size as General here, unlike on the card where it was also smaller).
2. **7-day trend sparklines, side by side** (`grid grid-cols-2 gap-2`): "Basic" card (`bg-secondary/15`) with an orange (`hsl(var(--primary))`) sparkline; "Performance" card (`bg-blue-500/5 border border-blue-500/10`) with a blue (`#3b82f6`) sparkline. Each `h-10` (40px), each with its own trend-line text colored per the shared `trendLineColor` helper.
3. **Strong-performance callout** (only if `daily.score >= 85`): green banner identical in style to the card's "allMet" banner тАФ *"Baseline micronutrient needs covered. If you're training hard, consider optimising toward athlete targets."*
4. **"What moved it today"** section тАФ repeats the same one-liner from the card, but as its own labeled block (`text-[11px] font-semibold text-muted-foreground/60` label + `text-sm text-foreground` value) rather than a small caption.
5. **"Layer 1 gaps (baseline)"** тАФ same row styling as the card's Top Gaps list, but percentage text reads `"{n}% of target"` instead of just `"{n}%"`, and the worst bar is `bg-primary/70`.
6. **"Layer 2 gaps (athlete optimisation)"** (only if Layer 2 has gaps) тАФ visually distinct from Layer 1 gaps: rows use `bg-blue-500/5 border border-blue-500/10` (vs. plain `bg-secondary/15` for Layer 1), percentage text reads `"{n}% of athlete target"`, and the worst bar is `bg-blue-500/60` (vs. orange for Layer 1).
7. **"Quick wins"** section тАФ up to 2 items from Layer 1's `topGaps`, each rendered as `bg-primary/5 border border-primary/10 rounded p-2`: `"Close {label} gap"` in `text-primary/80 font-medium` followed by `" тАФ add {suggestion}"` in muted text. If there are no gaps at all: *"All baseline targets covered. Focus on athlete optimisation above."*
8. **Footer** (`pt-2 border-t border-border/20`): disclaimer *"Based on logged foods and supplements. Estimates only; not medical advice."* + a "How this is scored тАФ references and methodology" link that closes this dialog and opens the reference dialog (┬з9.17.7b) after a 150ms delay (avoids two dialogs visually overlapping mid-transition).

---

#### 9.17.7b "How AMQS is scored" reference dialog

A separate `<Dialog>` (`sm:max-w-[420px] max-h-[85vh] overflow-y-auto`, title "How AMQS is scored" in `font-display`), opened from either the card footer or the detail dialog footer. Purely educational/static content тАФ no data fetching. Sections, each `<h4 className="font-semibold text-sm">` + `<p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">`:

1. **"Two-layer model"** тАФ explains Layer 1 (Adequacy, population RNIs) vs Layer 2 (Athlete Optimisation, sports-nutrition-informed stricter targets).
2. **"How the score is calculated"** тАФ plain-language restatement of the capped-adequacy weighted-average formula, noting Iron/Calcium/Vitamin D/Magnesium/Zinc carry higher weights.
3. **"Tier thresholds"** тАФ a small list re-using `getTierColor` badges next to each tier's numeric range (Elite 95тАУ100 with the note "Requires critical nutrients тЙе70% of target", Optimal 85тАУ94, Good 70тАУ84, Fair 50тАУ69, Basic <50).
4. **"Tracked nutrients"** тАФ lists all 17 by name (not key), and a one-line note that Layer 2 reuses the same 17 with stricter targets where evidence supports it.
5. **"Key references"** тАФ a bulleted, italicized-title citation list (Thomas/Erdman/Burke 2016 JAND; Maughan et al. 2018 IOC Consensus BJSM; IOM Dietary Reference Intakes; Burke & Deakin Clinical Sports Nutrition 5th ed; Holick 2011 JCEM; Volpe 2015 Curr Sports Med Rep) тАФ replicate real citations relevant to your own nutrient targets rather than inventing placeholders; this list exists specifically to give the scoring model credibility and a paper trail for the "not medical advice" framing.
6. **"Evidence caveat"** тАФ explicitly states Layer 1 is population-level DRI/RNI, Layer 2 is an optional non-official optimisation benchmark, and that some nutrients intentionally keep Layer 2 equal to Layer 1 where stronger athlete-specific targets aren't defensible.
7. **Footer disclaimer** (identical pattern to the other two disclaimers): *"These are general nutrition targets, not medical advice. Blood tests, a diagnosed deficiency, your clinician, or a registered dietitian always override generic app-generated targets."*
