#### 9.17.8 Dedicated `/micronutrients` page (`micronutrients.tsx`)

This page is deliberately thin тАФ its only additions over the card are a date navigator and a full-width, colorful version of the trend chart. Screenshot reference: title "Micronutrient Score" is on the page's own header (not shown in the attached screenshots, which start mid-scroll), but the trend section below the card is the "7-Day Trend" block visible in the reference images.

1. **Date navigator** тАФ prev/next day buttons (`variant="outline" size="icon"`, `ChevronLeft`/`ChevronRight` icons) + native `<input type="date">` (`w-[160px] font-medium`) preceded by a small `Calendar` icon, plus a "Today" shortcut button (`variant="ghost" size="sm"`) that only appears when not viewing today. State is a local `selectedDate` string (`yyyy-MM-dd`), passed straight into `<AMQSCard date={selectedDate} .../>`.
2. **Full-width 7-day trend chart** тАФ its own `bg-card rounded-xl p-5 space-y-4` container (note: `p-5`/20px padding here, slightly less than the main card's `p-6`). Fetches its own `trend/:selectedDate` query (independent of the one inside `AMQSCard`, so there are 4 total AMQS network requests when this page loads: card's score, card's score-range, card's trend, page's trend). This chart differs visually from the card's monochrome mini-sparkline тАФ it is the colorful, primary visual on the page:
   - **Header row** (`flex items-center justify-between`): left side "7-Day Trend" (`text-sm font-semibold`) + "Basic vs Performance this week" (`text-[11px] text-muted-foreground/60`) caption. Right side, right-aligned two-line trend readout: `"Basic {formatTrendLine}"` and `"Perf {formatTrendLine}"`, each `text-xs font-medium`, colored green/amber/muted per the shared `trendLineColor` helper тАФ in the reference screenshot both read green: `"Basic тЖС +24 vs last week"` / `"Perf тЖС +23 vs last week"`.
   - **Chart body**, `h-40` (160px tall), `<AreaChart>` with `margin={{top:4,right:4,left:0,bottom:0}}`. Two `<Area>` series plotted on the same 0тАУ100 Y-axis (hidden): Layer 1 ("l1") тАФ `stroke: hsl(var(--primary))` (orange), `strokeWidth: 2`, `strokeOpacity: 0.7`, gradient fill from `hsl(var(--primary))` at 20% opacity fading to 0; Layer 2 ("l2") тАФ `stroke: #3b82f6` (blue), `strokeWidth: 1.5` (thinner than L1, reinforcing it as secondary), `strokeOpacity: 0.5`, gradient fill from `#3b82f6` at 12% opacity fading to 0. In the reference screenshot this renders as an orange line sitting slightly above a blue line, both following the same general hump shape, with the area beneath shaded in each color. X-axis shows visible `MM-DD` date ticks (`date.slice(5)`, `fontSize: 10`, opacity 0.5, no axis line/tick marks). A `<Tooltip>` (`background: hsl(var(--card))`, `border: 1px solid hsl(var(--border))`, `borderRadius: 8`, `fontSize: 11`) appears on hover, showing both series' raw values.
   - **Below the chart:** two stat cards (`grid grid-cols-2 gap-3`) тАФ left "General avg" (`bg-secondary/15 rounded-lg p-3`, caption `text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground/60`, value `text-lg font-bold font-mono` white, sub-caption "Baseline adequacy" `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/50`); right "Performance avg" (`bg-blue-500/5 border border-blue-500/10`, same type scale but value tinted `text-muted-foreground/70`, sub-caption "Athlete optimisation"). In the reference screenshot these read `94` and `92` respectively.
   - **Page footer** (`text-center space-y-1 pb-4`, below the trend card, not inside it): italic disclaimer `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/50` тАФ *"AMQS combines food and supplement micronutrient data. Estimates only тАФ not medical advice."* тАФ directly followed by `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/40` тАФ *"Basic = baseline adequacy targets ┬╖ Performance = athlete optimisation targets"*.
3. Chart is only rendered if `trend` has resolved AND `chartData.length > 1` (i.e., not on a brand-new account with <2 days of history).

**Key visual distinction to preserve when replicating:** the *card's* mini-sparkline (┬з9.17.7, point 4) is intentionally monochrome/muted тАФ it's a glanceable hint, not the main event. The *page's* full chart is intentionally the vivid orange-vs-blue dual-line version тАФ it's the page's whole reason for existing. Don't accidentally swap these or make the card's sparkline colorful; that would undercut the page's exclusivity as the "detailed trend" destination.

---

#### 9.17.9 Step-by-step replication checklist

1. **Data model:** Add a 17-key micronutrient-per-100g table to your ingredient/food catalog, plus a `commonScore` (0тАУ1) field per ingredient. Add a `microsPerUnit` JSONB-style field to your supplement catalog (per-dose-unit values for whichever of the 17 keys apply).
2. **Aggregation (`micros.ts` equivalent):** Write two functions that sum today's food-entry and taken-supplement-intake micronutrient contributions respectively, plus a composite-food decomposition map for any multi-ingredient quick-add meals. Merge into one `totals` dict.
3. **Scoring engine (`amqs.ts` equivalent):** Hardcode the 17-nutrient table above verbatim (weights + both target layers, sex-specific values). Implement the capped-adequacy weighted-average formula for Layer 1 and Layer 2 independently. Implement tier thresholds and the critical-nutrient Elite floor (always checked against Layer 1 coverage, even for Layer 2's tier).
4. **Gaps + 3 suggestions:** For each layer, sort under-target nutrients ascending by pctOfTarget, take the top 3 тЖТ these become the "Top gaps" rows. For each gap's suggestion, rank ingredients by `potency*0.6 + potency*commonScore*0.4`, prefer candidates with `commonScore >= 0.5` (┬з9.17.3) тАФ a gap with no qualifying ingredient simply renders without a "Try:" line.
5. **Confidence:** Compute `itemsWithMicros / totalItems` across food entries + taken supplements; map to Low/Medium/High at the 40%/75% breakpoints.
6. **Trend:** Compute daily AMQS for a rolling 14-day window, split into two 7-day halves, diff the averages, classify at ┬▒3 threshold. Do this for both layers in one response.
7. **API:** Expose `score/:date`, `score-range/:start/:end`, `trend/:date`, and a raw `micros/:date` debug endpoint, all scoped to the authenticated user.
8. **Dashboard card тАФ pixel-accurate UI:** Build the empty/populated states exactly as in ┬з9.17.7 тАФ this is the highest-traffic surface. Use the exact design tokens: `--primary` orange (`hsl(24 100% 50%)`) for General/worst-gap/micro-goal accents, literal `#3b82f6` blue for every Layer-2 surface, `font-mono` for all score digits, `font-sans`/Inter for body copy, `font-display`/Space Grotesk only in dialog titles, and the single-muted-foreground-color-at-varying-opacity system (`/70 тЖТ /60 тЖТ /50 тЖТ /40 тЖТ /30`) rather than inventing new grays. Match the type scale precisely: `text-4xl font-extrabold` General score, `text-xl font-semibold` Performance score, `text-[10px]`/`text-[11px]`/`text-xs` for captions/labels/body in that ascending order.
9. **Detail + reference dialogs:** Replicate the "AMQS Details" dialog (┬з9.17.7a тАФ side-by-side score cards, dual sparklines, Layer 1 vs Layer 2 gap sections with distinct orange/blue styling, quick wins) and the separate "How AMQS is scored" methodology dialog (┬з9.17.7b тАФ two-layer explainer, formula, tier thresholds, full nutrient list, real citations, evidence caveat).
10. **Dedicated page:** Wrap the same card component with a date navigator and add the full-width, vividly-colored dual-line 7-day chart per ┬з9.17.8 (orange Layer 1 over blue Layer 2, `h-40`, visible axis + tooltip) plus the General/Performance average stat cards тАФ don't reimplement AMQS logic separately for the page, and don't let the card's own sparkline become colorful (keep that muted/monochrome тАФ see the key visual distinction note above).
11. **Copy/disclaimers:** Reuse the exact disclaimer strings verbatim тАФ they're doing real compliance work ("not medical advice", "Basic = baseline adequacy... Performance = athlete optimisation", "Blood tests, diagnosed deficiencies, or a registered dietitian override these figures").

---

### 9.18 Add Food Dialog тАФ Full Replication Guide

The "Add Food" dialog (`FoodEntryDialog` in `dashboard.tsx`, ~lines 2235тАУ4505) is the single entry point for logging food. It is one component with **4 tabs** (Search / Whole Food / Barcode / Custom) sharing one `grams` state var and one submit path per tab. A companion `EditFoodDialog` (lines 4506тАУ4767) duplicates the count/grams unit logic for editing existing entries. There is also a small "Create Custom Food" sub-dialog reachable from the Barcode tab.

#### 9.18.0 File map

| Concern | File |
|---|---|
| Main dialog (4 tabs, all state, submit handlers) | `client/src/pages/dashboard.tsx` (`FoodEntryDialog`, ~2235тАУ4505) |
| Edit dialog (grams/macro edit + count-mode) | `client/src/pages/dashboard.tsx` (`EditFoodDialog`, 4506тАУ4767) |
| Core-food unit config (count-mode data) | `client/src/lib/coreFoodUnits.ts` |
| Curated quick-add meals ("Core Foods" list on Whole Food tab empty state) | `client/src/pages/dashboard.tsx` (`CORE_FOODS`, ~line 2212) |
| Mutations (`useCreateFoodEntry`, `useUpdateFoodEntry`) | `client/src/hooks/use-logs.ts` |
| OFF fuzzy-match engine (barcode тЖТ ingredient mapping) | `server/lib/offMatch.ts` |
| Barcode + custom-food + food-entry routes | `server/routes.ts` (barcode: 553тАУ812; food entries: 1880тАУ1980) |
| `foodEntries` table schema | `shared/schema.ts` (147тАУ169) |
| Local ingredient DB (per-100g macros/micros, ~700 items) | `data/ingredients.json` |

#### 9.18.1 The 4 tabs at a glance

| Tab | Data source | Grams/serving control | Submit target |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Search** | Open Food Facts live API (`GET /api/foods/search?q=`) | Fixed to OFF serving; tapping a result immediately calls `createEntry` | `POST /api/food-entries` (`sourceType: "off"`) |
| **Whole Food** | Local `data/ingredients.json` (autocomplete) | Count mode (steppers) for ~30 curated foods, else free-form grams input with quick-amount chips | `POST /api/food-entries` (`sourceType: "ingredient"`) |
| **Barcode** | OFF barcode lookup (`GET /api/food/barcode/:code`) + local custom-food DB, plus a live camera scanner | Free-form grams input | `POST /api/food-entries` (`sourceType: "off"`, plus a micronutrient-mapping side effect) |
| **Custom** | Manual entry (name + all 5 macro fields) | Free-form grams input | `POST /api/food-entries` (`sourceType: "manual"`) |

All 4 tabs share: `grams`, `date`, `selectedMeal`, `selectedSnackIndex` state, and ultimately call the same `useCreateFoodEntry()` mutation, which hits `POST /api/food-entries` and on success invalidates `/api/me/food`, `/api/me/food-entries/range`, `/api/me/logs`, `/api/me/amqs/score(-range)`, and `/api/me/supplement-micros`, then shows a smart toast (see ┬з9.18.6).

#### 9.18.2 `foodEntries` schema тАФ what the server actually persists

```ts
// shared/schema.ts
foodEntries = {
  id, userId, date,              // ISO yyyy-MM-dd
  name, grams, calories, protein, carbs, fat, fibre,
  meal,                          // breakfast|lunch|dinner|snack
  snackIndex,                    // only for meal="snack"; groups multiple snacks per day

  // OFF / provenance tracking:
  sourceType,                    // 'manual' | 'off' | 'ingredient'
  offBarcode,                    // barcode string if scanned/looked up
  ingredientIndex,                // index into ingredients.json тАФ powers AMQS micronutrient rollup
  macroSource,                   // 'off' | 'ingredient' | 'manual' | 'mixed'
  microSource,                   // 'ingredient' | 'none'

  // Raw/cooked basis normalization (Whole Food tab only):
  enteredBasis,                  // 'raw' | 'cooked' | null
  normalizedGrams,               // grams converted to canonicalBasis for nutrition math
  yieldFactorUsed,                // cookedYieldFactor applied, for audit/display
}
```

**Key insight:** the server stores whatever macros the client computed and sent тАФ it does **not** recompute calories/protein/carbs/fat/fibre from `ingredientIndex` + `grams` server-side. All nutrition math (per-100g ├Ч grams/100, rawтЖФcooked conversion, unit-to-grams conversion) happens client-side before submit. `ingredientIndex` and `microSource` exist purely so the AMQS micronutrient engine (┬з9.17) can later re-derive full micronutrient profiles from `data/ingredients.json` using the stored index тАФ the macro fields on the row are a frozen snapshot, immune to later edits of the ingredient database.

#### 9.18.3 Whole Food tab тАФ count vs. grams mode (the core "faithful replication" detail)

This is the most nuanced UI/logic combination in the dialog. Two independent client-only mechanisms layer on top of the same `grams` field:

**Mechanism A тАФ Raw/Cooked basis toggle** (any ingredient with `supportsCookedToggle: true` in `ingredients.json`, e.g. rice, chicken breast, pasta):
- Shown only when `selectedIngredient.supportsCookedToggle` is true.
- Two-button segmented toggle: `Raw` / `Cooked`, default = ingredient's `canonicalBasis`.
- `getNormalizedGrams()` converts the entered grams into the canonical basis using `cookedYieldFactor` (e.g. rice cookedтЖТraw divides by ~0.35; the exact factor is per-ingredient in `ingredients.json`, field `cookedYieldFactor`).
- Nutrition math always runs on the **normalized** (canonical-basis) grams, never the raw user-entered number, when the toggle is present.
- A helper caption appears when the entered basis тЙа canonical basis: `"Nutrition calculated from {normalizedGrams}g {canonicalBasis} equivalent (yield factor: {cookedYieldFactor})"`.
- On submit, the entry stores `enteredBasis`, `normalizedGrams`, and `yieldFactorUsed` for later audit/display; `grams` itself stores the raw user-entered amount (what they'd recognize on their plate).

**Mechanism B тАФ Count/Size unit mode** (foods present in `CORE_FOOD_UNITS` map in `coreFoodUnits.ts`, e.g. "Egg", "Banana", "Slice of Bread" тАФ ~30 curated whole foods keyed by *exact* ingredient name):
- On ingredient select, `getCoreFoodUnit(name)` is checked; if a match exists, the UI **defaults to count mode** and shows a `Count` / `Grams` segmented toggle (same visual pattern as the basis toggle: `bg-primary text-primary-foreground` for active, `text-muted-foreground` for inactive).
- **Count mode UI:**
  - Optional **Size** row (only if `unit.supportsSize`): 3 buttons (Small/Medium/Large), each showing its gram value below the label (from `unit.gramsBySize[size]`) when available; selected = `border-primary bg-primary/10`.
  - **Count** stepper: тИТ / + buttons (h-9 w-9, disabled at count тЙд1 or тЙе20) around a large `text-2xl font-extrabold font-mono` count display, plus a live `"тЙИ {grams}g total"` caption.
  - Every stepper/size click calls `computeUnitGrams(unit, count, size)` and writes the result straight into `grams` тАФ the user never sees or edits a raw grams number in this mode.
- **Grams mode (fallback):** a plain numeric input + quick-amount chips (`quickAmounts`), identical in look to the non-unit case.
- `computeUnitGrams(unit, count, size)` (in `coreFoodUnits.ts`): if `unit.supportsSize`, returns `unit.gramsBySize[size] * count`; else returns `unit.gramsPerUnit * count`.
- **Server never knows about "count" or "size."** By the time the entry reaches `POST /api/food-entries`, only the final `grams` integer is sent тАФ count/size/unit-label are 100% client-side UX sugar over the same per-100g ingredient math every other tab uses. Do not add a `unit`/`count` column server-side; the mobile client should replicate this as pure local state.

**Nutrition preview card** (shown under either mechanism once an ingredient is selected): dark `bg-secondary/30 rounded-lg p-4` panel, header row `"Estimated Nutrition"` + `text-lg font-bold text-primary` calorie figure, then a 4-column `grid grid-cols-4` of Prot/Carb/Fat/Fib each as `{label: 10px bold caption}` over `{value: text-sm font-mono}`, with Fibre alone tinted `text-emerald-500`/`text-emerald-600`. This exact 4-column macro-chip layout recurs 3 times in the dialog (Whole Food preview, Barcode preview, and тАФ with per-item styling тАФ the OFF search result rows) and should be extracted as one shared subcomponent in a mobile rebuild.

**Empty state:** when no ingredient is selected and search is empty, show the **"Core Foods"** quick-add list тАФ `CORE_FOODS` (curated common mixed meals, e.g. "Chicken & Rice Bowl") rendered as a vertical list of rows (`hover-elevate`, name + `"{serving}g serving"` caption on the left, calories on the right); tapping one calls `createEntry` directly with pre-baked macros (`sourceType: "manual"`, `macroSource: "manual"`, `microSource: "none"`) тАФ no dialog step, no confirmation, immediate log + toast.

#### 9.18.4 Barcode tab тАФ scan, lookup, and micronutrient mapping

**Manual entry path:** a barcode text input + "Lookup" button call `GET /api/food/barcode/:code`, which proxies Open Food Facts and returns `{ name, image_url, calories_kcal_100g, protein_g_100g, carbs_g_100g, fat_g_100g, fibre_g_100g, suggestions: { best, top } }`. `suggestions` come from the server-side fuzzy matcher (`server/lib/offMatch.ts`, `matchOffToIngredients`) which scores the OFF product name against every row in `data/ingredients.json` and returns a confidence tier:
- `finalScore >= 0.45` тЖТ `"high"` confidence (auto-applied as the micronutrient mapping, no user action needed)
- `finalScore >= 0.25` тЖТ `"medium"` (shown as a suggestion chip, user must confirm)
- below that тЖТ `"low"` or no match (user must search manually or explicitly skip)

**Not-found path:** if the barcode isn't in OFF, the UI shows an inline "Save to PRFMR database" mini-form (name, brand, kcal/protein/carbs/fat/fibre per 100g, optional serving size) that posts to `POST /api/food/barcode/:code/create`, adding it to the app's own custom-food store so it's found instantly next time (`queryClient.invalidateQueries(["/api/foods/custom"])`, then re-runs the lookup).

**Micronutrient mapping panel** (`section-micro-mapping`, shown once a barcode result is found): a bordered `bg-muted/30` card with three possible states тАФ
1. **Mapped:** green check row `"Mapped to: {ingredient.name}"`, with a "Change" link to reopen picking.
2. **Skipped:** italic `"Skipped (macros only)"` + "Enable micros" link.
3. **Unmapped (needs input):** shows up to 3 suggestion chips (colored border by confidence: emerald=high, amber=medium, none=low) each with a 2-line "why" caption (`s.reasons`) for medium/low confidence, a live-filtered ingredient search box (min 2 chars, top 10 matches), and a "Skip micros" text link. Choosing a suggestion or search result calls `saveIngredientMapping(ingredient, index)` тЖТ `POST /api/food/barcode/:code/map` which persists the OFF-barcodeтЖТingredient mapping server-side so future scans of the same barcode auto-resolve at `"high"` confidence without re-prompting.

**Camera scanner:** `Html5Qrcode` library, decoding EAN_13/EAN_8/UPC_A/UPC_E/CODE_128. Implementation detail worth preserving faithfully: it uses five separate boolean refs (`isRunningRef`, `startingRef`, `stoppingRef`, `didDecodeRef`, `cancelledRef`) plus a `startCountRef` counter purely to prevent race conditions from rapid start/stop taps (a common Html5Qrcode crash source тАФ calling `.start()` while a previous `.start()` promise is still pending throws). Camera constraint strategy: try `facingMode: "environment"` (rear camera) first, catch and retry with `"user"` (front camera) on failure тАФ needed because some desktop/laptop webcams reject `"environment"` outright. A collapsible debug panel (`showScannerDebug`) surfaces secure-context flag, origin, `MediaDevices` availability, camera count, start-call count, last error, and user agent тАФ keep this for support/debugging parity, it has caught real device-specific camera permission issues in testing.

Once a barcode result is loaded, the UI shows the same 4-column macro preview grid as Whole Food (┬з9.18.3), a grams input pre-filled from OFF's typical serving (or 100), quick-amount chips, then the micro-mapping panel, then a single "Add to Log" button (disabled while `isSavingMapping` is in flight, so the mapping write always completes before or alongside the food-entry write).

#### 9.18.5 Custom tab & "Add to My Foods" sub-dialog

The Custom tab is the simplest: a name field + a 6-field grid (grams, calories, protein, carbs, fat, fibre) with no per-100g math тАФ whatever numbers are typed are submitted verbatim as the total for that entry (`sourceType: "manual"`).

Separately, "Add to My Foods" (reachable from the Barcode tab's not-found state, or generally) opens a dedicated `Dialog` (not a tab) for saving a reusable custom food to the user's personal database: name*, brand, barcode (all optional except name), then a 5-column *per-100g* nutrition grid (calories*, protein, carbs, fat, fibre тАФ asterisked fields required to enable the Save button). Submits via `handleCreateCustomFood` тЖТ `POST /api/foods/custom`, which both saves the food for future quick-lookup (`GET /api/foods/custom/barcode/:code`) and immediately logs it as the current entry ("Save & Log" button label makes this dual behavior explicit).

#### 9.18.6 Server endpoints тАФ full reference

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `/api/foods/search?q=` | GET | Live OFF text search (Search tab results list) |
| `/api/foods/search/match` | POST | Client-side cached match-scoring helper for OFF results |
| `/api/ingredients` | GET | Full local ingredient DB (Whole Food tab autocomplete + AMQS) |
| `/api/food/barcode/:code` | GET | OFF barcode lookup + ingredient-match suggestions |
| `/api/food/barcode/:code/map` | POST | Persist a confirmed OFF-barcode тЖТ ingredient mapping |
| `/api/food/barcode/:code/create` | POST | Save a not-found OFF barcode into the custom-food store |
| `/api/foods/custom` | GET/POST/DELETE | User's personal reusable custom foods |
| `/api/foods/custom/barcode/:code` | GET | Look up a custom food by barcode |
| `/api/food-entries` (`api.food.create`) | POST | Create a logged food entry (all 4 tabs funnel here) тАФ requires auth; validates against `insertFoodEntrySchema` via `api.food.create.input.safeParse`; double-verifies the row was actually persisted by re-querying before returning 201 |
| `/api/me/food/:date` (`api.food.list`) | GET | List entries for a date |
| `/api/food-entries/range?username&start&end` | GET | Range query, normalizes dates to `yyyy-MM-dd` |
| `/api/food/:id` | PATCH | Update an entry (used by `EditFoodDialog`) |
| `/api/food/:id` (`api.food.delete`) | DELETE | Delete an entry |

**Note on the create endpoint's defensive verification:** `POST /api/food-entries` does not trust a truthy insert result тАФ after calling `storage.createFoodEntry`, it re-fetches the day's entries and confirms the new `id` is actually present before returning 201, logging `[food][create][error] reason="POST-INSERT verification failed"` and a 500 if not. This was clearly added after a real silent-failure incident; a mobile backend replication should keep this belt-and-suspenders check.

#### 9.18.7 Edit dialog тАФ gramsтЖФmacro auto-recalculation

`EditFoodDialog` (per-entry pencil icon, `opacity-100 sm:opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100` тАФ always visible on mobile/touch, hover-reveal on desktop) lets a user tweak an already-logged entry. Key mechanic: it captures the entry's **per-100g base values** once on open (`basePer100g = { calories, protein, carbs, fat, fibre } / grams * 100`), then on every grams change (including from count/size steppers) it recomputes all 5 macro fields from that fixed per-100g base тАФ but the macro fields remain independently editable afterward (typing directly into Calories/Protein/etc. does not fight back or re-derive from grams). This means: changing grams cascades to macros, but changing a macro field directly is a one-way override until grams changes again. It duplicates the exact same count/size stepper UI and `getCoreFoodUnit`/`computeUnitGrams` logic as the Whole Food tab (separate `editUnitMode/editUnitCount/editUnitSize` state тАФ not shared code, deliberately reimplemented inline). When `editUnitMode === "count"`, the Grams input becomes read-only (`opacity-50`) since it's fully derived. Also includes a meal/snack-index reassignment `Select` pair at the top, letting a user move an entry between breakfast/lunch/dinner/snack (with automatic "next snack #" suggestion) without deleting and re-adding it.

#### 9.18.8 Mutation success behavior тАФ the "smart toast"

`useCreateFoodEntry()` (in `use-logs.ts`) does more than invalidate caches: on success, it snapshots the AMQS score *before* invalidation, waits for the invalidated `/api/me/amqs/score/:date` to refetch, and picks the most encouraging thing to say:
1. If a toast was already shown in the last debounce window (`AMQS_TOAST_DEBOUNCE_MS`), just show a generic "Logged тАФ dashboard updated" toast (prevents toast spam from rapid multi-item logging).
2. Else if the AMQS score went up, show `"AMQS +{delta}"` with a "See updated gaps" action button that scrolls to the AMQS card.
3. Else if the user's previous #1 nutrient gap improved (`pctOfTarget` increased), show `"{gap label} gap improved by {N}%"` with the same action button.
4. Else, generic `"Logged тАФ dashboard updated... AMQS recalculating"`.

A mobile replication should preserve at least the score-delta and generic-fallback tiers тАФ this positive-reinforcement toast is a deliberate engagement mechanic tied directly to the AMQS feature (┬з9.17), not incidental UI polish.

#### 9.18.9 Pixel-accurate UI notes for faithful replication

- Dialog shell: standard shadcn `Dialog`/`DialogContent`, `DialogTitle` uses `font-display` (Space Grotesk).
- Tabs: shadcn `Tabs`/`TabsList`/`TabsTrigger` with 4 triggers (Search/Whole Food/Barcode/Custom); each `TabsContent` uses `space-y-4` to `space-y-6` + `py-4`.
- All segmented 2-button toggles (Raw/Cooked, Count/Grams) share one visual pattern: `flex items-center rounded-md border overflow-hidden`, each button `px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium`, active = `bg-primary text-primary-foreground`, inactive = `text-muted-foreground`. Replicate this as one shared `SegmentedToggle` component in mobile rather than hand-rolling per instance.
- Size-select buttons (Small/Medium/Large) and OptionBtn-style choices: `flex-1 py-1.5 rounded-md border text-xs font-medium capitalize`, selected = `border-primary bg-primary/10 text-foreground`, unselected = `border-border/40 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-secondary/30`.
- Stepper buttons: `h-9 w-9 rounded-md border border-border/60`, large glyph (`text-lg font-bold`), `disabled:opacity-30` at min/max bounds; count display `text-2xl font-extrabold font-mono`.
- The 4-column macro-preview grid (Prot/Carb/Fat/Fib) recurs verbatim in 2+ places: caption row `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-bold` (Fibre variant: `text-emerald-500`), value row `font-mono text-sm` (Fibre variant: `text-emerald-600`).
- OFF search result rows: `40├Ч40px` rounded thumbnail (or `UtensilsCrossed` placeholder icon in a bordered box), name `text-sm font-medium truncate`, brand `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate`, right-aligned calorie figure `text-sm font-mono font-medium` + macro summary `P{x} C{x} F{x}` in `text-[10px] text-muted-foreground`.
- Core Foods list rows: `hover-elevate`, name left / `"{serving}g serving"` caption, calories right in `text-sm font-mono font-medium` + `kcal` unit label.
- Barcode scanner viewport: `id="reader"`, `w-full rounded-lg border bg-black min-h-[200px]` when active, `hidden` otherwise; pulsing helper caption `"Position barcode within the frame"` (`animate-pulse`, `text-[10px]`).

#### 9.18.10 Replication checklist

1. Build the shared macro-preview grid and segmented-toggle as standalone components first тАФ they're reused 3тАУ4├Ч.
2. Implement `data/ingredients.json` as a bundled local asset (not a live DB table) with per-item `supportsCookedToggle`, `canonicalBasis`, `cookedYieldFactor`, `commonScore`, and macro/micro per-100g fields тАФ the Whole Food tab and AMQS both depend on it.
3. Port `coreFoodUnits.ts` verbatim (name-keyed lookup map + `computeUnitGrams`) тАФ it's small, pure, and has no server dependency.
4. Keep all count/size/basis math 100% client-side; the server contract is just `{ grams, calories, protein, carbs, fat, fibre, ...provenance fields }`.
5. Replicate the OFF barcode flow end-to-end: lookup тЖТ fuzzy-match suggestions тЖТ confirm/skip mapping тЖТ optional "not found, create it" fallback. Don't skip the confidence-tiered auto-apply-vs-prompt logic тАФ it's what makes high-confidence matches frictionless while still catching ambiguous ones.
6. For barcode scanning on mobile (native), use a platform barcode scanner (e.g. `expo-camera`'s barcode scanning or `vision-camera-code-scanner`) rather than porting Html5Qrcode; but preserve the same race-condition-safe start/stop guarding and the rearтЖТfront camera fallback behavior, plus a debug panel for support.
7. Reuse `POST /api/food-entries` as-is (already generic over sourceType) тАФ no new backend endpoints are needed for a mobile client, only new UI.
8. Preserve the defensive re-verification after insert on the create endpoint, and the "smart toast" tiering on the client тАФ both are deliberate reliability/engagement decisions, not incidental.

---

### 10.1 Calorie burn estimation
Defined in `server/lib/energy.ts`.

#### Core MET formula (`kcalFromMET`)
```
kcal/min = MET ├Ч 3.5 ├Ч bodyWeightKg / 200
sessionKcal = kcal/min ├Ч durationMinutes
```
Returns 0 if any input is zero or negative.

#### Strength training METs (`getStrengthMET`)
Used when no MET value comes from the activity catalog:
```
light    тЖТ 3.5
moderate тЖТ 5.0  тЖР default when intensity is null/unknown
vigorous тЖТ 6.0
```

#### Session calorie calculator (`calculateSessionCalories`)
```typescript
calculateSessionCalories(
  weightKg: number,
  input: {
    durationMinutes?: number | null,
    intensity?: string | null,
    sets?: Array<{ restSeconds?: number | null }>,
    activities?: Array<{ metValue: number; durationMinutes: number }>
  }
): { totalKcal, strengthKcal, activityKcal, estimatedMinutes }
```
- If `durationMinutes` is not provided but `sets` are, duration is **estimated from sets** (see below)
- Strength kcal = `kcalFromMET(strengthMET, weight, strengthMinutes)`
- Activity/cardio kcal = sum of `kcalFromMET(activity.metValue, weight, activity.durationMinutes)` for each activity
- `totalKcal = strengthKcal + activityKcal` (rounded)

#### Duration estimation from sets (`estimateDurationFromSets`)
When `durationMinutes` is absent and sets are available:
```
avgRestSeconds = mean of provided restSeconds values,
                 or 90s default if none provided
totalSeconds   = setCount ├Ч (35s per set + avgRestSeconds)
estimatedMinutes = ceil(totalSeconds / 60)
```
Default timing constants:
- `avgSetTimeSeconds = 35`
- `defaultRestSeconds = 90`

#### RPE adjustment for cardio (`getRpeKcalAdjustmentFactor`)
Applied **only to cardio** activities when the user logs an RPE value:
```
factor = 0.9 + (clamp(rpe, 1, 10) / 10) ├Ч 0.2
  RPE 1  тЖТ ├Ч0.92
  RPE 5  тЖТ ├Ч1.00
  RPE 10 тЖТ ├Ч1.10
finalKcal = baseKcal ├Ч factor
```
**Not applied to lifting** тАФ lifting uses `estimateLiftingCalories()` which has its own RPE model.  
**Not applied to leisure/recovery activities** тАФ these are excluded by name:

```
Excluded keywords (if activity name contains any of these, no RPE adjustment):
"leisure", "easy", "recovery", "warmup", "warm-up", "warm up",
"cooldown", "cool-down", "cool down", "mobility", "stretch",
"stretching", "gentle", "casual", "walking", "walk"
```

`shouldApplyRpeKcalAdjustment(activityName, activityType)` returns `false` for `activityType === "lifting"` or any name matching the exclusion list.

#### Lifting calorie estimation (`estimateLiftingCalories`)
Separate model used for `activityType === "lifting"` entries in `session_activities`:
```typescript
estimateLiftingCalories({
  bodyRegion: 'upper' | 'lower' | 'full',
  durationMinutes: number,
  rpe: number,       // 1тАУ10
  bodyWeightKg: number
}): number
```
METs by body region:
```
lower тЖТ 5.5
full  тЖТ 5.0
upper тЖТ 4.5
```
RPE is baked into this model directly (not via the cardio RPE factor).

#### kcal-per-rep display (`estimateKcalPerRep`)
```typescript
estimateKcalPerRep(totalKcal: number, totalReps: number): number | null
// Returns null if either input is 0; otherwise rounds to 1 decimal
// Purely a rough reference for the user тАФ not medically accurate
```

### 10.2 Training Load System тАФ complete specification

Source file: `server/lib/training-load.ts`

This system turns raw training data (RPE, duration, body region) into a daily load score, classifies it against a personalised baseline, generates natural-language warnings, and surfaces them both as an inline card on the training page and as a modal dialog.

---

#### 10.2.1 Per-activity load score тАФ `computeSessionLoad()`

Every activity in a session contributes a load score:

```
if rpe is present:
  activityLoad = rpe ├Ч durationMinutes

else (no RPE тАФ e.g. machine cardio with auto-kcal):
  activityLoad = estimatedKcal  (used as a proxy)
```

A session's contribution is the **sum** of all its activities' load scores.

**Lifting-specific load (for display on activity card, not used in ACWR):**
```
trainingLoadScore = durationMinutes ├Ч sessionRpe ├Ч bodyRegionMultiplier

bodyRegionMultiplier:
  upper тЖТ 1.0
  lower тЖТ 1.25
  full  тЖТ 1.1
```

---

#### 10.2.2 Day total тАФ `computeDailyLoad()`

Sums `computeSessionLoad()` across all activities for the day.

```typescript
{
  totalLoad:            number      // sum of all activity load scores
  classification:       DayClassification
  provisional:          boolean     // true if it's still today (partial data) or sessions exist but no activities
  sessionCount:         number
  totalDurationMinutes: number
  totalKcal:            number
}
```

**Day classification thresholds тАФ `classifyDayLoad()`**

| `totalLoad` (RPE ├Ч minutes) | Classification |
|---|---|
| < 300 | `"light"` |
| 300тАУ599 | `"moderate"` |
| 600тАУ899 | `"hard"` |
| тЙе 900 | `"very_hard"` |

---

#### 10.2.3 ACWR + warning engine тАФ `computeLoadWarnings()`

Takes today's `DailyLoadResult` and an array of prior days (newest-first).

**Step 1 тАФ Acute load (last 7 days)**
```
acuteLoad  = ╬г totalLoad for [today, yesterday, тАж, 6 days ago]
acuteDaily = Math.round((acuteLoad / 7) ├Ч 10) / 10
```

**Step 2 тАФ Active day count**
```
activeDaysInWindow = count of days where totalLoad > 0 across all days in the window
insufficientHistory = activeDaysInWindow < 7
```
When `insufficientHistory` is `true`, ACWR and `relativeLoad` are **both forced to `null`** тАФ a baseline built mostly from zero-load rest days would produce spurious high ratios for new users.

**Step 3 тАФ Baseline (28 тЖТ 14 тЖТ 7 fallback chain)**
```
for n in [28, 14, 7]:
  if totalDaysAvailable >= n:
    baselineLoad    = Math.round((╬г totalLoad[0..n] / n) ├Ч 10) / 10
    baselineDaysUsed = n
    break
```

**Step 4 тАФ ACWR**
```
if !insufficientHistory AND baselineLoad > 0:
  acwr = Math.round((acuteDaily / baselineLoad) ├Ч 100) / 100
else:
  acwr = null
```

**Step 5 тАФ Relative load (today vs baseline)**
```
if !insufficientHistory AND baselineLoad > 0:
  relativeLoad = Math.round((todayLoad / baselineLoad) ├Ч 100) / 100
else:
  relativeLoad = null
```

**Step 6 тАФ Stress flags**

Per-day high-stress determination (`isHighStress()`):
```
if relativeLoad is not null:  high = relativeLoad > 1.2
else (no baseline):           high = totalLoad >= 600
```

Very-high stress:
```
if relativeLoad is not null:  veryHigh = relativeLoad > 1.4
else:                         veryHigh = totalLoad >= 900
```

Stacking flags (uses today, yesterday, and 2-days-ago):
```
backToBackHardDays = todayHigh AND y1High
highLoadCluster    = 2+ of [today, y1, y2] are high-stress
threeDayStreak     = todayHigh AND y1High AND y2High
```

**Step 7 тАФ loadStatus**
```
if acwr === null:  loadStatus = null
elif acwr < 0.8:  loadStatus = "low"
elif acwr <= 1.5: loadStatus = "stable"
else:             loadStatus = "spike"
```

**Step 8 тАФ Warning text generation**

Up to 2 warnings are generated. Priority order: spike/elevated first, stacking second.

```
Condition                        Warning text
тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФА
acwr > 1.5                       "Today's load is well above your recent baseline.
                                  Consider keeping the next session lighter or
                                  prioritising recovery."

relativeLoad > 1.3               "Today's load is above your recent baseline.
(and acwr тЙд 1.5 or acwr null)    A lighter follow-up session or extra recovery
                                  may help."

threeDayStreak = true            "Training stress has been building across the
                                  last 3 days. It may help to reduce intensity
                                  or include a lighter day."

highLoadCluster = true           "Training stress is accumulating across recent
(and not threeDayStreak)         days. Recovery needs may be higher than usual
                                  over the next 24тАУ48 hours."
```

Final list is capped at `warnings.slice(0, 2)`.

---

#### 10.2.4 ACWR risk bands (displayed in `/load-trend`)

| ACWR value | Label | UI colour |
|---|---|---|
| `null` | "No baseline yet" | `text-muted-foreground` |
| < 0.8 | "Under-trained (< 0.8)" | `text-blue-400` |
| 0.8тАУ1.3 | "Optimal zone (0.8тАУ1.3)" | `text-green-400` |
| 1.3тАУ1.5 | "Elevated risk (1.3тАУ1.5)" | `text-yellow-400` |
| > 1.5 | "High risk spike (> 1.5)" | `text-red-400` |

---

#### 10.2.5 `LoadWarningResult` тАФ full returned shape

```typescript
{
  warnings:            string[]         // 0тАУ2 natural-language warning strings
  backToBackHardDays:  boolean
  highLoadCluster:     boolean
  threeDayStreak:      boolean
  acuteLoad:           number           // 7-day sum
  acuteDaily:          number           // acuteLoad / 7 (1dp)
  baselineLoad:        number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:    number | null    // 28, 14, or 7
  acwr:                number | null
  relativeLoad:        number | null    // today / baseline
  highStress:          boolean
  veryHighStress:      boolean
  chronicLoad:         number           // legacy alias for baselineLoad (0 when null)
  loadRatio:           number | null    // alias for acwr
  loadStatus:          "low"|"stable"|"spike"|null
  activeDaysInWindow:  number
  insufficientHistory: boolean
}
```

---

#### 10.2.6 `GET /api/me/training-load/:date` тАФ full response shape

Auth required. Fetches 28 days of history, applies any user override, then runs `computeLoadWarnings()`.

**Override logic:**
- If the user has saved an override for today (`light` or `moderate`), stress flags (`highStress`, `veryHighStress`) are forced false and stress-related warnings are stripped.
- Overrides for prior days are also respected тАФ `light`/`moderate` prior-day overrides feed corrected classifications back into stacking detection.

```typescript
{
  // From DailyLoadResult (today):
  totalLoad:             number
  classification:        "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"
  provisional:           boolean
  sessionCount:          number
  totalDurationMinutes:  number
  totalKcal:             number

  // Added by the route:
  date:                  string   // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  overrideClassification: string | null
  effectiveClassification: "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"  // override ?? classification

  // From LoadWarningResult (spread in):
  warnings:              string[]
  backToBackHardDays:    boolean
  highLoadCluster:       boolean
  threeDayStreak:        boolean
  acuteLoad:             number
  acuteDaily:            number
  baselineLoad:          number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:      number | null
  acwr:                  number | null
  relativeLoad:          number | null
  highStress:            boolean
  veryHighStress:        boolean
  loadStatus:            "low"|"stable"|"spike"|null
  activeDaysInWindow:    number
  insufficientHistory:   boolean
}
```

---

#### 10.2.7 `GET /api/me/training/load-history/:date` тАФ 28-day chart data

Auth required. Returns history in **chronological order** (oldest first) for chart rendering.

```typescript
{
  history: Array<{
    date:           string   // "YYYY-MM-DD"
    totalLoad:      number
    classification: "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"
    relativeLoad:   number | null   // day totalLoad / baselineLoad (null before 7 active days)
    sessionCount:   number
  }>,
  baselineLoad:      number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:  number | null
  acuteLoad:         number
  acuteDaily:        number
  acwr:              number | null
  date:              string   // the reference date used
}
```

---

#### 10.2.8 `POST /api/me/training/load-override/:date` тАФ save user classification

Auth required. Validated values: `"light"` | `"moderate"` | `"hard"` | `"very_hard"`.

```
Request:  { classification: string }
Response: { success: true, overrideClassification: string }
Error:    400 { message: "Invalid classification" }
```

The override is upserted in `training_load_overrides` table. On the next call to `GET /api/me/training-load/:date`, the `effectiveClassification` reflects it and stress warnings are conditionally suppressed.

---

#### 10.2.9 Frontend тАФ inline load insight on the Training page

The training page (`client/src/pages/training.tsx`) fetches load data on every date change:

```typescript
useQuery({
  queryKey: ["/api/me/training-load", selectedDate],
  queryFn: () => fetch(`/api/me/training-load/${selectedDate}`),
  staleTime: 0,   // always re-fetch on mount
})
```

**`dayLoad` useMemo derivation** тАФ determines the badge shown on the training date card:

1. If `trainingLoadData.effectiveClassification` is present тЖТ use it (respects overrides)
2. Otherwise fallback: compute locally from `sessions.activities` using the same thresholds

Badge colour mapping:
```
light       bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30
moderate    bg-yellow-500/15 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-500/30
hard        bg-orange-500/15 text-orange-400 border-orange-500/30
very_hard   bg-red-500/15 text-red-400 border-red-500/30
```

If the classification was user-overridden, an `(overridden)` note appears next to the badge.

**Inline warning banners:** When `trainingLoadData.warnings` has entries, each is shown below the classification badge as a small `text-orange-400/70` line with an `AlertTriangle` icon (`data-testid="text-load-warning-{i}"`).

**"28-day trend" link:** Always visible below the warnings. Navigates to `/load-trend`. `data-testid="button-view-load-trend"`.

---

#### 10.2.10 Frontend тАФ `checkAndShowLoadWarning()`

Called automatically after every successful mutation that changes training data:
- After adding a lifting set (`addSetMutation.onSuccess`)
- After adding a cardio/activity (`addActivityMutation.onSuccess`)
- After editing an activity (`editActivityMutation.onSuccess`)

```typescript
async function checkAndShowLoadWarning(date: string) {
  const data = await fetch(`/api/me/training-load/${date}`)
  if (data.warnings.length > 0) {
    _pendingLoadWarning = { analysis: data, date }
    setLoadWarningModal({ open: true, analysis: data })
  }
}
```

**`_pendingLoadWarning` тАФ module-level persistence:**  
Declared at module scope (outside the component), not in React state. This means it survives component unmounts (e.g. navigating away to the trend page and back). On component mount, the `useState` initialiser checks `_pendingLoadWarning` for today's date and re-opens the modal if it hasn't been acknowledged yet.

---

#### 10.2.11 Frontend тАФ `TrainingLoadWarningModal`

Component: `client/src/components/TrainingLoadWarningModal.tsx`  
`data-testid="modal-load-warning"`

**Trigger:** Shown when `loadWarningModal.open === true` (set by `checkAndShowLoadWarning`).

**Cannot be dismissed** by clicking outside or pressing Escape тАФ `onInteractOutside` and `onEscapeKeyDown` both call `e.preventDefault()`. The only way to close it is the "Continue" button.

**Layout тАФ three sections:**

1. **Metrics row** (3 equal columns):
   - Today тАФ `analysis.totalLoad` / "load pts"
   - Baseline тАФ `Math.round(analysis.baselineLoad)` / `{N}d avg` (or `"< 7 days"` if null)
   - ACWR тАФ `analysis.acwr.toFixed(2)` / "ratio" (or `"building baseline"` when `insufficientHistory`)

2. **Sparse history notice** (shown only when `analysis.insufficientHistory === true`):
   > "We're still building your training baseline. Until you have at least 7 training days logged, load insights use simple thresholds."

3. **System estimate badge** тАФ `effectiveClassification` displayed with colour coding:
   ```
   light       bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30
   moderate    bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-500/30
   hard        bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400 border-orange-500/30
   very_hard   bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border-red-500/30
   ```

4. **Warning list** тАФ each warning in a `bg-yellow-500/5 border-yellow-500/20` container. Icon logic:
   - Warning text contains "spike" тЖТ `TrendingUp` in `text-red-400`
   - Warning text contains "elevated" тЖТ `TrendingUp` in `text-orange-400`
   - Otherwise тЖТ `AlertTriangle` in `text-yellow-400`
   - `data-testid="load-warning-{i}"`

5. **Override select** (`data-testid="select-load-override"`):
   ```
   Options:  "Use system estimate" (value="keep") | "Light day" | "Moderate day" | "Hard day" | "Very hard day"
   ```
   When a non-`keep` value is selected, a hint appears: *"Your rating will be saved for this day and used to reduce unnecessary warnings."*

6. **No-baseline notice** (when `analysis.baselineLoad === null`):
   > "You have fewer than 7 days of data. Thresholds are based on absolute load until your baseline is established."

**Actions:**

- **"Continue"** (`data-testid="button-load-acknowledge"`) тАФ if an override was chosen, calls `POST /api/me/training/load-override/{date}` first, then clears `_pendingLoadWarning` and closes the modal.
- **"View 28-day load trend"** (`data-testid="button-view-load-trend"`) тАФ navigates to `/load-trend` **without** closing or acknowledging the modal. The modal re-opens when the user navigates back because `_pendingLoadWarning` is still set.

---

#### 10.2.12 Frontend тАФ Load Trend page (`/load-trend`)

Route: `client/src/pages/load-trend.tsx`  
Data: `GET /api/me/training/load-history/{today}`

**4 summary stat cards:**

| Card label | Value | Sub-label |
|---|---|---|
| ACWR | `data.acwr.toFixed(2)` or `"тАФ"` | ACWR status label (see ┬з10.2.4) |
| Baseline | `Math.round(data.baselineLoad)` or `"тАФ"` | `"{N}-day avg"` or `"< 7 days data"` |
| Acute (7d) | `data.acuteLoad` | `"{data.acuteDaily.toFixed(0)}/day avg"` |
| High-stress | count of days where `relativeLoad > 1.2` (or `totalLoad >= 600` if no baseline) | `"of {trainingDays} training days"` |

**Chart 1 тАФ Absolute Load** (always shown):
- Type: `ComposedChart` with a single `Bar` series (`dataKey="totalLoad"`)
- X-axis: `date`, formatted `"d MMM"`, tick interval 6
- Y-axis: raw load units
- Reference lines (dashed):
  - `y=300` тАФ green `#22c55e` (light/moderate boundary)
  - `y=600` тАФ orange `#f97316` (moderate/hard boundary)
  - `y=900` тАФ red `#ef4444` (hard/very_hard boundary)
  - `y=baselineLoad` тАФ primary colour, labelled `"baseline"` (only when baselineLoad is set)
- Bar fill: `hsl(var(--primary))` at `opacity=0.75`, corner radius `[2,2,0,0]`

**Chart 2 тАФ Relative Load** (only shown when at least one entry has `relativeLoad !== null`):
- Type: `ComposedChart` with a single `Bar` series (`dataKey="relativeLoad"`)
- Y-axis: formatted with `├Ч` suffix
- Reference lines:
  - `y=1.0` тАФ muted, dashed (baseline = 1)
  - `y=1.2` тАФ yellow `#eab308`, labelled `"high stress"`
  - `y=1.4` тАФ red `#ef4444`, labelled `"very high"`
- Sub-note: *"1.0 = exactly at baseline ┬╖ >1.2 high stress ┬╖ >1.4 very high stress"*

**Custom tooltip** тАФ shown on bar hover:
```
Date (formatted "EEE d MMM")
Load      {totalLoad}
Relative  {relativeLoad.toFixed(2)}├Ч   (if not null)
Class     {classification}             (coloured)
Sessions  {sessionCount}               (if > 0)
```

**ACWR education card** (always at the bottom):
> "The Acute:Chronic Workload Ratio (ACWR) compares your 7-day average load to your baseline. Research suggests the 'sweet spot' is **0.8тАУ1.3** тАФ below this suggests detraining, above 1.5 indicates injury risk elevation."
> "Baseline window: 28 days тЖТ 14 days тЖТ 7 days as your history builds."
> Citation: *Gabbett, T.J. (2016). British Journal of Sports Medicine, 50(5), 273тАУ280.*

---

#### 10.2.13 Classification colour reference (all UI contexts)

| Classification | Badge text | Bar colour | Badge CSS classes |
|---|---|---|---|
| `light` | Light | `#22c55e` | `bg-green-500/20 text-green-400` |
| `moderate` | Moderate | `#eab308` | `bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400` |
| `hard` | Hard | `#f97316` | `bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400` |
| `very_hard` | Very Hard | `#ef4444` | `bg-red-500/20 text-red-400` |

Note: the training page day-badge uses slightly different opacity variants (`/15` background, `/30` border) while the modal uses `/20` background, `/30` border.

### 10.3 `computeLoadWarnings()` тАФ see ┬з10.2.3 above

## 11. Food Logging System

### 11.1 Entry sources
1. **Manual** тАФ user types macros directly
2. **Core Foods Quick-Add** тАФ pre-curated list of common meals (see ┬з12)
3. **Open Food Facts search** тАФ barcode or text search via `/api/foods/search`
4. **Barcode scan** тАФ html5-qrcode тЖТ `/api/food/barcode/:code`
5. **Saved Meals (templates)** тАФ one-tap log of a saved meal template
6. **Copy from another day** тАФ `/api/me/meals/copy`
7. **AI Quick Log** тАФ natural language тЖТ `AILogDialog.tsx`

### 11.2 Raw vs cooked weight
Each entry has `enteredBasis: 'raw'|'cooked'` and `isRawWeight: boolean`.  
The server applies a **cook-factor conversion** to standardise all entries to cooked weight before calculating macros/micros.  
Typical factors (stored in `ingredients.json`): rice rawтЖТcooked тЙИ 0.4, chicken rawтЖТcooked тЙИ 0.75.

### 11.3 Micronutrient resolution chain

`getFoodMicrosForDate()` in `server/lib/micros.ts` processes each food entry in this priority order:

**Step 1 тАФ Composite food name match (highest priority)**  
Check `entry.name.toLowerCase().trim()` against the `COMPOSITE_FOODS` map (see ┬з13).  
If matched:
- Scale each component's gram weight by `loggedGrams / referenceServing`
- Look up each component in `ingredients.json` by case-insensitive name
- Sum `(micro_per_100g ├Ч componentGrams) / 100` for each of the 17 `MICRO_KEYS`
- This path is followed for **all** core food quick-add entries

**Step 2 тАФ OFF entry with ingredient mapping**  
If `entry.sourceType === "off"` AND `entry.microSource === "ingredient"` AND `entry.ingredientIndex` is a valid number:
- Look up `ingredients[ingredientIndex]` directly (by array position, not name)
- Sum `(micro_per_100g ├Ч entryGrams) / 100`
- This path is followed when the user has mapped a scanned barcode to an ingredient

**Step 3 тАФ Manual entry name fallback**  
If `entry.sourceType !== "off"`:
- Case-insensitive name search in `ingredients.json` (`i.name.toLowerCase() === entry.name.toLowerCase()`)
- If matched, use that ingredient's micros
- Allows whole-food manual entries (e.g. "Chicken breast") to get micros automatically

**Step 4 тАФ No micros**  
OFF entries without a valid mapping (`microSource !== "ingredient"`) are skipped entirely тАФ they contribute zero to AMQS.

#### Micro key lookup helper (`getMicronutrientValue`)
```typescript
// From shared/utils.ts
getMicronutrientValue(ingredient, `${key}_per_100g`)
// Returns null if the key doesn't exist on the ingredient object
```

#### How core foods map to scanned/OFF foods
Core food quick-adds work via **name-based composite matching** (Step 1 above) тАФ no `ingredientIndex` is needed.  
When a user scans a barcode for a product that is similar to a core food (e.g., a branded porridge), the barcode flow runs separately and the user can map it to an ingredient via `/api/food/barcode/:code/map`. The mapping writes `ingredientIndex` and `microSource: "ingredient"` to the `food_entries` row, enabling Step 2 on future lookups.

### 11.4 Barcode flow
1. Client sends barcode to `/api/food/barcode/:code`
2. Server checks `off_product_mappings` for existing mapping
3. If not found тЖТ fetches from Open Food Facts API
4. If found with high-confidence match тЖТ returns ingredient micros automatically
5. If low confidence тЖТ client shows "map to ingredient" UI for the user to pick
6. User selection saved via `/api/food/barcode/:code/map`

### 11.5 Meal sections
Meals: `breakfast`, `lunch`, `dinner`, `snack`  
Snacks are numbered with `snackIndex` (0, 1, 2тАж) to support multiple snack slots.

### 11.6 Macro warnings
Visual warnings appear when logged macros exceed targets by >10%.

---

## 11.7 Quick Log тАФ AI-Assisted Natural Language Logging

Quick Log lets the user describe what they've done in plain English. The parser classifies the text client-side, shows a confirmation screen, and only writes to the database after the user taps a confirm button. **Nothing is saved during parsing.**

---

### 11.7.1 Entry point тАФ dashboard header button

**Location:** Dashboard header action bar, alongside "Add Food", "Log Weight", and "Log Macros".

```tsx
<Button
  variant="outline"
  size="default"
  onClick={() => setAiLogOpen(true)}
  data-testid="button-ai-log"
>
  <Sparkles className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
  Quick Log
</Button>
```

`AILogDialog` is mounted once at the top of the dashboard `return()`:

```tsx
<AILogDialog
  open={aiLogOpen}
  onOpenChange={setAiLogOpen}
  date={selectedDate}
  onSuccess={() => setAiLogOpen(false)}
/>
```

---

### 11.7.2 Dialog structure тАФ 4 states

**File:** `client/src/components/AILogDialog.tsx`

```
DialogState = "input" | "review" | "saving" | "done"
```

| State | What the user sees |
|---|---|
| `input` | Textarea + optional mic icon + "Review" button |
| `review` | Intent-specific confirmation card with editable fields |
| `saving` | Confirm button shows spinner (mutation pending) |
| `done` | Success screen with "Log another" button |

**Dialog container:** `sm:max-w-md`  
**Title:** Sparkles icon + `"Quick Log"` (font-display)

---

### 11.7.3 Input state UI

```
DialogHeader: Sparkles icon + "Quick Log"

Description (text-xs text-muted-foreground):
  "Describe what you want to log in plain language.
   You'll review everything before it's saved."

Textarea (relative wrapper):
  value={inputText}
  placeholder: "e.g. '2 eggs and toast for breakfast' ┬╖
                'Morning weight 71.8' ┬╖ 'Pads 60 min at 7pm'"
  className="pr-10 resize-none min-h-[80px]"
  data-testid="ai-log-input"
  onKeyDown: Cmd/Ctrl+Enter тЖТ handleParse()
  
  [Mic button] (absolute right-2 top-2, only if SpeechRecognition supported):
    idle:      Mic icon, text-muted-foreground
    listening: MicOff icon, text-red-400 bg-red-500/10
    data-testid="ai-mic-button"

[If isListening]:
  "тЧП Listening тАФ speak naturally, stops after 3s silence"  (text-red-400)
  interim text shown as italic muted text

Button row:
  [Review] flex-1, disabled when inputText.trim() empty
    <Edit2 /> Review
    data-testid="ai-parse-button"
  [Cancel] variant=ghost тЖТ onOpenChange(false)

Footer (text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-center opacity-60):
  "Cmd/Ctrl+Enter to review ┬╖ Nothing is saved until you confirm"
```

---

### 11.7.4 Parser тАФ `client/src/lib/aiLogParser.ts`

ЁЯТ╗ **CLIENT-SIDE ONLY.** No network requests made during parsing.

#### Pipeline

```
1. Normalise input (lowercase, trim)
2. Score all 5 intents using keyword banks + regex
3. Pick highest-scoring intent (minimum score: 2)
4. Sub-parse to extract structured entities
5. Return typed ParseResult with requiresConfirmation: true
```

#### Intent priority order (scored simultaneously, highest wins)

| Intent | Trigger condition |
|---|---|
| `create_recurring_training_schedule` | `"every [weekday]"` pattern |
| `log_weight` | Weight trigger phrase (`"weight"`, `"weigh"`, `"bw"`) + numeric extraction |
| `log_training_session` | Activity keyword match (from `TRAINING_ACTIVITY_KEYWORDS`) |
| `log_supplements` | Supplement keyword match + optionally a "taken/took" verb |
| `log_food` | Meal keyword / food trigger phrase + extractable food items |
| `unknown` | No intent scores тЙе 2 |

#### Scoring functions

| Intent | Key signals | Score examples |
|---|---|---|
| recurring | `every [day]` pattern | +4; matching training keyword +1 |
| weight | weight trigger phrase | +3; extracted numeric weight +4 |
| training | activity keyword | +3; duration present +2; time of day +1 |
| supplements | per keyword match | +2 each; taken/took verb +2 |
| food | food trigger phrase | +2; meal keyword +2; each food item +2 (max +6) |

#### Intent types and ParseResult shapes

```typescript
// All intents share these base fields:
// requiresConfirmation: true (always)
// rawInput: string
// confidence: "high" | "medium" | "low"
// missingFields: string[]

ParsedFood: {
  intent: "log_food";
  meal: "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack";
  items: FoodItem[];  // { rawText, normalizedName, count?, sizeHint?, gramsHint? }
}

ParsedWeight: {
  intent: "log_weight";
  weightKg: number;  // auto-converts lbs тЖТ kg
}

ParsedTraining: {
  intent: "log_training_session";
  activityName: string;   // canonical catalog name (from ACTIVITY_CANONICAL_NAME map)
  durationMinutes: number; // defaults 60 if not detected
  timeOfDay: "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening";
  timeLabel?: string;       // e.g. "7pm"
}

ParsedSupplements: {
  intent: "log_supplements";
  items: string[];   // matched supplement display names (title-cased)
}

ParsedRecurring: {
  intent: "create_recurring_training_schedule";
  dayOfWeek: string;   // full day name e.g. "Tuesday"
  scope?: "fight camp" | "general";
  sessions: RecurringSession[];
}

ParsedUnknown: {
  intent: "unknown";
  clarificationHint: string;
}
```

#### Confidence levels

| Level | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `high` | Multiple strong signals (meal keyword + food items, or weight trigger + number) |
| `medium` | Single strong signal or ambiguous detection |
| `low` | Parser uncertain |

Displayed as a coloured `<Badge>` in the review card:
- `high` тЖТ emerald (`bg-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-400`)
- `medium` тЖТ yellow
- `low` тЖТ red

#### Ingredient matching (food intent only)

After parsing, `AILogDialog` fuzzy-matches each `FoodItem.normalizedName` against `GET /api/ingredients` (loaded once, `staleTime: 5min`). The matching algorithm (`matchIngredient`):

1. Exact name match тЖТ score 100
2. Name starts with query тЖТ 80
3. Name contains query тЖТ 60
4. Query contains name тЖТ 50
5. Word-by-word overlap (тЙе3 chars) тЖТ 15 per overlapping word

Macros calculated: `Math.round(nutrient_per_100g ├Ч grams / 100)`

Gram resolution order:
1. Explicit `gramsHint` from parser (e.g. "100g of chicken")
2. `count ├Ч coreFoodUnit` grams (from `coreFoodUnits.ts`)
3. `count ├Ч 100`
4. Default: 100g

#### Activity canonicalisation

The parser maps raw activity keywords to catalog-search terms before hitting `/api/activities`:

```
"pads"   тЖТ "Muay Thai"
"bjj"    тЖТ "Judo/Jiu-Jitsu"
"lifting"тЖТ "Strength Training"
"run"    тЖТ "Running (moderate)"
// etc. (full map in ACTIVITY_CANONICAL_NAME in aiLogParser.ts)
```

---

### 11.7.5 Review state тАФ 6 intent-specific cards

#### 1. Food review card (`log_food`)

```
Meal badge (capitalize) + ConfidenceBadge
"Log this meal?"

Per-item rows (space-y-2):
  div className="flex items-start gap-3 rounded-lg border p-3 text-sm"
    [toggle button] data-testid="ai-food-toggle-{i}"
      confirmed тЖТ CheckCircle2 (text-emerald-400)
      rejected  тЖТ XCircle (text-muted-foreground)
    [item details]:
      if matched тЖТ ingredient name + inline grams input + macros
        grams input: className="w-14 bg-secondary/50 rounded px-1 py-0.5 text-xs text-center font-mono"
                     data-testid="ai-food-grams-{i}"
                     onChange тЖТ recalculates macros live
        macro display: "{grams}g  {kcal} kcal  {P}g P  {C}g C  {F}g F"
      if unmatched тЖТ italic muted "Unrecognised: "{name}" тАФ deselected"
  
  [if unmatched items exist]:
    "{n} item(s) not matched to the ingredient list тАФ they will be skipped.
     Use "Add Food" to log them manually."

  [if confirmed items > 0]:
    totals bar: "Total: {kcal} kcal  {P}g protein"  (bg-secondary/40)

  [Log {n} item(s)] data-testid="ai-confirm-food"   disabled: confirmed=0 || saving
  [тЖР Edit]          data-testid="ai-edit-back"       тЖТ setDialogState("input")
```

On confirm: `POST /api/food` for each confirmed+matched item with:
```json
{
  "date": "...",
  "name": "{ingredient.name}",
  "grams": {grams},
  "calories": {n}, "protein": {n}, "carbs": {n}, "fat": {n}, "fibre": {n},
  "meal": "{meal}",
  "sourceType": "ingredient",
  "ingredientIndex": {n},
  "macroSource": "ingredient",
  "microSource": "ingredient"
}
```
Cache invalidated: `["/api/me/food/{date}"]`, `["/api/me/amqs/score"]`

#### 2. Weight review card (`log_weight`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Log morning weight?"

Row (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3):

  input step=0.1 min=30 max=250  data-testid="ai-weight-input"

[тЖР Edit]  data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

On confirm: `POST /api/weights` with `{ date, weight: weightValue }`  
Cache invalidated: `weights/range`, `weight-cut`, `targets/effective`, `morning-status`

#### 3. Training review card (`log_training_session`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Log this training session?"

Card (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3 space-y-3):
  Activity:  inline text input  data-testid="ai-training-activity"
             onChange тЖТ also updates activitySearchQ for catalog suggestions
  
  [Activity suggestions] (if activitySearchQ тЙе 2 chars):
    Fetches GET /api/activities?query={q}   staleTime 60s
    Shows up to 5 pill-buttons  data-testid="activity-suggestion-{id}"
    Click тЖТ sets activityName, clears search
  
  Duration:  number input (min=1)  data-testid="ai-training-duration"  + "min"

[If duration not detected]: yellow warning "Duration was not detected тАФ defaulted to 60 min."

[Log Session] data-testid="ai-confirm-training"   disabled: !activityName || saving
[тЖР Edit]      data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

On confirm, 3 sequential API calls:
1. `POST /api/workouts/sessions` тЖТ `{ date, timeOfDay, title: activityName, intensity: "moderate" }`
2. `GET /api/activities?query={activityName}` тЖТ find best-match MET value
3. `POST /api/workouts/sessions/{id}/activities` тЖТ `{ name, durationMinutes, intensity: "moderate", activityType: "cardio", metValue: bestActivity.metValue ?? 6, activityCatalogId }`

Cache invalidated: `workouts/sessions`, `training/summary`, `targets/effective`

#### 4. Supplements review card (`log_supplements`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Mark as taken?"

Per-supplement rows:
  [toggle] data-testid="ai-supp-toggle-{i}"
  Raw name (user input)
  if matched:   "тЖТ {supplement.name}" (text-muted-foreground)
  if unmatched: "Not found in your supplements тАФ will be skipped" (text-yellow-400)

[If no matches]:
  "None of the named supplements matched your saved list.
   Add them in the Supplements section first, then log them here."

[Mark Taken] data-testid="ai-confirm-supplements"  disabled: !hasMatches || saving
[тЖР Edit]     data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

Supplement matching uses `GET /api/me/supplements` (loaded when dialog opens). The `matchSupplement` function uses the same fuzzy scoring as ingredient matching.

On confirm: `POST /api/supplement-intakes` for each matched+included item:
```json
{ "supplementId": {id}, "stackId": {id | null}, "date": "...", "taken": true }
```
Cache invalidated: `["/api/me/supplement-intakes/{date}"]`

#### 5. Recurring training card (`create_recurring_training_schedule`)

```
ConfidenceBadge  +  optional "Fight Camp" badge (if scope = "fight camp")
"Create {dayOfWeek} sessions?"

Notice (text-xs text-muted-foreground):
  "V1: This will create sessions for the next {dayOfWeek} ({formatted date}) only.
   Full recurring scheduling can be set up in the Training Log."

Per-session cards (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3):
  Activity name
  timeLabel (if present) ┬╖ timeOfDay ┬╖ {durationMinutes} min

[Create Next {dayOfWeek}] data-testid="ai-confirm-recurring"  disabled: saving
[тЖР Edit]                  data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

Date target: `getNextDayDate(dayOfWeek)` тАФ finds the next occurrence of that weekday (always тЙе 1 day ahead).

On confirm: for each session, same 3-step sequence as single training (POST session тЖТ lookup activity тЖТ POST activity).

#### 6. Unknown intent card

```
Yellow warning box:
  "Not sure what to log"
  {clarificationHint}

Suggestion list:
  "2 eggs and 2 slices of toast for breakfast"
  "Morning weight 71.8"
  "Pads for 60 min at 7pm"
  "Creatine and Vitamin D taken"

[тЖР Try again] data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

---

### 11.7.6 Done state

```
CheckCircle2 (h-12 w-12 text-emerald-400)
"Logged successfully"

[Log another] variant=outline  data-testid="ai-log-another"
  тЖТ resets dialogState, inputText, parsed  + calls onSuccess()
```

### 11.7.7 Voice input (Web Speech API)

Microphone button only renders when `window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition` is truthy.

```
recognition.lang = "en-GB"
recognition.continuous = true
recognition.interimResults = true
recognition.maxAlternatives = 1
```

Silence timer: 3 000 ms (`SILENCE_TIMEOUT_MS`). Resets on every `onresult` event. When it fires, `stopListening()` is called.

Final transcript chunks are **appended** to `inputText` (space-separated). Interim transcript is shown below the textarea as italic text while the user speaks.

## 13. Composite Food Micronutrient Map

Defined in `server/lib/micros.ts` as `COMPOSITE_FOODS`.

**How it works:**
1. The entry name is lowercased and trimmed, then matched as a key in this map
2. Each component references an ingredient by **exact name** in `ingredients.json` (case-insensitive match)
3. Component gram weights are **per reference serving** тАФ they are scaled proportionally if the user logged a different gram amount: `componentGrams ├Ч (loggedGrams / referenceServing)`
4. Only ingredients that have tracked micros contribute тАФ coffee/espresso is **intentionally omitted** from all coffee drinks because it contains negligible amounts of the 17 tracked nutrients

> тЪая╕П The ingredient names below are the exact strings that must exist in `ingredients.json`. If you rename any ingredient, the composite lookup silently fails (a `validateCompositeIngredients()` startup check warns in console if any are missing).

| Core Food (matched lowercase) | Ref. Serving | Components (ingredient name in ingredients.json тЖТ grams) |
|---|---|---|
| porridge (oats + milk) | 250 g | `Oats (Raw)` тЖТ 40 g ┬╖ `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 200 g |
| porridge (oats + water) | 250 g | `Oats (Raw)` тЖТ 45 g |
| cappuccino (whole milk) | 240 g | `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 120 g *(espresso omitted тАФ no tracked micros)* |
| latte (whole milk) | 350 g | `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 200 g |
| flat white | 200 g | `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 130 g |
| cappuccino (oat milk) | 240 g | `Oat Milk` тЖТ 120 g |
| toast with butter (white) | 45 g | `Bread (White Sliced)` тЖТ 30 g ┬╖ `Butter` тЖТ 10 g |
| toast without butter (white) | 30 g | `Bread (White Sliced)` тЖТ 30 g |
| toast with butter (wholemeal) | 50 g | `Bread (Wholemeal)` тЖТ 36 g ┬╖ `Butter` тЖТ 10 g |
| mashed potato | 200 g | `Potatoes (Boiled)` тЖТ 180 g ┬╖ `Butter` тЖТ 10 g ┬╖ `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 20 g |
| scrambled eggs (2 eggs, butter) | 130 g | `Eggs, Whole (Raw)` тЖТ 100 g ┬╖ `Butter` тЖТ 10 g ┬╖ `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 20 g |
| overnight oats | 300 g | `Oats (Raw)` тЖТ 50 g ┬╖ `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 150 g ┬╖ `Greek Yogurt (Plain)` тЖТ 50 g |
| beans on toast | 260 g | `Baked Beans (Canned)` тЖТ 200 g ┬╖ `Bread (White Sliced)` тЖТ 60 g |
| greek yoghurt with honey | 170 g | `Greek Yogurt (Plain)` тЖТ 150 g ┬╖ `Honey` тЖТ 15 g |
| cereal with milk | 270 g | `Milk (Whole)` тЖТ 200 g *(cereal omitted тАФ highly variable, no single micro profile)* |

**Note on foods without a composite entry:**  
`Tuna Mayo Sandwich`, `Chicken Wrap`, `PB&J Sandwich`, and `Protein Shake` variants are in the Quick-Add list but **not** in `COMPOSITE_FOODS`. Entries with these names fall through to Step 3 of the resolution chain (manual name fallback against `ingredients.json`) and will only get micros if an exact-name match exists there.
