## 14. Supplement Tracker

### 14.1 User flow
1. User adds supplements to their "shelf" via the Add Supplement dialog (from catalog or as a custom entry)
2. Optionally groups supplements into stacks (see `/stacks` page)
3. Optionally enables a daily reminder time per supplement
4. Each day, logs intake (taken/skipped) via `supplement_intakes`
5. Micronutrients from **taken** supplements that have a `catalogId` are added to daily AMQS

### 14.2 AMQS micro integration

Only supplements with a `catalogId` (i.e. linked to the `supplement_catalog` table) contribute micronutrients. Custom supplements without a catalog link contribute zero micros.

`server/lib/micros.ts` aggregates supplement micros alongside food micros before AMQS scoring:
```
for each intake on the date where taken === true:
  catalog = supplement_catalog[supplement.catalogId]
  for each nutrient in catalog.microsPerUnit:
    totalMicros[nutrient] += supplement.doseAmount ├Ч catalog.microsPerUnit[nutrient]
```

This merged total (food micros + supplement micros) is what feeds `GET /api/me/amqs/micros/:date`.

**UI signal:** On the supplement shelf list, any supplement with a `catalogId` shows a `"AMQS tracked"` badge (default variant) and the sub-line: *"Contributing to your AMQS score"*.

### 14.3 Disclaimer gate for reminders
Before a supplement reminder can be enabled, the user must accept a disclaimer. This is checked via `GET /api/me/disclaimer/supplement_reminders` and accepted via `POST /api/me/disclaimer/supplement_reminders`. The disclaimer type string is `"supplement_reminders"`. The state is stored in `userDisclaimerAcceptance`.

### 14.4 Supplement form тАФ field options

**Form options (physical form of the supplement):**
```
"pill" | "capsule" | "powder" | "liquid" | "tablet" | "softgel" | "gummy" | "other"
```

**Dose units:**
```
"mcg" | "mg" | "g" | "IU" | "ml" | "serving" | "CFU"
```

**Reminder time default:** `"08:00"` (HH:MM string, input type="time")

### 14.5 Add Supplement dialog тАФ complete field spec

Opened by tapping the "Add Supplement" button (`data-testid="button-add-supplement"`).

Fields are **uncontrolled local state** тАФ not react-hook-form. Form is submitted via `onSubmit` handler.

**Field 1 тАФ Catalog selector** (`data-testid="select-catalog"`)
- Label: "Select from Catalog (optional)"
- Component: shadcn `Select`
- First option: `value="custom"` тЖТ "Custom Supplement"
- Remaining options: one `SelectItem` per catalog entry (`value=item.id.toString()`, label=`item.name`)
- **On catalog item selected:**
  - Sets `catalogId` state
  - Auto-fills `name` with `item.name`
  - Auto-fills `doseUnit` with `item.defaultUnit`
- **On "custom" selected:** clears `catalogId` and `doseUnit`
- **Catalog hint** (shown only when a catalog item is selected):
  - `bg-secondary/50 p-2 rounded` with `Info` icon
  - Text: `item.notes` if present, otherwise `"This supplement's micronutrients will be tracked for AMQS."`

**Field 2 тАФ Name** (`data-testid="input-supplement-name"`)
- Label: "Supplement Name *"
- Required тАФ submit is blocked if empty
- Placeholder: `"e.g., Vitamin D3"`

**Field 3 + 4 тАФ Dose (2-column grid)**
- Left: Dose Amount (`data-testid="input-dose-amount"`) тАФ `type="number"`, `step="any"`, placeholder `"e.g., 25"`
- Right: Dose Unit (`data-testid="select-dose-unit"`) тАФ shadcn Select, options from `DOSE_UNITS`

**Field 5 тАФ Brand** (`data-testid="input-supplement-brand"`)
- Label: "Brand (optional)"
- Placeholder: `"e.g., Nature Made"`

**Field 6 тАФ Form** (`data-testid="select-supplement-form"`)
- Label: "Form (optional)"
- shadcn Select, options from `FORM_OPTIONS`, all capitalized

**Field 7 тАФ Notes** (`data-testid="input-supplement-notes"`)
- Label: "Notes (optional)"
- shadcn `Textarea`, `resize-none`
- Placeholder: `"Any personal notes..."`

**Field 8 тАФ Daily Reminder toggle** (`data-testid="toggle-reminder-enabled"`)
- Custom toggle switch тАФ NOT a shadcn Switch
- `role="switch"`, `aria-checked={reminderEnabled}`
- Style when off: `bg-secondary`; style when on: `bg-primary`
- Thumb: `h-3.5 w-3.5` white circle, `translate-x-1` (off) тЖТ `translate-x-4` (on)
- When toggled on тЖТ shows a time input (`data-testid="input-reminder-time"`)
  - `type="time"`, default `"08:00"`
  - Only sent to server when `reminderEnabled === true`

**Submit button** (`data-testid="button-save-supplement"`)
- Label: "Add Supplement" / "Adding..." (pending)
- Disabled when `isPending` or name is empty

**POST body sent to `/api/supplements`:**
```typescript
{
  name:            string          // trimmed, required
  brand?:          string          // trimmed, omitted if empty
  form?:           string          // omitted if empty
  notes?:          string          // trimmed, omitted if empty
  catalogId?:      number          // omitted if custom (no catalogId)
  doseAmount?:     number          // parseFloat, omitted if empty
  doseUnit?:       string          // omitted if empty
  reminderEnabled: boolean
  reminderTime?:   string          // HH:MM, only if reminderEnabled === true
}
```

**On success:** invalidates `["/api/me/supplements"]`, `["/api/me/stacks/scheduled"]`, `["/api/me/amqs/score"]`, `["/api/me/amqs/score-range"]`. Closes dialog. Toast: "Supplement added".

### 14.6 Edit Supplement dialog

Opened by tapping the `Pencil` icon on a supplement row (`data-testid="button-edit-supplement-{id}"`). All fields pre-filled from the existing `Supplement` object.

Identical field layout to Add. Key differences:
- Title: "Edit Supplement"
- Submit button: "Save Changes" / "Saving..."
- Calls `PATCH /api/supplements/{id}`
- Catalog selector: when switching to "custom", does NOT clear the existing `doseUnit` (only sets `catalogId = null`)
- `doseAmount` sent as `null` (not omitted) when cleared; `doseUnit` sent as `null` when cleared; `reminderTime` sent as `null` when reminder disabled

**PATCH body:**
```typescript
{
  name?:            string
  brand?:           string
  form?:            string
  notes?:           string
  catalogId?:       number | null
  doseAmount?:      number | null
  doseUnit?:        string | null
  reminderEnabled?: boolean
  reminderTime?:    string | null
}
```

**On success:** invalidates same 4 query keys as Add. Closes dialog. Toast: "Supplement updated".

### 14.7 Delete supplement

Tapping the `Trash2` icon (`data-testid="button-delete-supplement-{id}"`) immediately fires `DELETE /api/supplements/{id}` тАФ no confirmation dialog. On success: invalidates same 4 query keys. Toast: "Supplement deleted".

### 14.8 Supplement shelf list item тАФ exact row layout

Each `motion.div` item in the `AnimatePresence` list:
```
animation: initial { opacity:0, y:10 } тЖТ animate { opacity:1, y:0 }
exit: { opacity:0, x:-20 }
transition: { duration: 0.2 }
className: "flex items-center justify-between p-4 rounded-lg border bg-secondary/30 group"
data-testid: "supplement-item-{supp.id}"
```

Left column (flex-1):
```
Row 1 (flex, items-center, gap-2, flex-wrap):
  <p className="font-medium">{supp.name}</p>
  IF doseAmount && doseUnit:
    <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px]">{doseAmount} {doseUnit}</Badge>
  IF form:
    <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-[10px] capitalize">{form}</Badge>
  IF catalogId:
    <Badge variant="default" className="text-[10px]">AMQS tracked</Badge>

Row 2 (conditional, shown when catalogId is set):
  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground/60 mt-0.5">Contributing to your AMQS score</p>

Row 3 (conditional, shown when reminderEnabled && reminderTime):
  <p className="text-xs text-primary/70 mt-0.5">тП░ Daily reminder at {reminderTime}</p>

Row 4 (brand + notes):
  IF brand: <span>{brand}</span>
  IF notes: <span className="block text-xs mt-1 italic">{notes}</span>
```

Right column (action buttons):
```
Pencil button: size="icon" variant="ghost"
  className includes "opacity-100 sm:opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
  data-testid="button-edit-supplement-{supp.id}"

Trash2 button: size="icon" variant="ghost"
  className includes "text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
  data-testid="button-delete-supplement-{supp.id}"
```

### 14.9 Supplement catalog (`GET /api/supplement-catalog`)

Returns all `SupplementCatalogItem[]`. Fetched with `staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000` (5 min) and `retry: 2`.

Each catalog item has:
```typescript
{
  id:           number
  name:         string
  defaultUnit:  string       // e.g. "mg", "mcg", "IU"
  notes:        string | null
  microsPerUnit: Record<string, number>  // keyed by MICRO_KEYS
}
```

When a catalog item is selected in the Add/Edit form:
1. `name` is auto-populated from `item.name`
2. `doseUnit` is auto-populated from `item.defaultUnit`
3. A hint box appears **immediately below the catalog selector**:
   - Style: `flex items-start gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-secondary/50 p-2 rounded`
   - `Info` icon (lucide, `h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 flex-shrink-0`)
   - Text: `item.notes` if the catalog item has notes, otherwise the fallback string `"This supplement's micronutrients will be tracked for AMQS."`
4. On save, `catalogId` is stored тЖТ enables `microsPerUnit ├Ч doseAmount` micro aggregation server-side

The hint is **only shown when a catalog item is actively selected** (not when "Custom Supplement" is selected or no selection has been made).

> **Catalog content is fully API-driven.** Call `GET /api/supplement-catalog` to get the live list тАФ names, `defaultUnit`, `notes`, and `microsPerUnit` are all returned. No hard-coding needed.

> **Fallback hint** (when `item.notes` is null): `"This supplement's micronutrients will be tracked for AMQS."`

Note: some catalog items have a non-empty `microsPerUnit` (e.g. Vitamin D3, Zinc, Omega-3) while others have an empty `{}` (e.g. Creatine, Vitamin K2). Both show the "AMQS tracked" badge on the shelf because they have a `catalogId`, but only items with non-empty `microsPerUnit` actually contribute to the AMQS score.

If catalog fails to load, a destructive card error is shown at the top of the page (but the form still works тАФ user can add a custom supplement without catalog).

---

## 15. Authentication System тАФ Full Reference

> **Do not re-implement any of the following.** Everything described here is already fully built in `server/auth.ts`, `server/auth-routes.ts`, and `server/invite-routes.ts`. The endpoint table in ┬з16.1 and ┬з16.2 lists every URL. This section explains the mechanics so a replicating agent understands what already exists.

---

### 15.1 Session configuration (`server/auth.ts` тЖТ `setupAuth()`)

Sessions are stored in PostgreSQL using `connect-pg-simple`. The table is named `session` and is created automatically if missing.

```
Store:   connect-pg-simple, conString = DATABASE_URL
Secret:  SESSION_SECRET env var (required in production; fatal crash if missing)
resave:  false
saveUninitialized: false
```

**Cookie settings:**
- `httpOnly: true`
- `sameSite: "lax"`
- `secure: true` in production, `false` in development
- `maxAge: 30 days` (browser) / `90 days` (PWA тАФ when `x-app-mode: standalone` request header is present)

The PWA session extension is done by a middleware that reads `req.headers["x-app-mode"]` on every authenticated request and adjusts `req.session.cookie.maxAge` in-place. No separate endpoint needed.

---

### 15.2 Passport.js тАФ local strategy (`server/auth.ts`)

- `usernameField: "identifier"` тАФ accepts either email or username in the same field
- Detection: if `identifier` contains `@` тЖТ treat as email lookup; otherwise username lookup
- Password hashing: **Argon2** (`argon2.hash` / `argon2.verify`). Not bcrypt. Never swap.
- Google-only accounts have `passwordHash = null`. Attempting a local login on such an account returns: `"This account uses Google login. Please sign in with Google."`
- `passport.serializeUser` stores only `user.id` (integer) in the session
- `passport.deserializeUser` re-fetches from `usersAuth` by id on every request
- `req.user` shape: `{ id: number, email: string, username: string }`

---

### 15.3 Google OAuth 2.0 (`server/auth.ts` + `server/routes.ts`)

**Environment variables required:** `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`, `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`
**Callback URL:** `GOOGLE_CALLBACK_URL` env var, or `${APP_BASE_URL}/auth/google/callback` as fallback.

If neither env var is set, the Google strategy is silently skipped тАФ local auth still works.

**Routes (no `/api` prefix):**
- `GET /auth/google` тЖТ captures optional `?src=` query param into `req.session.pendingSource`, then redirects to Google consent
- `GET /auth/google/callback` тЖТ on success: applies `pendingSource` as the user's `source` field (only if `source` is still `"google"`), then redirects to `/dashboard`; on failure: redirects to `/?error=google_auth_failed`

**Google strategy account-merge logic (in order):**
1. Look up `usersAuth` by the email returned from Google
2. If found and already a Google account with matching `providerUserId` тЖТ log in as-is
3. If found as a local account that is **not yet email-verified** тЖТ return error (user must verify email first)
4. If found as a verified local account тЖТ link: set `provider = "google"`, `providerUserId`, `emailVerified = true` on the existing row; log user in
5. If not found тЖТ create new `usersAuth` + `users` row. Username is derived from `profile.displayName`, lowercased, non-alphanumeric chars stripped, truncated to 16 chars; suffix `1`, `2` тАж appended until unique. New Google accounts are always `emailVerified = true`.

---

### 15.4 Email verification flow

- After `POST /api/auth/register`: server calls `createVerificationToken(authUser.id)` тЖТ sends a verification email via Resend (non-blocking, errors logged but don't fail the request). A welcome email is also sent.
- Token is stored hashed in a `verification_tokens` table (managed by `server/lib/verification-tokens.ts`).
- `GET /api/auth/verify-email?token=` is a server-side redirect handler. It calls `verifyToken(token)`, then:
  - On success тЖТ `302` to `/verify-email?success=1`
  - On failure тЖТ `302` to `/verify-email?error=<reason>` (reasons: `invalid`, `expired`, `server`)
- The client page `verify-email.tsx` reads the `?success` / `?error` query params and shows the appropriate message. No API call needed from the client.
- `POST /api/auth/resend-verification` (requires auth session, rate-limited 3 req / 15 min) тЖТ re-generates token and resends email.
- The `EmailVerificationBanner` component on the dashboard shows an orange top bar if `authUser.emailVerified === false`. It has a "Resend email" button that calls `/api/auth/resend-verification`.

---

### 15.5 Password reset flow

All three endpoints are public (no session required):

1. `POST /api/auth/forgot-password` тАФ body: `{ email }`. Always returns the same message regardless of whether the email exists (no user enumeration). Rate-limited: 5 req / 15 min. Server creates a reset token via `createPasswordResetToken(userId)` and sends a reset email via Resend.
2. The reset email contains a link to `/reset-password?token=<token>`.
3. `POST /api/auth/reset-password` тАФ body: `{ token, password }`. Password validation: min 8 chars, тЙе1 letter, тЙе1 digit. On success: updates `passwordHash` in `usersAuth`, invalidates the token. Returns `{ message }`.

Token helpers live in `server/lib/password-reset-tokens.ts`. Tokens are single-use and time-limited.

---

### 15.6 Invite-only beta system (`server/invite-routes.ts`)

**Tables involved:** `invite_requests`, `invites`, `beta_waitlist`

**Flow:**
1. User visits `/start`, enters their email, clicks "Request Invite"
2. `POST /api/invites/request` тЖТ checks beta cap (`BETA_USER_LIMIT` env var, checked against `COUNT(*)` of `usersAuth`). If full: adds email to `beta_waitlist`, returns 403. If space: generates a 10-char uppercase alphanumeric code (`generateCode()`), hashes it with SHA-256, inserts into `invites` with 7-day expiry, max 1 use. Sends invite email via Resend.
3. User receives email with code, returns to `/start` or `/signup`
4. `GET /api/invites/validate?token=` тЖТ verifies hash, expiry, `uses < max_uses`. Returns `{ valid, email? }`.
5. `POST /api/auth/register` тЖТ re-validates and atomically redeems the invite (increments `uses`, sets `usedByUserId`) inside a DB transaction. If cap is reached between validation and registration, the new user is added to `beta_waitlist` instead.

**Source tracking:** The `source` field on `usersAuth` and `users` rows records where the user came from. The `/start` page asks users to select their source (`instagram`, `tiktok`, `google`, `friend`, `coach`, `search`, etc.) and stores it in `localStorage` as `prfmr_source`. It is passed as `source` in the `POST /api/invites/request` body and as `source` in the `POST /api/auth/register` body. For Google signups the `?src=` query param on `/auth/google` carries the source through the OAuth redirect via `req.session.pendingSource`.

**Beta cap:** `BETA_USER_LIMIT` env var (integer). `getBetaUserLimit()` in `server/lib/beta-cap.ts` reads this with a fallback. `isBetaFull()` compares `COUNT(*) FROM users_auth` against the limit.

---

### 15.7 Username rules

- 3тАУ20 characters, lowercase alphanumeric + underscore + hyphen
- Normalised to lowercase on write
- Cannot match any reserved word (list in `shared/username-validation.ts`)
- `GET /api/auth/username-available?username=` checks format + DB uniqueness
- **Change rate limit: max 3 changes per 24 hours** per user (tracked in `username_changes` table). Returns HTTP 429 with `{ error, code: "RATE_LIMITED", nextAllowedAt: ISO string }` when exceeded.
- Changing username: `PATCH /api/auth/username` updates both `usersAuth.username` and `users.username` and inserts a row into `username_changes`. The session `req.user.username` is updated in-place; if the username change happens in `routes.ts` (profile page flow), the session is destroyed and client must re-login (`{ reloginRequired: true }`).

---

### 15.8 `requireAuth` middleware

Exported from `server/auth.ts`:
```typescript
export function requireAuth(req, res, next) {
  if (req.isAuthenticated()) return next();
  res.status(401).json({ message: "Unauthorized" });
}
```

Used on all protected routes. Most app routes also use `getAuthenticatedUser(req, res)` which additionally verifies the `users` profile row exists and returns `{ authUser, profileUser }` тАФ returning null and sending 401/404 automatically if not.

---

### 15.9 Special account: `onboardtester`

After `POST /api/user/me/onboard` completes for username `onboardtester`, a 90-second `setTimeout` resets all profile fields (`age`, `gender`, `height`, `currentWeight`, `activityLevel`, `goal`, `experienceLevel`, `targetCalories`, `targetProtein`, `targetCarbs`, `targetFat`, `bodyFatPct`) to `null` тАФ keeping this account perpetually ready for fresh onboarding demos in production.

---

### 15.10 Client-side route guards (`client/src/components/protected-route.tsx`)

Three guard components are exported. All read from `useAuth()` (тЖТ `/api/auth/me`) and `useUser()` (тЖТ `/api/user/me`).

**`isOnboardingComplete(profile)`** тАФ the shared check used by all guards:
```typescript
profile.targetCalories != null &&
profile.age != null &&
profile.gender != null &&
profile.height != null &&
profile.currentWeight != null &&
profile.activityLevel != null
```

| Guard | Applied to | Behaviour |
|---|---|---|
| `ProtectedRoute` | All authenticated app pages | No auth тЖТ `/` (login). Auth but not onboarded тЖТ `/onboarding`. |
| `PublicOnlyRoute` | `/`, `/login`, `/signup`, `/start`, `/forgot-password`, `/reset-password` | If authenticated + onboarded тЖТ `/dashboard`. If authenticated + not onboarded тЖТ `/onboarding`. |
| `OnboardingGuard` | `/onboarding` | No auth тЖТ `/`. Already onboarded тЖТ `/dashboard` (unless `?recalculate` query param present, or `prfmr_onboarding_completing` is set in `localStorage`). |

**`prfmr_onboarding_completing`** localStorage key: set when the wizard reaches the final submission steps (steps 28тАУ31) to prevent `OnboardingGuard` from redirecting away before the POST completes.

**`?recalculate` query param** on `/onboarding`: allows an already-onboarded user to re-run the wizard to update their targets without being redirected to the dashboard.

---

## 16. Full API Endpoint Reference

All endpoints require an authenticated session unless noted as **Public**.  
All responses are JSON. Error format: `{ message: string }`.  
All `/api` routes have `Cache-Control: no-store` globally applied.

---

### 16.1 Authentication (`/api/auth/*`)

Mounted via `app.use("/api/auth", authRoutes)`. Rate-limited: 10 req / 15 min for login/register/reset.

| Method | Path | Auth | Request body | Validation | Response |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| POST | `/api/auth/register` | Public | `{ email, username, password, inviteToken, source? }` | `insertAuthUserSchema` + invite token check + beta cap | 201 `{ user: { id, email, username, emailVerified: false } }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/login` | Public | `{ identifier, password }` | identifier min 1, password min 1 | `{ user: { id, email, username, emailVerified } }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/logout` | Yes | Empty | тАФ | `{ ok: true }` + clears `connect.sid` cookie |
| GET  | `/api/auth/me` | Yes | тАФ | тАФ | `{ user: { id, email, username, emailVerified } }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/resend-verification` | Yes | Empty | тАФ | `{ message }` (3 req / 15 min) |
| GET  | `/api/auth/verify-email?token=` | Public | Query: `token` | Token from DB | Redirect to `/verify-email?success=1` or `?error=...` |
| POST | `/api/auth/forgot-password` | Public | `{ email }` | Email format | `{ message }` тАФ same response always (no user enumeration); 5 req / 15 min |
| POST | `/api/auth/reset-password` | Public | `{ token, password }` | password: min 8 chars, тЙе1 letter, тЙе1 digit | `{ message }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/change-email` | Yes | `{ newEmail }` | Email format | `{ message }` + sends verification email |
| GET  | `/api/auth/username-available?username=` | Public | Query: `username` | `validateUsername()` | `{ available: boolean, error?: string }` |
| PATCH | `/api/auth/username` | Yes | `{ username }` | `validateUsername()` + 3 per 24h rate limit | `{ message, newUsername }` or 429 `{ error, code: "RATE_LIMITED", nextAllowedAt }` |
| GET  | `/api/auth/notifications/vapid-public-key` | Public | тАФ | тАФ | `{ publicKey }` |
| GET  | `/api/auth/notifications/status` | Public | тАФ | тАФ | `{ enabled: boolean }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/notifications/subscribe` | Yes | `{ endpoint: URL, keys: { p256dh, auth } }` | Zod URL + key presence | `{ message }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/notifications/unsubscribe` | Yes | `{ endpoint }` | endpoint presence | `{ message }` |
| POST | `/api/auth/notifications/test` | Yes | Empty | тАФ | `{ message, sent, failed }` |
| GET  | `/auth/google` | Public | тАФ | тАФ | Redirect to Google consent (no `/api` prefix) |
| GET  | `/auth/google/callback` | Public | тАФ | тАФ | Redirect to `/dashboard` or `/?error=google_auth_failed` (no `/api` prefix) |

**`insertAuthUserSchema` fields:**
- `email`: valid email, lowercased
- `username`: 3тАУ20 chars, alphanumeric/underscore/hyphen, normalised to lowercase, not reserved
- `password`: min 8 chars, тЙе1 letter, тЙе1 digit

**Username rate limit:** max 3 changes per 24 hours per user. Returns HTTP 429 with `{ error, code: "RATE_LIMITED", nextAllowedAt: ISO string }`.

---

### 16.2 Invites (`/api/invites/*`)

Mounted via `app.use("/api/invites", inviteRoutes)`. Rate-limited: 5 req / hr.

| Method | Path | Auth | Request body | Response |

| POST | `/api/invites/request` | Public | `{ email, source? }` | `{ message }` тАФ sends invite code email. 403 if beta full (added to waitlist). |

Invite codes: 10-char uppercase alphanumeric, valid 7 days, max 1 use, stored as SHA-256 hash.

### 16.5 User / Profile

| Method | Path | Auth | Request body | Validation | Response |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| GET  | `/api/user/me` | Yes | тАФ | тАФ | Full `User` object |
| GET  | `/api/me` | Yes | тАФ | тАФ | Same (legacy alias) |
| POST | `/api/user/me/onboard` | Yes | Onboarding body (see below) | `api.user.onboard.input` Zod schema | Updated `User`; seeds today's weight log |
| PATCH | `/api/me/body-composition` | Yes | `{ bodyFatPct: number \| null }` | 0.0тАУ1.0 decimal (e.g. 0.15 = 15%) | Updated `User` |
| PATCH | `/api/me/sport` | Yes | `{ mainSport: string \| null }` | max 80 chars | Updated `User` |
| PUT  | `/api/me/profile-photo` | Yes | `{ profilePhotoUrl }` | presence check | Updated `User` |
| GET  | `/api/username/available?username=` | Public | тАФ | `validateUsername()` | `{ available: boolean, reason? }` |
| PATCH | `/api/me/username` | Yes | `{ username }` | `validateUsername()` + 3/24h | `{ message, reloginRequired: true, newUsername }` |

**Onboarding body (`POST /api/user/me/onboard`):**
```typescript
{
  gender:           "male" | "female"
  age:              number
  height:           number          // cm
  currentWeight:    number          // kg
  activityLevel:    "sedentary" | "light" | "moderate" | "active" | "very_active"
  goal:             "fat_loss" | "maintenance" | "weight_gain"
  experienceLevel:  "beginner" | "intermediate" | "advanced"
  bodyFatPct?:      number          // 0.0тАУ1.0
  // Survey fields (all optional strings):
  surveyCutExperience?, surveyCutOutcome?, surveyCalorieKnowledge?,
  surveyUnderfueling?, surveyTrainingLoadTracking?, surveyMicroKnowledge?,
  surveyEnergyScore?, surveyPerformance?,
  surveyMainProblems?: string[]
  surveyCommitment?, surveyStarRating?
}
```
Sanitisation defaults: ageтЖТ25, heightтЖТ170, currentWeightтЖТ70 if null/NaN.  
Calls `calculateTargets()` server-side and stores resulting targets.  
Seeds today's weight log with `currentWeight`.  
Username `onboardtester`: 90-second timeout auto-resets all profile fields to null after completion.

---

### 16.6 Add Food тАФ Complete Flow

This section documents every way food can be logged, how data flows from the UI to the `food_entries` table, how micronutrient data is resolved, and how count mode and raw/cooked weight conversions work.

---

#### Entry points тАФ five ways to add a food

| Path | Source | macroSource | microSource | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Whole food (ingredient) | User selects from ingredients.json catalog | `"ingredient"` | `"ingredient"` | Full micronutrient scoring available |
| OFF text search | User searches тЖТ picks OFF result | `"off"` | `"ingredient"` if mapped, else `"none"` | Macros from OFF; micros from mapped ingredient |
| Barcode scan | Camera scan тЖТ OFF lookup | `"off"` | `"ingredient"` if mapped, else `"none"` | Same OFF pipeline via barcode |
| Manual entry | User types name + macros | `"ingredient"` | `"none"` | No micronutrient data |
| Custom food | From user's "My Database" | `"off"` | `"none"` | Created once, reused from custom_foods table |

---

#### Reading food entries

| Method | Path | Auth | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/me/food/:date` | Yes | All `FoodEntry[]` for the authenticated user on that date (YYYY-MM-DD) |
| GET | `/api/me/food-entries/range?start=&end=` | Yes | Date range; both `start` and `end` required (YYYY-MM-DD) |
| GET | `/api/food/:username/:date` | Public | Public read by username (used for sharing/admin) |

---

#### `GET /api/foods/search?q=` тАФ Open Food Facts text search

Minimum query length: 2 characters. Returns up to 20 results. No auth required. Results are in-memory cached per query key with a TTL (evicted when cache exceeds 200 entries).

**Search strategy:**
1. Always queries UK-tagged products first
2. If UK returns fewer than 5 results, also queries the world endpoint (no country filter)
3. Merges results, UK results take deduplication priority
4. Ranks using a query-aware scoring engine (`parseFoodSearchQuery` + `rankOffResult`)
5. Returns top 20

**Response shape** (each item is an OFF product object):
```
{ name, brand, categories, image_url, macros_per_100g: { kcal, protein, carbs, fat, fibre }, barcode?, ... }
```

---

#### `POST /api/foods/search/match` тАФ Match a food name to an ingredient

Used to suggest a micronutrient-mapped ingredient for a manually entered or OFF-sourced food.

**Request:**
```
{ name: string, brand?: string, calories?: number, protein?: number, carbs?: number, fat?: number }
```

**Response:**
```
{ suggestions: { best: MatchCandidate | null, top: MatchCandidate[] } }
```

`MatchCandidate`:
```
{ ingredientIndex: number, ingredientName: string, confidence: "high"|"medium"|"low",
  method: "exact"|"synonym"|"fuzzy"|"user_selected", score: number, reasons: string[] }
```

**Matching algorithm** (from `server/lib/offMatch.ts`):
1. **Exact match** тАФ normalised name equality тЖТ confidence `high`, score 1.0
2. **Synonym match** тАФ checked against a hardcoded synonym dictionary (e.g. "chicken breast slices" тЖТ "Chicken Deli Slices") тЖТ confidence `high` or `medium` for processed products
3. **Fuzzy scoring** тАФ composite of Jaccard + Dice token similarity (55%), category similarity (20%), macro profile sanity (15%), brand similarity (10%). Minimum score threshold 0.08 to be included. Confidence: тЙе0.45 = high, тЙе0.25 = medium, <0.25 = low.

**Processing penalty:** Products identified as processed (ready meals, protein bars, sauces, crisps, etc.) have their best-match confidence capped at `medium` unless the matched ingredient is itself a processed food type.

---

#### `GET /api/food/barcode/:code` тАФ Barcode lookup

No auth required for the lookup itself; auth is needed to create a custom food. Queries `https://world.openfoodfacts.org/api/v0/product/{code}.json`.

**Response when found in OFF:**
```typescript
{
  found: true,
  barcode: string,
  off: {
    name: string,
    brand: string | null,
    categories: string | null,
    image_url: string | null,
    macros_per_100g: { kcal, protein, carbs, fat, fibre }
  },
  mapping: {                          // null if not yet mapped
    ingredientIndex: number,
    ingredientName: string,
    matchConfidence: "high"|"medium"|"low",
    verifiedByUser: boolean
  } | null,
  suggestions: {                      // auto-generated match suggestions
    best: MatchCandidate | null,
    top: MatchCandidate[]
  },
  computedDefaults: {
    macroSource: "off",
    microSource: "internal" | "none"  // "internal" if an existing mapping exists
  }
}
```

**Response when not in OFF but found in custom foods:**
```typescript
{
  found: true,
  barcode: string,
  source: "custom",
  custom: { id, name, brand, servingSizeG, macros_per_100g },
  computedDefaults: { macroSource: "custom", microSource: "none" }
}
```

**Response when not found:**
```
{ found: false, barcode: string, canCreate: boolean }
```

---

#### `POST /api/food/barcode/:code/map` тАФ Save a barcodeтЖТingredient mapping

Auth required. Persists a record to the `off_product_mappings` table so the next scan of this barcode automatically resolves micros.

**Request:**
```
{
  ingredientIndex: number,        // zero-based index into ingredients.json
  offName?: string,
  offBrand?: string,
  offCategories?: string,
  verifiedByUser?: boolean,       // default true
  rememberMapping?: boolean       // default true тАФ set false to return a temporary mapping without saving
}
```

**Response:**
```
{ success: true, mapping: { ingredientIndex, ingredientName, matchConfidence, verifiedByUser }, temporary?: true }
```

When a mapping is saved, any future log entry with `offBarcode = code` can set `microSource: "ingredient"` and `ingredientIndex` to unlock full AMQS scoring.

---

#### `POST /api/food/barcode/:code/create` тАФ Create a custom food from a barcode

Auth required. Validated with Zod. Creates a record in `custom_foods`.

**Schema:**
```
name         string    min 1, max 200 тАФ REQUIRED
brand        string    max 200
kcal         number    0тАУ9999 (per 100g)
protein      number    0тАУ999
carbs        number    0тАУ999
fat          number    0тАУ999
fibre        number    0тАУ999
servingSizeG number    min 1, max 9999
```

Returns `409` if a custom food with this barcode already exists for this user.

---

#### Custom Foods database (`/api/foods/custom`)

| Method | Path | Auth | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/foods/custom?q=&limit=` | Yes | Optional name search, default limit 50 |
| GET | `/api/foods/custom/:id` | Yes | Single item |
| POST | `/api/foods/custom` | Yes | Create тАФ see schema below |
| PUT | `/api/foods/custom/:id` | Yes | Full update |
| DELETE | `/api/foods/custom/:id` | Yes | тАФ |
| GET | `/api/foods/custom/barcode/:code` | Yes | Lookup by barcode |

**Custom food create/update schema (Zod-validated):**
```
name          string    REQUIRED min 1
brand         string    optional
servingSizeG  integer   optional positive
kcalPer100g   integer   REQUIRED тЙе 0
proteinPer100g  number  optional тЙе 0
carbsPer100g    number  optional тЙе 0
fatPer100g      number  optional тЙе 0
fibrePer100g    number  optional тЙе 0
saltPer100g     number  optional тЙе 0
sugarPer100g    number  optional тЙе 0
barcode         string  optional
```

---

#### `POST /api/food` тАФ Create food entry

Validated against `insertFoodEntrySchema` (derived from the `food_entries` table via `drizzle-zod`).
`userId` is injected server-side from the authenticated session тАФ do **not** send it.

**Required fields:**
```
name        string         Display name of the food (e.g. "Chicken Breast (Grilled)")
date        string         YYYY-MM-DD тАФ the diary date to log to
meal        string         "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack"
calories    integer        kcal тАФ whole number
protein     integer        grams тАФ whole number
carbs       integer        grams тАФ whole number
fat         integer        grams тАФ whole number
```

**Optional fields:**
```
grams             integer   Serving size in grams (default: 100)
fibre             integer   Dietary fibre in grams (default: 0)
snackIndex        integer   Position within the snack section; only used when meal="snack"
sourceType        string    "manual" | "off" | "ingredient" (default: "manual")
offBarcode        string    Barcode string тАФ only when sourceType="off"
ingredientIndex   integer   Zero-based index into ingredients.json тАФ enables micronutrient scoring
macroSource       string    "off" | "ingredient" | "mixed" (default: "ingredient")
microSource       string    "ingredient" | "none" (default: "none")
enteredBasis      string    "raw" | "cooked" | null тАФ see Raw/Cooked section below
normalizedGrams   integer   Canonical gram weight after rawтЖТcooked conversion
yieldFactorUsed   number    Yield factor used during conversion (e.g. 0.75)
```

**Server behaviour:**
- After insert, the server runs a verification SELECT. If the row cannot be confirmed: `500 { error: "Food entry verification failed" }`
- `estimatedKcal` on the session is NOT recalculated by food entries тАФ calorie credits come from training sessions only

**Error responses:**
```
400 { error: "Validation failed", issues: [{ path, message }] }
401 { error: "Not authenticated" }
404 { error: "User profile not found" }
500 { error: "Food entry was not persisted тАФ no valid row returned" }
500 { error: "Food entry verification failed тАФ row not found after insert" }
500 { error: "Failed to save food entry" }
```

---

#### `PATCH /api/food/:id` тАФ Update food entry

Accepts any subset of the fields above. No Zod validation тАФ passes `req.body` directly to storage. Returns updated `FoodEntry` or `404 { message: "Food entry not found" }`.

---

#### `DELETE /api/food/:id`

Returns 204 on success, `500 { error }` on failure.

---

#### `FoodEntry` full response shape

```typescript
{
  id:               number
  userId:           number
  date:             string         // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  name:             string
  grams:            number | null  // default 100
  calories:         number
  protein:          number
  carbs:            number
  fat:              number
  fibre:            number | null  // default 0
  meal:             string         // "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack"
  snackIndex:       number | null
  sourceType:       string         // "manual" | "off" | "ingredient"
  offBarcode:       string | null
  ingredientIndex:  number | null
  macroSource:      string         // "off" | "ingredient" | "mixed"
  microSource:      string         // "ingredient" | "none"
  enteredBasis:     string | null  // "raw" | "cooked" | null
  normalizedGrams:  number | null
  yieldFactorUsed:  number | null
}
```

---

#### Micronutrient mapping тАФ how it works end-to-end

Micronutrients are **not stored in food_entries**. They are computed on-demand by `getFoodMicrosForDate()` in `server/lib/micros.ts` by reading from `data/ingredients.json` (loaded once, then in-memory cached).

**`ingredients.json` тАФ the `Ingredient` type:**
```typescript
{
  name:                    string
  calories_per_100g:       number
  protein_g_per_100g:      number
  carbs_g_per_100g:        number
  fat_g_per_100g:          number
  fibre_g_per_100g:        number
  iron_mg_per_100g?:       number | null
  calcium_mg_per_100g?:    number | null
  magnesium_mg_per_100g?:  number | null
  zinc_mg_per_100g?:       number | null
  potassium_mg_per_100g?:  number | null
  vitamin_c_mg_per_100g?:  number | null
  vitamin_a_ug_per_100g?:  number | null
  vitamin_b12_ug_per_100g?:number | null
  folate_ug_per_100g?:     number | null
  iodine_ug_per_100g?:     number | null
  selenium_ug_per_100g?:   number | null
  vitamin_d_ug_per_100g?:  number | null
  // Layer 2 nutrients:
  vitamin_b1_mg_per_100g?: number | null
  vitamin_b2_mg_per_100g?: number | null
  vitamin_b3_mg_per_100g?: number | null
  vitamin_b6_mg_per_100g?: number | null
  omega3_g_per_100g?:      number | null
  // Metadata:
  supportsCookedToggle?:   boolean
  canonicalBasis?:         "raw" | "cooked" | null
  cookedYieldFactor?:      number | null
  commonScore?:            number
}
```

**17 tracked micronutrients:** iron, calcium, vitamin D, magnesium, zinc, iodine, selenium, folate, vitamin B12, vitamin C, vitamin A, potassium, vitamin B1, vitamin B2, vitamin B3, vitamin B6, omega-3.

**Resolution rules (in priority order):**

1. **Composite / core food** тАФ if `entry.name` (lowercased) matches a key in the `COMPOSITE_FOODS` map, the entry is decomposed into its component ingredients. Each component's micros are scaled proportionally: `contribution = (component_grams ├Ч scale) ├Ч micro_per_100g / 100` where `scale = entryGrams / serving`. Composite foods include: porridge, mashed potato, scrambled eggs, overnight oats, beans on toast, toast variants, coffee drinks, greek yoghurt with honey, etc.

2. **Mapped OFF entry** тАФ if `sourceType === "off"` AND `microSource === "ingredient"` AND `ingredientIndex` is a valid integer, the ingredient at `ingredients[ingredientIndex]` is used for micro calculation. Formula: `contribution = entryGrams ├Ч micro_per_100g / 100`. Gram weight used is `normalizedGrams` if present, otherwise `grams`.

3. **Whole food / manual entry (name match)** тАФ if `sourceType !== "off"`, a case-insensitive name match against `ingredients.json` is attempted. If matched, micros are calculated as above.

4. **No match** тАФ entry contributes zero micros. `microSource` will be `"none"`.

**Gram weight used for micro calc:** `normalizedGrams || grams`. If the user entered a cooked weight but the ingredient's `canonicalBasis` is `"raw"`, the client computes `normalizedGrams` before sending (see Raw/Cooked section).

---

#### Raw vs Cooked weight toggle

Only ingredients with `supportsCookedToggle: true` in `ingredients.json` show the raw/cooked toggle in the UI. Examples: chicken breast (raw canonical), potatoes, rice.

**Fields involved:**
- `enteredBasis` тАФ `"raw"` or `"cooked"` (what the user weighed)
- `canonicalBasis` тАФ from the ingredient entry in `ingredients.json` тАФ which basis the macro/micro values are expressed per
- `cookedYieldFactor` тАФ from `ingredients.json` тАФ the multiplier from raw to cooked (e.g. `0.75` means 100g raw тЖТ 75g cooked)
- `normalizedGrams` тАФ the gram weight converted to the canonical basis, used for all nutrition calculations
- `yieldFactorUsed` тАФ stored for auditability

**Client-side conversion formula:**
```javascript
// enteredBasis = "cooked", canonicalBasis = "raw"  (e.g. chicken breast)
normalizedGrams = enteredGrams / cookedYieldFactor

// enteredBasis = "raw", canonicalBasis = "cooked"  (e.g. pasta)
normalizedGrams = enteredGrams * cookedYieldFactor
```

**What gets sent to `POST /api/food`:**
```javascript
{
  grams: enteredGrams,              // what the user actually weighed
  enteredBasis: "raw" | "cooked",
  normalizedGrams: Math.round(normalizedGrams),
  yieldFactorUsed: ingredient.cookedYieldFactor,
  // macros are calculated from normalizedGrams ├Ч per_100g / 100
}
```

Macros (calories, protein, carbs, fat) are always calculated from `normalizedGrams` when it is present, ensuring the food diary reflects canonical nutrition values even when the user weighed cooked food.

---

#### Count mode vs grams mode

For specific whole foods (eggs, fruit, bread, etc.), the "Add food" dialog shows a count stepper (1, 2, 3тАж) with an optional size selector (small / medium / large), rather than a raw grams input.

This is defined in `client/src/lib/coreFoodUnits.ts`. Only ingredients explicitly listed in `CORE_FOOD_UNITS` support count mode. The key must exactly match the ingredient name in `ingredients.json`.

**Count config type:**
```typescript
interface CoreFoodUnit {
  supportsCount: true
  supportsSize: boolean           // true тЖТ shows small / medium / large selector
  defaultCount: number
  defaultSize?: "small"|"medium"|"large"
  gramsBySize?: { small: number, medium: number, large: number }   // when supportsSize === true
  gramsPerUnit?: number           // when supportsSize === false
  unitLabel: string               // displayed in UI, e.g. "egg", "slice", "banana"
}
```

**Gram conversion:**
```javascript
// With size selector:
totalGrams = Math.round(gramsBySize[selectedSize] * count)

// Without size selector:
totalGrams = Math.round(gramsPerUnit * count)
```

`totalGrams` replaces the grams input and feeds directly into macro calculation (`per_100g ├Ч totalGrams / 100`).

Count mode is **purely a client-side UX feature**. The `POST /api/food` request always sends `grams` (the resolved total), never a count. The server has no knowledge of count mode.

**Helper functions exported from `coreFoodUnits.ts`:**
```typescript
getCoreFoodUnit(foodName: string): CoreFoodUnit | null
computeUnitGrams(unit: CoreFoodUnit, count: number, size: UnitSize): number
```

---

Foods that support size show gram weights for small / medium / large. Foods without size show a single gram-per-unit value.

---

**Adding a new count-mode food**

To add a new ingredient to count mode:
1. Find the exact name as it appears in `data/ingredients.json`
2. Add an entry to `CORE_FOOD_UNITS` in `client/src/lib/coreFoodUnits.ts` keyed by that exact name
3. Set `supportsSize: true` and provide `gramsBySize` if sizes differ meaningfully; otherwise `supportsSize: false` and `gramsPerUnit`
4. Set a sensible `defaultCount` and `defaultSize` (if applicable)
5. Gram weights must be sourced from USDA FDC standard portion sizes

---

#### Composite / Core Foods (meal decomposition)

Some common mixed-dish entries (e.g. "Porridge (Oats + Milk)", "Scrambled Eggs (2 Eggs, Butter)") are treated specially by the micro engine via the `COMPOSITE_FOODS` map in `server/lib/micros.ts`.

These are matched by exact case-insensitive name. When matched, micros are derived from the component ingredients scaled to the logged gram weight тАФ bypassing the normal single-ingredient lookup. This allows multi-ingredient dishes to contribute accurate micronutrient data without requiring a separate entry per ingredient.

The client must log these using their exact canonical names. If the name doesn't match the `COMPOSITE_FOODS` key, they fall back to the normal name-match path.

---

#### `GET /api/ingredients` тАФ Full ingredient list

Returns the full `ingredients.json` array (~307 items) including all macro and micro data. Public endpoint, no auth required. Used by the client to populate the whole-food search/autocomplete.

#### Saved meal templates

| Method | Path | Auth | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/me/meals/templates` | Yes | List all templates with items |
| POST | `/api/me/meals/templates/from-log` | Yes | Create template from an existing diary meal тАФ see below |
| POST | `/api/me/meals/templates/:id/log` | Yes | Log a template to a date/meal тАФ see below |
| DELETE | `/api/me/meals/templates/:id` | Yes | тАФ |

**Create template from log:**
```
{ date: "YYYY-MM-DD", meal: string, name: string }
```
Captures all food entries from that meal as a reusable template. Preserves `sourceType`, `ingredientIndex`, `offBarcode`, `macroSource`, `microSource` per item.

**Log a template:**
```
{ date: "YYYY-MM-DD", meal: string }
```
Creates new `food_entries` rows for each item in the template (same as `POST /api/food` ├Ч N).  
Returns `{ count: number, entries: FoodEntry[] }`.

---

#### Copy a meal

```
POST /api/me/meals/copy
{ fromDate: "YYYY-MM-DD", fromMeal: string, toDate: "YYYY-MM-DD", toMeal?: string }
```
Copies all entries from `fromDate`/`fromMeal` to `toDate`/`toMeal` (defaults to same meal name if `toMeal` omitted). Preserves all source/ingredient metadata.  
Returns `{ count: number, entries: FoodEntry[] }`.  
`400` if no entries found for the source meal.

---

#### `POST /api/food` тАФ Create food entry

Validated against `insertFoodEntrySchema` (derived from the `food_entries` table via `drizzle-zod`).  
`userId` is injected server-side from the authenticated session тАФ do **not** send it.

**Required fields:**
```
name        string         Display name of the food (e.g. "Chicken Breast (Grilled)")
date        string         YYYY-MM-DD тАФ the diary date to log to
meal        string         "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack"
calories    integer        kcal тАФ whole number
protein     integer        grams тАФ whole number
carbs       integer        grams тАФ whole number
fat         integer        grams тАФ whole number
```

**Optional fields:**
```
grams             integer   Serving size in grams (default: 100)
fibre             integer   Dietary fibre in grams (default: 0)
snackIndex        integer   Position slot within the snack section; only used when meal="snack"
sourceType        string    "manual" | "off" | "ingredient" (default: "manual")
                            manual   = user typed it in
                            off      = came from Open Food Facts barcode scan
                            ingredient = matched to an entry in ingredients.json
offBarcode        string    Barcode string if sourceType="off" (e.g. "5000112548167")
ingredientIndex   integer   Zero-based index into ingredients.json; enables full micronutrient scoring
macroSource       string    "off" | "ingredient" | "mixed" (default: "ingredient")
                            Tells AMQS which macros to trust for scoring
microSource       string    "ingredient" | "none" (default: "none")
                            "ingredient" = micros will be computed via ingredients.json entry
enteredBasis      string    "raw" | "cooked" | null
                            raw    = the gram weight was measured before cooking
                            cooked = the gram weight was measured after cooking
                            null   = not applicable (pre-packaged food, etc.)
normalizedGrams   integer   Canonical gram weight after rawтЖТcooked conversion (set by client or omitted)
yieldFactorUsed   number    Cooked yield factor applied during conversion (e.g. 0.75 for grilled chicken)
```

**Response:** `201 FoodEntry` тАФ the inserted row including `id`.  
After insert, the server verifies the row exists via a follow-up SELECT. If it cannot be confirmed, returns `500 { error: "Food entry verification failed" }`.

**Error responses:**
```
400 { error: "Validation failed", issues: [{ path, message }] }   тАФ schema validation failure
401 { error: "Not authenticated" }
404 { error: "User profile not found" }
500 { error: "Food entry was not persisted тАФ no valid row returned" }
500 { error: "Failed to save food entry" }
```

---

#### `PATCH /api/food/:id` тАФ Update food entry

Accepts any subset of the fields listed above (all optional).  
No Zod validation тАФ passes `req.body` directly to `storage.updateFoodEntry(id, req.body)`.  
Returns the updated `FoodEntry` on success, or `404 { message: "Food entry not found" }` on failure.

---

#### `POST /api/me/meals/copy` тАФ Copy a meal

```
{ fromDate: "YYYY-MM-DD", fromMeal: string, toDate: "YYYY-MM-DD", toMeal?: string }
```
Copies all food entries from `fromDate`/`fromMeal` to `toDate`/`toMeal` (defaults to same meal name if `toMeal` omitted).  
Returns `{ count: number, entries: FoodEntry[] }`.

---

#### `FoodEntry` full response shape

```typescript
{
  id:               number
  userId:           number
  date:             string         // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  name:             string
  grams:            number | null  // default 100
  calories:         number
  protein:          number
  carbs:            number
  fat:              number
  fibre:            number | null  // default 0
  meal:             string         // "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack"
  snackIndex:       number | null
  sourceType:       string         // "manual" | "off" | "ingredient"
  offBarcode:       string | null
  ingredientIndex:  number | null
  macroSource:      string         // "off" | "ingredient" | "mixed"
  microSource:      string         // "ingredient" | "none"
  enteredBasis:     string | null  // "raw" | "cooked" | null
  normalizedGrams:  number | null
  yieldFactorUsed:  number | null
}
```

### 16.14 Training Sessions & Exercises

#### Catalog endpoints (public тАФ no auth required)

| Method | Path | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/exercises?query=` | Exercise catalog. `query` param optional тАФ filters by name. Returns 503 if catalog is empty (unseeded DB). |
| GET | `/api/activities?query=` | Activity catalog with stored MET values. `query` param optional. Returns 503 if empty. |

**`ExerciseCatalogItem` shape:**
```
{ id, name, category, equipment, primaryMuscle, isCommon }
category:   "push" | "pull" | "legs" | "core" | "full_body"
equipment:  "barbell" | "dumbbell" | "machine" | "bodyweight" | "cable" | "kettlebell" | "bands" | "other"
```

**`ActivityCatalogItem` shape:**
```
{ id, name, intensity, metValue }
intensity:  "light" | "moderate" | "vigorous"
metValue:   float  тАФ the MET value stored in the activity_catalog table (e.g. 8.0 for running)
```
> MET values are **stored in the `activity_catalog` database table**, seeded at startup. They are not hardcoded in route logic. The catalog is the single source of truth for MET values тАФ the client must look up the activity and pass the `metValue` when creating an activity log.

---

#### `POST /api/workouts/sessions` тАФ Create a session

**Required fields:**
```
date        string   YYYY-MM-DD
timeOfDay   string   "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening"
```

**Optional fields:**
```
title             string   Free text session name (null if omitted)
notes             string   Free text notes (null if omitted)
durationMinutes   integer  Overall session duration (not used for calorie calc тАФ see activities)
intensity         string   "light" | "moderate" | "vigorous" (legacy тАФ not used for calorie calc)
isPlanned         boolean  default false
trainingBlockId   integer  Links session to a training block
```

**Server behaviour:**
- `userId` is injected from session (never sent by client)
- `estimatedKcal` initialises to `0`; recalculated automatically whenever exercises/activities are added or edited
- `estimatedMet` is `null` on creation (aggregate MET not computed)
- Creating a session for a date **automatically deletes any rest-day mark** for that date

**Response:** `201 WorkoutSession`
```
{ id, userId, date, timeOfDay, title, notes, durationMinutes, intensity, estimatedMet, estimatedKcal, isPlanned, trainingBlockId }
```

**Error responses:**
```
400 { message: "date and timeOfDay are required" }
500 { message: "Failed to create workout session" }
```

---

#### `GET /api/workouts/sessions?start=&end=` тАФ List sessions (with full detail)

Auth required. `start` and `end` query params required (YYYY-MM-DD).

Returns sessions expanded with nested exercises+sets and activities:
```typescript
WorkoutSession & {
  exercises: (WorkoutExercise & { sets: WorkoutSet[] })[]
  activities: SessionActivity[]
}
```

---

#### `PATCH /api/workouts/sessions/:id` тАФ Update session

Only `title` and `notes` are currently writable via PATCH. Intensity/duration are managed via exercises and activities.

---

#### `DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id` тАФ Delete session

Returns 204. Cascades to all child exercises, sets, and activities.

---

#### `POST /api/workouts/sessions/:sessionId/exercises` тАФ Add a strength exercise

**Required:**
```
name   string   Display name of the exercise (e.g. "Back Squat")
```

**Optional:**
```
exerciseCatalogId   integer   Links to exercise_catalog.id for catalog-matched exercises
intensity           string    "light" | "moderate" | "vigorous" (default: "moderate")
                              Used in per-set kcal estimates (light=3, moderate=4.5, vigorous=6 kcal/set)
durationMinutes     integer   Manual duration override
```

**Server behaviour:**
- `orderIndex` is auto-assigned as `max(existing orderIndex) + 1`
- `estimatedKcal` starts at 0 and is recalculated when sets are added
- Triggers `recalculateSessionCalories()` after insert

**Response:** `201 WorkoutExercise`
```
{ id, sessionId, exerciseCatalogId, name, orderIndex, intensity, durationMinutes, estimatedKcal }
```

---

#### `POST /api/workouts/exercises/:exerciseId/sets` тАФ Add a set

**Required:**
```
reps   integer   Number of reps (0 is valid for failed/timed sets)
```

**Optional:**
```
weightKg        number   Load in kg (null for bodyweight)
rpe             number   Rate of Perceived Exertion 1тАУ10 (set-level RPE)
restSeconds     integer  Rest after this set in seconds
tempo           string   Tempo string e.g. "3-1-2-0" (eccentric-pause-concentric-pause)
durationSeconds integer  For timed/isometric sets
```

**Server behaviour:**
- `setIndex` is auto-assigned as `max(existing setIndex) + 1`
- Adding a set triggers `recalculateSessionCalories()` which recomputes exercise kcal as `setCount ├Ч kcalPerSet[intensity]`

**Response:** `201 WorkoutSet`
```
{ id, workoutExerciseId, setIndex, reps, weightKg, rpe, restSeconds, tempo, durationSeconds }
```

---

#### `POST /api/workouts/sessions/:sessionId/activities` тАФ Add a cardio or lifting activity

This is the primary way to log cardio (running, cycling, sparring, etc.) and lifting blocks with time+RPE.

**Required for all activity types:**
```
name              string    Display name (e.g. "Running", "Boxing Sparring")
durationMinutes   integer   Duration in minutes
```

**For `activityType = "cardio"` (default):**
```
metValue    number   REQUIRED тАФ MET value from activity_catalog or user-provided
                     Formula: kcal/min = MET ├Ч 3.5 ├Ч bodyweightKg / 200
intensity   string   "light" | "moderate" | "vigorous" (stored, not used in kcal calc)
activityCatalogId  integer  optional тАФ links to activity_catalog.id
rpe         number   optional тАФ RPE 1тАУ10 for this cardio effort
                     If provided, a scaling factor is applied to the MET kcal estimate:
                     factor = 0.9 + (rpe / 10) ├Ч 0.2
                     RPE 1 тЖТ ├Ч0.92  |  RPE 5 тЖТ ├Ч1.00  |  RPE 10 тЖТ ├Ч1.10
                     NOT applied to leisure/walking/recovery activities (name-matched)
```

**For `activityType = "lifting"`:**
```
activityType   string   must be "lifting"
sessionRpe     number   REQUIRED тАФ session-level RPE 1тАУ10
bodyRegion     string   REQUIRED тАФ "upper" | "lower" | "full"
```

**Server kcal formula тАФ cardio:**
```
rawKcal       = round((metValue ├Ч 3.5 ├Ч bodyweightKg / 200) ├Ч durationMinutes)
rpeFactor     = 0.9 + (rpe / 10) ├Ч 0.2   [only for eligible activities]
estimatedKcal = round(rawKcal ├Ч rpeFactor)
```

**Server kcal formula тАФ lifting:**
```
MET is derived from sessionRpe via lookup table:
  RPE 1тАУ3  тЖТ MET 3.5
  RPE 4тАУ5  тЖТ MET 4.5
  RPE 6тАУ7  тЖТ MET 5.0
  RPE 8тАУ9  тЖТ MET 6.0
  RPE 10   тЖТ MET 6.5

regionMultiplier (kcal):
  upper тЖТ 1.0
  lower тЖТ 1.1
  full  тЖТ 1.15

estimatedKcal = round(MET ├Ч bodyweightKg ├Ч (durationMinutes / 60) ├Ч regionMultiplier)
```

**Training Load Score тАФ lifting only:**
```
regionMultiplier (load):
  upper тЖТ 1.0
  lower тЖТ 1.25
  full  тЖТ 1.1

trainingLoadScore = round(durationMinutes ├Ч sessionRpe ├Ч regionMultiplier)
```

**Bodyweight resolution** (for all kcal calcs):  
Server resolves `bodyweightKg` via: today's weight log тЖТ average of last 7 weight logs тЖТ `users.currentWeight`. If none available, `estimatedKcal = 0`.

**Lifting activity name:** prefixed with `[Lifting] ` at storage time.

**Response:** `201 SessionActivity`
```
{ id, sessionId, activityCatalogId, name, durationMinutes, intensity, metValue,
  estimatedKcal, activityType, sessionRpe, bodyRegion, trainingLoadScore, rpe }
```

**Error responses:**
```
400 { message: "name and durationMinutes are required" }
400 { message: "metValue is required for cardio activities" }
400 { message: "sessionRpe and bodyRegion are required for lifting activities" }
404 { message: "Session not found" }
```

---

#### `PATCH /api/workouts/activities/:id` тАФ Update an activity

Accepts any subset of the activity fields. When `durationMinutes`, `metValue`, `sessionRpe`, `bodyRegion`, or `rpe` changes, `estimatedKcal` and `trainingLoadScore` are **fully recalculated server-side** using the same formulas above. The updated value is persisted before the response is sent.

---

#### `PATCH /api/workouts/exercises/:id` / `PATCH /api/workouts/sets/:id`

Accepts any subset of the respective fields. No Zod validation тАФ passes body directly to storage update. Returns the updated record or `404 { message }`.

---

#### `DELETE /api/workouts/exercises/:id` / `DELETE /api/workouts/sets/:id` / `DELETE /api/workouts/activities/:id`

All return 204. Deleting an exercise, set, or activity triggers `recalculateSessionCalories()` to keep `workoutSessions.estimatedKcal` accurate.

---

#### `recalculateSessionCalories()` тАФ how the session total is maintained

Called automatically after every create/update/delete of an exercise, set, or activity. It:

1. Re-derives kcal for each **strength exercise** as `setCount ├Ч kcalPerSet[intensity]`:
   - `light` тЖТ 3 kcal/set, `moderate` тЖТ 4.5 kcal/set, `vigorous` тЖТ 6 kcal/set
2. Re-derives kcal for each **lifting activity** using `estimateLiftingCalories()` with the user's current resolved bodyweight
3. Re-derives kcal for each **cardio activity** as `round((MET ├Ч 3.5 ├Ч weight / 200) ├Ч duration ├Ч rpeFactor)`
4. Writes the total back to `workoutSessions.estimatedKcal`

---

| Method | Path | Auth | Response |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/training/summary/:username/:date` | Yes | `{ date, totalKcal, sessions: [{ id, timeOfDay, estimatedKcal, exerciseCount, activityCount }] }` |

### 16.15 Training Calories & Load

| Method | Path | Auth | Request body | Response |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/me/training/summary/:date` | Yes | тАФ | `{ date, totalKcal, totalKcalAdjusted, sessions: [...], isRestDay }` |
| POST | `/api/me/training/manual-burn` | Yes | See below | `201 { sessionId, caloriesBurned, date, label }` |
| POST | `/api/me/training/load` | Yes | See below | `{ trainingLoadScore, bodyRegionMultiplier, ... }` |
| GET | `/api/me/training-load/:date` | Yes | тАФ | Full ACWR + load data (see ┬з10.2) |
| GET | `/api/me/training/load-history/:date` | Yes | тАФ | 28-day load history array |
| POST | `/api/me/training/load-override/:date` | Yes | `{ classification: string }` | Updated override |

---

#### `POST /api/me/training/manual-burn` тАФ Log calories without a structured session

Validated inline with Zod:
```
caloriesBurned   integer   REQUIRED тАФ 1тАУ5000
durationMinutes  integer   optional тАФ 1тАУ600
label            string    optional тАФ max 50 chars (default: "Manual entry")
date             string    optional тАФ YYYY-MM-DD (default: today)
```
Creates a `WorkoutSession` titled `[Manual] {label}` plus a matching `SessionActivity` with `metValue: 0`. `timeOfDay` is derived from the current server clock hour.

**Error:** `400 { message: "Invalid input", errors: { fieldErrors } }`

---

#### `POST /api/me/training/load` тАФ Preview training load score

Validated inline with Zod:
```
durationMinutes   integer   REQUIRED тАФ 1тАУ600
sessionRpe        number    REQUIRED тАФ 1тАУ10
bodyRegion        string    REQUIRED тАФ "upper" | "lower" | "full"
```
Returns the result of `calculateTrainingLoad()` without persisting anything:
```typescript
{
  sessionType: "lifting",
  bodyRegion: string,
  durationMinutes: number,
  sessionRpe: number,
  bodyRegionMultiplier: number,  // upper=1.0, lower=1.25, full=1.1
  trainingLoadScore: number      // = durationMinutes ├Ч sessionRpe ├Ч multiplier
}
```

---

## 18. Onboarding Flow тАФ Full Reference

> **Do not re-implement the onboarding POST endpoint or the server-side calculation logic.** The endpoint `POST /api/user/me/onboard` already exists in `server/routes.ts`. It validates the body with `onboardingSchema`, calls `calculateTargets()` server-side, seeds the initial weight log, and persists everything in one `storage.updateUser()` call.

---

### 18.1 Client wizard (`client/src/pages/onboarding.tsx`)

Multi-step wizard, ~22 visible steps (internal step count may be higher due to conditional steps).

| Step | Content |
|---|---|
| 0 | Splash тАФ full-screen background image, orange CTA button absolutely positioned at `bottom: 4%` (`data-testid="button-splash-cta"`) |
| 1тАУ3 | Basic profile: gender, age, height |
| 4 | Current weight |
| 5 | Activity level (sedentary / lightly active / moderately active / very active / extremely active) |
| 6 | Goal selection (fat loss / maintenance / weight gain) |
| 7 | Experience level |
| 8тАУ14 | Survey questions (cut experience, cut outcome, calorie knowledge, underfueling, load tracking, micro knowledge, energy score, performance) |
| 15 | Main problems multi-select (stored as `text[]`) |
| 16 | Commitment level |
| 17 | Star rating |
| 18 | Target preview (calculated from inputs so far тАФ display only, not yet persisted) |
| 19 | Body fat % (optional) |
| 20 | Fight camp setup (optional тАФ date, target weight, weigh-in timing) |
| 21 | Projected weight cut chart (`calculateWeightCutPlan()` with entered data) |
| 22+ | Done / confirmation тАФ `POST /api/user/me/onboard` is made here |

**`prfmr_onboarding_completing`** is set in `localStorage` when the user reaches the final steps so that `OnboardingGuard` doesn't redirect them to `/dashboard` before the POST completes. Cleared after successful POST.

**`?recalculate`** query param: if present on `/onboarding`, `OnboardingGuard` allows an already-onboarded user to proceed through the wizard again (to update targets). The same `POST /api/user/me/onboard` endpoint handles both first-time and recalculation submissions.

---

### 18.2 `POST /api/user/me/onboard` тАФ server endpoint

**Auth:** requires session. **File:** `server/routes.ts`.

**Request body schema** тАФ `onboardingSchema` from `shared/schema.ts` (a `.pick()` subset of `insertUserSchema`):

| Field | Type | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `gender` | `"male" \| "female"` | Required for BMR |
| `age` | `number` | Sanitised to 25 if null/NaN |
| `height` | `number` | cm; sanitised to 170 if null/NaN |
| `currentWeight` | `number` | kg; sanitised to 70 if null/NaN |
| `activityLevel` | string | One of the TDEE multiplier keys |
| `goal` | string | `"fat_loss" \| "maintenance" \| "weight_gain"`; sanitised to `"fat_loss"` if null |
| `experienceLevel` | string | Optional |
| `mainSport` | string | Optional, max 80 chars |
| `surveyCutExperience` | string | Optional |
| `surveyCutOutcome` | string | Optional |
| `surveyCalorieKnowledge` | string | Optional |
| `surveyUnderfueling` | string | Optional |
| `surveyTrainingLoadTracking` | string | Optional |
| `surveyMicroKnowledge` | string | Optional |
| `surveyEnergyScore` | string | Optional |
| `surveyPerformance` | string | Optional |
| `surveyMainProblems` | `string[]` | Optional text array |
| `surveyCommitment` | string | Optional |
| `surveyStarRating` | string/number | Optional |

**Server-side processing:**
1. Parses body with `onboardingSchema` (Zod)
2. Sanitises null/NaN fields (age тЖТ 25, height тЖТ 170, weight тЖТ 70, goal тЖТ `"fat_loss"`)
3. Calls `calculateTargets({ gender, weight, height, age, activityLevel, goal })` тАФ this is the server-side Mifflin-St Jeor + TDEE + goal-adjustment engine (see ┬з5). The client **does not** do this calculation independently for persistence.
4. Sanitises resulting targets (NaN тЖТ sensible defaults)
5. Calls `storage.updateUser(username, { ...data, ...targets })` to persist everything in the `users` table
6. Seeds today's weight log via `storage.upsertWeight({ userId, date: today, weight: currentWeight })` (non-fatal if fails)
7. Returns the full updated `User` object
8. If `username === "onboardtester"`: schedules a 90-second auto-reset of all profile fields (see ┬з15.9)

**Response:** `200 OK` тАФ full `User` object from the `users` table, including all computed targets.

**On success (client side):** `useUser()` cache is invalidated тЖТ `isOnboardingComplete()` returns `true` тЖТ `OnboardingGuard` redirects to `/dashboard`.

---

### 18.3 Survey fields persisted to `users` table

These are saved alongside the core profile fields in the same `POST /api/user/me/onboard` call:

```
surveyCutExperience       text
surveyCutOutcome          text
surveyCalorieKnowledge    text
surveyUnderfueling        text
surveyTrainingLoadTracking text
surveyMicroKnowledge      text
surveyEnergyScore         text
surveyPerformance         text
surveyMainProblems        text[]
surveyCommitment          text
surveyStarRating          text/numeric
```

- Background image: `attached_assets/BD246D36-3AE7-426E-88E2-322E8390F5AB_1777392079503.jpeg` тАФ fills `100vw ├Ч 100dvh`, `object-cover`
- The image has a button graphic baked into the design
- An orange `<Button>` is **absolutely positioned** at `bottom: 4%` over the baked-in button area, `data-testid="button-splash-cta"`
- No other UI elements on step 0

- Wrapper card: `border-0 shadow-none bg-transparent` (no visible card border or shadow)
- Progress bar track: `bg-white/5`
- Nav divider: `border-white/5`
- `OptionBtn` (choice options): `ring-1 ring-primary/50` (selected), `bg-secondary/60` (unselected) тАФ no `border-2`
- Logo at top of non-splash steps: `no_back_logo_1777367768475.png` at `height: 34px`

### 18.6 Sign-up flow (end-to-end)

This is the complete user journey from landing to dashboard:

```
/start (PublicOnlyRoute)
  тЖУ  User selects source (stored in localStorage as "prfmr_source")
  тЖУ  User enters email тЖТ POST /api/invites/request
  тЖУ  Email arrives with 10-char invite code
  тЖУ  User enters code тЖТ GET /api/invites/validate?token= (checked client-side)
  тЖУ  User clicks "Sign up with code"
/signup (PublicOnlyRoute)
  тЖУ  User enters username + password
  тЖУ  POST /api/auth/register { email, username, password, inviteToken, source }
  тЖУ  Server: validates invite, checks beta cap, creates usersAuth + users rows,
           sends verification email + welcome email, logs user in via req.login()
  тЖУ  Client: on 201 тЖТ navigate to /onboarding
/onboarding (OnboardingGuard)
  тЖУ  User completes 22-step wizard
  тЖУ  POST /api/user/me/onboard { all profile + survey fields }
  тЖУ  Server: calculates targets, seeds weight log, returns updated User
  тЖУ  Client: invalidates useUser() cache тЖТ isOnboardingComplete() = true тЖТ redirect
/dashboard (ProtectedRoute)
```

**Google OAuth sign-up variant:**
```
/start
  тЖУ  User selects source (required before Google button is active)
  тЖУ  User clicks "Sign up with Google"
  тЖУ  window.location.href = "/auth/google?src=<source>"
GET /auth/google  (server stores src in session.pendingSource, redirects to Google)
GET /auth/google/callback
  тЖУ  Google strategy: creates or links usersAuth + users rows
  тЖУ  Session pendingSource applied to user.source
  тЖУ  Redirect to /dashboard
/dashboard тЖТ ProtectedRoute sees no onboarding тЖТ redirects to /onboarding
/onboarding
  тЖУ  Same wizard тЖТ POST /api/user/me/onboard
/dashboard
```

---

### 18.7 Sign-in flow (end-to-end)

```
/ or /login (PublicOnlyRoute)
  тЖУ  User enters email/username + password
  тЖУ  POST /api/auth/login { identifier, password }
  тЖУ  Server: Passport local strategy; returns { user: { id, email, username, emailVerified } }
  тЖУ  Client: on success тЖТ navigate based on isOnboardingComplete():
             true  тЖТ /dashboard
             false тЖТ /onboarding
```

**Google sign-in from /login:**
```
  тЖУ  User clicks "Sign in with Google"
  тЖУ  window.location.href = "/auth/google"  (no src param from login page)
GET /auth/google тЖТ GET /auth/google/callback
  тЖУ  Existing account matched or linked
  тЖУ  Redirect to /dashboard
  тЖУ  ProtectedRoute checks onboarding, redirects if needed
```

**Error state:** If Google callback fails тЖТ redirect to `/?error=google_auth_failed`. The `/login` page reads `?error=google_auth_failed` from the URL and shows a destructive banner (`data-testid="text-google-error"`).
